# math-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Remarks on pairwise comparisons, transition amplitudes, and qubit states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04092)
*Jean-Pierre Magnot*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从成对比较（pairwise comparison）的视角审视有限族量子比特态（qubit states），区分了复数振幅、跃迁概率和相位值成对比较三个层次的数据，并展示了非正交情形下U(1)值互反成对比较结构中的三角缺陷与归一化Bargmann不变量及几何相位（geometric phase）之间的自然联系，从而为量子运动学中的不一致性量（inconsistency-type quantities）提供了简洁诠释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立成对比较语言与初等量子几何（elementary quantum geometry）之间的共通框架，从概念层面揭示两者之间的内在联系。

Method: 从纯态间的跃迁振幅（transition amplitudes）出发，区分复数振幅、跃迁概率和相位值成对比较三个层次；分析非正交情形下U(1)值互反成对比较结构的三角缺陷，将其与归一化Bargmann不变量建立关联；并讨论来自秩至多为2的Gram矩阵（Gram matrices）的可实现性约束，以及从酉相位数据到更一般跃迁数据的过渡。

Result: 相位数据在非正交情形下定义了一种U(1)值互反成对比较结构，其三角缺陷自然对应于归一化Bargmann不变量，从而与几何相位相关联。这一关联为量子运动学中的不一致性量提供了简洁的物理解释。

Conclusion: 本文主要具有概念性意义，通过成对比较与初等量子几何之间的共通语言，为理解量子态族的结构提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We discuss a pairwise-comparison viewpoint on finite families of qubit states. Starting from transition amplitudes between pure states, we distinguish three associated levels of comparison data: complex amplitudes, transition probabilities, and phase-valued pairwise comparisons. In the non-orthogonal case, the phase data define a \(U(1)\)-valued reciprocal pairwise comparison structure. We show that the corresponding triangular defects are naturally related to normalized Bargmann invariants and therefore to geometric phases. This gives a simple interpretation of inconsistency-type quantities in terms of quantum kinematics. We also comment on realizability constraints coming from Gram matrices of rank at most two, and on the passage from unitary phase data to more general transition data. The aim of the paper is mainly conceptual: to isolate a common language between pairwise comparisons and elementary quantum geometry.

</details>


### [2] [Quantum Dynamics: A Dilation-Based Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04096)
*Caleb A. Mickelson*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本论文以有限维开放量子系统为背景，系统介绍了基于膨胀（dilation）视角的动力学建模方法，将约化动力学（reduced dynamics）表示为系统与环境联合的幺正演化（unitary evolution），并详细讨论了斯坦斯普林膨胀（Stinespring dilation）在解析与Lipschitz连续动力学曲线（dynamical curves）下的精确与近似结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开放量子系统（open quantum systems）研究中，传统方法通过约化动力学描述系统演化，将环境作为间接因素处理。本文旨在提出并推广一种替代性的膨胀（dilation）视角，为有限维量子动力学提供更统一的数学框架。

Method: 首先回顾约化动力学视角与量子信道（quantum channels）语言，将有限维量子动力学形式化为信道值动力学曲线（channel-valued dynamical curves）；随后利用该框架讨论曲线的斯坦斯普林膨胀（Stinespring dilation），并分别给出解析曲线与Lipschitz连续曲线下的精确膨胀结果与近似膨胀结果，同时分析t=0处可能出现的奇异行为。

Result: 对于解析动力学曲线（analytic dynamical curves），获得了精确的有限维斯坦斯普林膨胀结果；对于Lipschitz连续动力学曲线（Lipschitz-continuous dynamical curves），证明了它们允许近似有限维斯坦斯普林膨胀。

Conclusion: 该论文从数学角度提供了基于膨胀（dilation）的量子动力学建模导论，并论证了视角转换可以为开放量子系统理论中的问题提出新的表述方式。

Abstract: In the study of open quantum systems, one commonly describes the evolution of a system of interest through reduced dynamics, obtained by treating the environment indirectly rather than as a part of the full model. This thesis presents an expository account of an alternative, dilation-based viewpoint in the finite-dimensional setting, where a family of reduced dynamics is represented through unitary evolution on a larger system consisting of the original system together with an ancillary environment. After reviewing the reduced-dynamics perspective and the language of quantum channels, we formulate finite-dimensional quantum dynamics as channel-valued dynamical curves and use this framework to discuss Stinespring dilations of such curves. We then present exact dilation results for analytic dynamical curves, explain the singular behavior that can arise at t=0, and describe approximation results showing that Lipschitz-continuous dynamical curves admit approximate finite-dimensional Stinespring dilations. The thesis therefore provides a mathematically focused introduction to dilation-based modeling of quantum dynamics and argues that a change of perspective can lead to new ways of formulating problems in the theory of open quantum systems.

</details>


### [3] [Anchored random clusters and SLE excursions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04395)
*Federico Camia,Valentino F. Foit,Rongvoram Nivesvivat*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提供了一篇教学性综述，利用共形场论（CFT）技术计算上半平面中 Schramm-Loewner Evolution（SLE）的可观测物理量，通过将可观测物理量表达为涉及退化边界算符（degenerate boundary operators）的体-边关联函数（bulk-boundary correlation functions），从而满足特定微分方程。文章不仅复现了SLE的左通概率、格林函数和锚定临界逾渗团簇的广义密度等经典结果，还推导了临界Fortuin-Kasteleyn（FK）团簇中关节点密度（densities of pivotal points）的新公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提供一套系统且具教学性的CFT方法框架，用于计算上半平面中的SLE可观测物理量，同时推导一些新的解析结果。

Method: 采用共形场论（CFT）技术，将所需的SLE可观测物理量构造为包含退化边界算符的体-边关联函数，利用此类关联函数满足的微分方程进行求解。

Result: 复现了Schramm的SLE左通概率、SLE格林函数以及Kleban、Simmons和Ziff首次获得的“锚定”临界逾渗团簇广义密度；得到了临界FK（Fortuin-Kasteleyn）团簇关节点密度的新解析公式。

Conclusion: CFT方法可有效地系统化推导上半平面中的SLE可观测物理量，并能推广至此前未知的解析结果。

Abstract: We provide a pedagogical review of CFT techniques to compute certain Schramm-Loewner Evolution (SLE) observables in the upper half-plane. The approach relies on the ability to express the observables as bulk-boundary correlation functions that involve degenerate boundary operators and, therefore, obey certain differential equations. In particular, we recover Schramm's left-passage probability for SLE, the SLE Green's functions, and the generalized densities of ``anchored'' critical percolation clusters first obtained by Kleban, Simmons, and Ziff. We also obtain new formulas corresponding to the densities of pivotal points between critical Fortuin-Kasteleyn (FK) clusters.

</details>


### [4] [Time-Dependent Dynamical Dimensional Transmutation in the $SU(2)$ Gross-Neveu Model with Time-Dependent Interaction Strength](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05111)
*Parameshwar R. Pasnoori*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在特定耦合强度时间演化条件下，含时SU(2) Gross-Neveu模型的动力学演化可等价于静态模型的重整化群（renormalization group, RG）流，时间t对应于截断对数lnΛ。通过广义Bethe ansatz框架，揭示了系统在绝热区的动力学维度嬗变（dynamical dimensional transmutation）以及在大时间尺度下的渐近自由（asymptotic freedom）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索含时相互作用的量子场论（quantum field theory）是否仍保持可积性（integrability），并试图建立含时模型的动力学演化与静态模型RG流之间的对应关系，从而深化对非平衡量子场论中动力学标度行为的理解。

Method: 采用广义Bethe ansatz（generalized Bethe ansatz）框架分析含时$SU(2)$ Gross-Neveu模型，约束耦合强度$g(t)$的时间轨迹须精确匹配静态模型RG流方程的轨迹，并将时间t与截断对数lnΛ等同起来。

Result: 在绝热区（$t\sim t_0$, $α_0=1$），系统产生含时质量间隙（time-dependent mass gap）$m(Δt)=m_0 e^{-πα_0Δt}$，呈现动力学维度嬗变；在大时间尺度（$t\gg t_0$）或快速驱动条件下，系统趋于渐近自由，并趋近$SU(2)_1$ WZNW模型——即静态模型的紫外不动点（UV fixed point）。

Conclusion: 含时模型中的时间进程等价于静态模型中的RG流，从而建立了非平衡量子场论动力学与平衡态重正化群行为之间的深层联系。

Abstract: In this work we consider the time-dependent $SU(2)$ Gross-Neveu model, which is a quantum field theory of fermions which interact with each other through spin exchange interaction with time-dependent coupling strength $g(t)$. Using the recently formulated generalized Bethe ansatz framework, we show that the system is integrable provided the time-dependent coupling strength is such that its trajectories in time are exactly same as that of the renormalization group (RG) flow equations corresponding to the static model, where time `$t$' of the time-dependent model is identified with the logarithm of the cutoff `$\ln Λ$' of the static model. In the scaling regime $Λ\rightarrow\infty$, the above relation between time and the logarithm of the cutoff provides a characteristic time scale $t_0$. We analyze the exact time-dependent wavefunction in the case of coupling strength decreasing with time and show that in the adiabatic regime, which corresponds to $t\sim t_0$ for drive rate $α_0=1$, the system exhibits a time-dependent dynamical dimensional transmutation where a time dependent mass gap is generated, which at time $t=t_0+Δt$ is given by $m(Δt)=m_0 e^{-πα_0Δt}$, where $m_0=Λe^{-πα_0 t_0}$. Comparing this with the mass gap of the static model, we identify the adiabatic regime of the time-dependent model with the scaling regime of the static model. In the case of very large time scales $t\gg t_0$ for drive rate $α_0$ or for very fast drive rates $α$ such that $αt \gg α_0t_0$, for any $t<L$, we argue that the system is asymptotically free and approaches the $SU(2)_1$ Wess-Zumino-Novikov-Witten (WZNW) model, which corresponds to the UV fixed point of the $SU(2)$ Gross-Neveu model. Hence we establish that progression of time in the time-dependent model is equivalent to RG flow in the corresponding static model.

</details>

### [5] [Chiral Magnetic Effect and Negative Magnetoresistance across the phase diagram of finite-density SU(2) gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04743)
*P. V. Buividovich,L. von Smekal,D. Smith*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文利用格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）模拟，在有限温度、有限化学势和弱外磁场下，研究了$SU(2)$规范理论中手征磁效应（CME）的信号。研究发现CME响应在夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）区间接近自由无质量费米子的普适值，而对负磁电阻（NMR）的观测结果偏离基于最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）的预测，且二者在相图中的行为存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征磁效应（Chiral Magnetic Effect, CME）是夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）和非中心重离子碰撞中的重要输运现象。此前对CME与负磁电阻（Negative Magnetoresistance, NMR）之间关系的理解仍不充分，特别是在有限温度和密度条件下的微观机制尚待澄清。

Method: 采用$SU(2)$规范理论结合$N_f=2$味动态费米子（dynamical fermions）进行格点模拟，在有限温度$T$、夸克化学势$\mu$和弱外磁场$eB$下，分别计算轴密度-矢量流关联函数（axial density-vector current correlator）以及双矢量流关联函数（two vector current correlator），以分别直接和间接探测CME信号。

Result: CME响应在夸克-胶子等离子体区间随温度和密度的变化较弱，接近自由无质量费米子的普适值；在强子相中，低温和高密度下CME受到轻微抑制。NMR在相图中表现出与CME定性不同的行为，在高温或高密度下受到强烈抑制，且其大小显著低于基于自由费米子最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）的预测。未发现CME强度在$(μ,T)$相图中的交叉（crossover）或二级相变（second-order phase transition）线附近出现统计上显著的增强。

Conclusion: 对于$eB \lesssim m_\pi^2$的弱磁场，CME与NMR之间的关系可能并非如预期的那样直接。研究结果不支持在相变边界附近CME强度显著增强的假设。

Abstract: We study the signatures of the Chiral Magnetic Effect (CME) in $SU(2)$ gauge theory with $N_f = 2$ flavours of dynamical fermions at finite temperature $T$, quark chemical potential $μ$ and a weak external magnetic field $e B$. We consider both the correlator of the axial density and the vector current, which gives direct access to the out-of-equilibrium CME, and the correlator of two vector currents, which probes the CME indirectly via the enhancement of the longitudinal electric conductivity (Negative Magnetoresistance, NMR). We find that the CME response extracted from the vector-axial correlator exhibits a rather weak dependence on temperature and density in the quark-gluon plasma regime, and is very close to the universal value for free massless quarks. The CME is mildly suppressed at low temperatures and large densities in the hadronic phase. In contrast, the NMR behaves in a qualitatively different way across the phase diagram, and is strongly suppressed at either large densities or temperatures. The magnitude of the NMR response appears to be considerably smaller than the prediction based on the lowest Landau level calculation for free quarks. Our findings suggest that for relatively small magnetic field strengths $e B \lesssim m_π^2$ the relation between the CME and NMR might not be as direct as expected. We also do not find statistically significant indications for an enhancement of the CME strength in the vicinity of the crossover or second-order phase transition lines in the $(μ, T)$ phase diagram.

</details>

### [6] [Gamma Factory: A New Experimental Paradigm for CERN's HL-LHC--FCC-ee Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04240)
*Mieczyslaw Witold Krasny*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: Gamma Factory（GF）提案旨在利用CERN加速器设施，通过部分剥离离子（partially stripped ions）的激光激发，产生高强度、高准直、极化的次级和三级粒子束，开启粒子物理、核物理、原子物理等跨学科研究新范式，并为LHC运行提供潜在的新型能源方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CERN加速器复合体在粒子、核物理、原子物理、基础物理与应用物理交叉领域存在尚未被充分开发的潜力。GF旨在利用LHC中高相对论性部分剥离离子束（partially stripped ions）的内部自由度，通过激光共振激发生成高强度光子束及其衍生的多种三级粒子束，从而拓展新的研究计划。

Method: 在LHC中产生、加速、冷却并存储高相对论性部分剥离离子束，使其充当有效的原子阱（atomic trap）；利用激光光子共振激发离子内部自由度；激光脉冲储存于法布里-珀罗腔（Fabry–Perot cavities）中，与循环离子束相互作用，产生高能、高准直、极化的次级光子束；进一步利用这些光子束生成极化的电子、正电子、μ子、中子、放射性离子及标记中微子等三级粒子束。

Result: 预期产生的光子束强度比现有伽马射线源高出数个数量级；三级粒子束涵盖极化电子、正电子、μ子、中子、放射性离子以及味或CP标记的中微子（flavour- or CP-tagged neutrinos）；在特定构型下，同一光子驱动过程还可用于产生LHC运行所需的插头功率（plug-power）。

Conclusion: 冷相对论性原子束、高强度光子束与三级粒子束共同构成一个多功能实验平台，可在CERN开辟广泛的新科学机遇。基于现有加速器基础设施与最先进激光技术，GF提供了一条经济高效且可及时推进的研究路径，能够在HL-LHC时代与未来FCC时代之间维持实验创新。

Abstract: The Gamma Factory (GF) proposal \cite{Krasny:2015ffb} is motivated by the recognition of a largely untapped potential of the CERN accelerator complex to enable a new research programme at the intersection of particle, nuclear, atomic, fundamental, and applied physics. The central concept is to produce, accelerate, cool, and store atomic beams of highly relativistic partially stripped ions in the LHC, which would serve as an effective atomic trap. The internal degrees of freedom of these ions are then resonantly excited using laser photons. In the GF scheme, laser-cooled atomic beams serve both as high-precision probes and as low-emittance beam sources for high-luminosity LHC operation in the ion-ion collision mode. Interactions between laser pulses stored in Fabry--Perot cavities and circulating ion beams give rise to high-energy, highly collimated, and polarised secondary photon beams. Their expected intensities exceed those of existing gamma-ray sources by several orders of magnitude. These photon beams can further be used to generate unprecedented-intensity, tertiary beams of polarised electrons, positrons, muons, neutrons, radioactive ions, and flavour- or CP-tagged neutrinos. Furthermore, under a specific configuration, the same photon-driven processes may be exploited in an energy-production scheme generating the requisite plug-power for LHC operation. Together, cold relativistic atomic beams, high-intensity photon beams, and tertiary beams constitute a versatile experimental platform capable of opening a wide range of new scientific opportunities at CERN. By exploiting existing accelerator infrastructure and available state-of-the-art laser technologies, the GF offers a path to a cost-effective and timely programme capable of sustaining experimental innovation and bridging the gap between the HL-LHC era and the future FCC era.

</details>


<div id='math.SP'></div>

# math.SP [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Riesz property in the case of multiple eigenvalues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04659)
*Boris Mityagin,Petr Siegl*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究非对称扰动下自伴算子（self-adjoint operator）的谱投影（spectral projection）的谱性质与Riesz性质（Riesz property），特别针对具有任意重数（包括无穷重数）特征值的情形。证明了在特定条件下，多维谐振子、Landau哈密顿量（Landau Hamiltonian）以及球面上的Laplace-Beltrami算子（Laplace-Beltrami operator）在复值$L^r$势（complex-valued $L^r$-potential）扰动下，当$d/2 < r < \infty$时满足Riesz性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自伴算子受非对称扰动后的谱投影行为在数学物理中具有重要地位，但现有理论对特征值具有任意重数（含无穷重数）的情形覆盖不足。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统建立此类情形下谱投影的Riesz性质。

Method: 采用谱分析（spectral analysis）与算子扰动理论（perturbation theory of operators）的方法，研究非对称扰动下自伴算子谱投影的谱结构及Riesz性质。具体分析对象包括多维谐振子、Landau哈密顿量和球面上的Laplace-Beltrami算子。

Result: 建立了非对称扰动下自伴算子谱投影的Riesz性质，特别证明了对于多维谐振子、Landau哈密顿量和球面上的Laplace-Beltrami算子，在复值$L^r$势扰动下，当参数满足$d/2 < r < \infty$时，其谱投影具有Riesz性质。

Conclusion: 本文拓展了非自伴扰动谱理论的应用范围，证明了在较宽泛条件下（特征值可具任意重数、势函数为复值$L^r$类），关键谱投影性质（Riesz性质）依然成立。

Abstract: We analyze spectra and the Riesz property of spectral projections of non-symmetric perturbations of self-adjoint operators with eigenvalues having arbitrary multiplicities, including infinite ones. In particular, we establish the Riesz property for perturbations of the multi-dimensional harmonic oscillator, Landau Hamiltonian and Laplace-Beltrami operator on a sphere by complex-valued $L^r$-potentials if $d/2 < r < \infty$.

</details>


<div id='hep-th'></div>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Spindle solutions with hyperscalars in $D=4$ gauged supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04140)
*Igal Arav,Jerome P. Gauntlett,Jaeha Park,Matthew M. Roberts,Christopher Rosen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在 D=4 STU U(1)^4 规范超引力（gauged supergravity）中构造了超对称 AdS₂ × Σ 解的新类别，其中 Σ 是一个纺锤形（spindle），可提升为 D=11 超引力的光滑超对称解，并讨论了非互质整数、轨道球面（orbifold）以及超标量（hyperscalar）在极点处消失的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构造超对称加速黑洞（accelerating black holes）的近地平线极限中的新 AdS₂ × 纺锤形解，并探索相关全息重整化群流（holographic RG flow）的终点。

Method: 采用 D=4 STU U(1)^4 规范超引力理论，并将其与带荷超标量（charged hyperscalar）耦合；构造 AdS₂ × Σ 解，其中 Σ 为纺锤形，允许非互质整数 (n_N, n_S) 以及圆球面 S² 的轨道形变（orbifold），并允许超标量在极点处为零。

Result: 构造了允许非互质整数参数的 AdS₂ × 纺锤形解，包含轨道球面情形；超标量可于极点消失；非零超标量解可作为全息 RG 流的终点，该流由 STU 模型 AdS₂ 解的相关超标量形变（hyperscalar deformation）所触发。

Conclusion: 新解覆盖了更广泛的参数空间（包括非互质纺锤形和轨道球面），并通过全息 RG 流与 STU 模型的 AdS₂ 解相联系，在 D=11 超引力中实现光滑提升，丰富了超对称加速黑洞的全息对应框架。

Abstract: We construct new classes of supersymmetric $AdS_2\times Σ$ solutions, where $Σ=Σ(n_N,n_S)$ is a spindle. Such solutions can arise as the near horizon limit of supersymmetric, accelerating black holes. The solutions are constructed using $D=4$ STU $U(1)^4$ gauged supergravity theory coupled to a charged hyperscalar, and can be uplifted to obtain smooth, supersymmetric $AdS_2\times Y_9$ solutions of $D=11$ supergravity. We allow $(n_N,n_S)$ to be non-coprime integers, including orbifolds of the round $S^2$. We also allow the hyperscalar to vanish at the poles. The $AdS_2$ solutions with non-vanishing hyperscalar can naturally arise as the endpoint of holographic RG flows, triggered by relevant hyperscalar deformations of the $AdS_2$ solutions of the STU model.

</details>


### [9] [Heterotic String Theory Suggests a QCD Axion Near 0.5 neV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04142)
*Joshua N. Benabou,Giulio Alvise Dainelli,Mario Reig,Benjamin R. Safdi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明在杂化弦理论（heterotic string theory）及其对偶理论（包括I型弦理论）中，QCD轴子质量存在下限$m_a \gtrsim 0.5$ neV，该下限源于模型无关轴子（model-independent axion）的衰变常数由大统一理论（GUT）规范耦合固定。通过对Kreuzer-Skarke系综中环簇Calabi-Yau超曲面及完全交Calabi-Yau流形上的杂化紧化系综进行大规模计算，发现除极少数流形外，QCD轴子质量均精确处于$[0.5, 0.8]$ neV窗口内，该窗口应为DMRadio-GUT等集总元件探测器的高优先级目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦论景观（string landscape）中，QCD轴子的质量预期存在理论下限，但此前缺乏来自杂化弦理论及其对偶框架的系统性定量约束。该研究旨在通过大规模紧化系综（compactification ensemble）计算，明确QCD轴子的质量下限及其与GUT规范耦合的关系，为实验探测提供精确目标窗口。

Method: 利用Kreuzer-Skarke (KS) 系综中环簇Calabi-Yau超曲面以及完全交Calabi-Yau流形上的杂化弦紧化，对包含最多11个轴子（作者样本中与统一性一致的最大数目）的Kähler模空间（Kähler moduli space）进行广泛搜索，显式计算QCD轴子质量。

Result: 除极少数流形外，所有杂化紧化中QCD轴子的质量均精确等于模型无关轴子的质量值，处于$[0.5, 0.8]$ neV范围，具体数值取决于GUT规范耦合。杂态系综中的重轴子（heavy axion）群体在大爆炸核合成（big bang nucleosynthesis, BBN）之前普遍衰变，且能自然容纳轻子生成（leptogenesis），这与Type IIB轴子景观（axiverse）构造不同。

Conclusion: 杂化弦理论中QCD轴子质量存在严格的$0.5$ neV下限，该质量窗口应作为DMRadio-GUT等未来集总元件探测器的高优先级探测目标。杂化弦框架中的轴子现象学与Type IIB轴子景观存在显著差异，尤其在重轴子衰变与轻子生成可行性方面。

Abstract: We show that in heterotic string theory -- and dual corners of the landscape including Type I string theory -- the QCD axion mass is bounded from below by $m_a \gtrsim 0.5$ neV, a direct consequence of the model-independent axion whose decay constant is fixed by the grand unified theory (GUT) gauge coupling. We explicitly compute the mass of the QCD axion in an ensemble of heterotic compactifications on Calabi-Yau hypersurfaces of toric varieties sampled from the Kreuzer-Skarke (KS) ensemble, as well as on complete intersection Calabi-Yau manifolds. We then perform an extensive search over the Kähler moduli space of KS compactifications with up to $11$ axions -- the maximum we identify as consistent with unification in our sample. We establish that for all but a handful of manifolds the QCD axion mass is precisely the model-independent value, lying in $[0.5, 0.8]$ neV, depending on the GUT gauge coupling. This window should be a high-priority target for future lumped-element detectors such as DMRadio-GUT. We show that the heavy axion population in our heterotic ensemble generically decays before big bang nucleosynthesis and can naturally accommodate leptogenesis, unlike in Type IIB axiverse constructions.

</details>


### [10] [When AdS$_3$ Grows Hair: Boson Stars, Black Holes, and Double-Trace Deformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04145)
*Oscar J. C. Dias,David Sola Gil,Jorge E. Santos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过高精度谱方法构建了带有双迹边界条件的三维AdS引力中的玻色子星与有毛黑洞，完整给出了该理论在非线性层面的相图，并揭示了全局AdS$_3$不稳定后的非线性终结态以及有毛黑洞在微正则系综中的熵优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三维爱因斯坦引力与带有双迹边界条件（double-trace boundary conditions）的大质量复标量场耦合系统的非线性相结构，特别是BTZ黑洞在有毛解出现后的相变与基态选择问题。

Method: 采用高精度谱方法（high-precision spectral methods），数值构造了正则的AdS$_3$玻色子星（boson stars）以及轴对称和非轴对称的有毛黑洞（hairy black holes）。

Result: 对于每个方位角量子数$m$，有毛黑洞在对应的双迹不稳定性临界点从BTZ系列分岔而出；当双迹参数$\kappa < \kappa_{\rm AdS}$时，全局AdS$_3$变得不稳定，其非线性终结态是能量低于AdS$_3$的零频玻色子星；在微正则系综中，固定质量和角动量下有毛黑洞的熵始终大于BTZ；但在正则和巨正则系综中通常不占优；轴对称黑洞在奇异极端极限下满足广义最小能量定理。

Conclusion: 该结果完整给出了带有双迹形变的三维AdS引力的非线性相图，确认了低能基态为玻色子星，并阐明了有毛黑洞在不同系综中的热力学主导地位。

Abstract: We analyse three-dimensional Einstein gravity coupled to a massive complex scalar field with double-trace boundary conditions. Using high-precision spectral methods, we construct regular AdS$_3$ boson stars together with axisymmetric and non-axisymmetric hairy black holes. For each azimuthal number $m$, the hairy black holes bifurcate from the BTZ family at the corresponding double-trace instability onset. When the double-trace parameter satisfies $κ< κ_{\rm AdS}$, global AdS$_3$ becomes unstable and we identify its nonlinear endpoint as a zero-frequency boson star with energy below that of AdS$_3$, thereby providing the true ground state of the theory. In the microcanonical ensemble, hairy black holes always carry greater entropy than BTZ at fixed mass and angular momentum, and thus dominate whenever they exist. With notable exceptions, typically hairy black holes do not dominate the canonical nor the grand-canonical ensembles. We further show that, in the singular extremal limit, axisymmetric black holes saturate a generalised minimum-energy theorem under double-trace boundary conditions. These results yield the full nonlinear phase diagram of AdS$_3$ gravity with double-trace deformations.

</details>


### [11] [(Pseudo-)Dirac Gravitinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04146)
*Karim Benakli,Arno Goudeau*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文以Scherk-Schwarz超对称破缺为基准模型，论证了Dirac引力微子（Dirac gravitino）的低能有效理论需要超自旋-3/2投影的超空间描述，并分析了其与物质耦合、辐射质量及R对称性破缺的物理后果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准超引力（supergravity）中引力微子通常为Majorana粒子，而Scherk-Schwarz超对称破缺在S^1/Z_2上对费米子施加反周期边界条件后，会出现两个简并的Majorana自旋-3/2模式，自然形成Dirac引力微子。本文旨在澄清其低能有效理论的超空间实现、物质耦合及质量生成机制，并指出其与紫外完备（ultraviolet completion）的关联。

Method: 以最小超引力（minimal supergravity）中的Scherk-Schwarz超对称破缺为基准模型，采用超空间（superspace）方法分析Dirac自旋-3/2混合的局域实现；通过超流（supercurrent）耦合推导标量质量阈值（scalar threshold），并引入伴随通道物质流（companion-channel matter current）讨论Dirac费米子质量的生成。

Result: 在最小超引力中，Dirac自旋-3/2混合不存在局域的Dirac-gaugino型N=1超空间实现，必须投影到横超自旋-3/2（transverse superspin-3/2）扇区；标量阈值贡献为负，仅是可计算的标量质量矩阵贡献之一而非完整预言；Dirac费米子质量需要附加的伴随通道物质流，其归一化由紫外完备决定而非Dirac引力微子本身唯一确定。

Conclusion: Dirac引力微子低能理论伴随R对称性选择定则，其超空间描述受限于超自旋投影；标量质量与Dirac质量均需依赖紫外完备的信息；该方法可推广至单态费米子（singlet fermions）、模量场（modulini）及辐射Dirac中微子质量（radiative Dirac neutrino masses）等物理情景。

Abstract: We discuss low-energy effective theories with a Dirac gravitino. Our main benchmark is Scherk--Schwarz supersymmetry breaking with anti-periodic boundary conditions for fermions on S^1/Z_2. In this case two Majorana spin-3/2 modes are degenerate, so the low-energy theory is naturally organized around a Dirac gravitino and an associated R-symmetry selection rule. We show, in minimal supergravity, that this Dirac spin-3/2 mixing has no local Dirac-gaugino-type N=1 superspace realization: a superspace description requires projection onto the transverse superspin-3/2 sector. We then analyze some consequences for matter couplings and radiative masses. The ordinary gravitino supercurrent coupling gives the standard universal Scherk--Schwarz scalar threshold; in the minimal benchmark this contribution is negative, and should therefore be regarded as one calculable contribution to the scalar mass matrix, not as a complete scalar-spectrum prediction. Dirac fermion masses can be generated if an additional companion-channel matter current is present. The existence and normalization of this current are not fixed by the Dirac gravitino alone and depend on the ultraviolet completion. We finally discuss small R-breaking deformations, the resulting pseudo-Dirac regime, and comment on possible applications to singlet fermions, modulini, and radiative Dirac neutrino masses.

</details>


### [12] [Heterotic Flux Vacua with a Small Superpotential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04148)
*Evgeny I. Buchbinder,Andrei Constantin,Lucas T. Y. Leung,Andre Lukas,Burt Ovrut*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究带有NSNS三形式通量的杂化Calabi-Yau紧致化中的模稳定问题，发现通量超势在超对称极小点处的值|W₀|受到严格约束：超对称真空只能在模空间奇异点处实现|W₀|=0，在大复结构极限下不存在小|W₀|的真空；通过精确周期表达式在一参数和两参数模型中找到的|W₀|值仅勉强支持模稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 与IIB型弦论不同，杂化弦紧致化缺乏无标度结构（no-scale structure），非零通量超势通常对所有模（moduli）产生树级标量势，因此需要通量超势足够小以与非微扰效应竞争，从而控制模稳定化。本文旨在探究杂化Calabi-Yau紧致化中能否实现足够小的|W₀|。

Method: 在四维有效场论框架内，利用Calabi-Yau复结构模空间（complex structure moduli spaces）的特殊几何（special geometry），分析复结构F-项方程，推导出两个不可能性定理（no-go theorems）；随后使用精确周期表达式（exact period expressions）分析远离大复结构极限的具体模型。

Result: 推导出两条no-go定理：(1) 超对称真空仅在模空间奇异点处可实现|W₀|=0；(2) 在大复结构极限（large complex structure limit）下不存在小|W₀|的超对称真空。在远离该极限的一参数和两参数模型示例中，通过合适通量选择可获得量级为1的|W₀|，部分一参数模型的值略低于1。

Conclusion: 杂化弦通量超势的小值受到高度约束，所研究示例中获得的|W₀|值仅勉强与模稳定化（moduli stabilisation）兼容。

Abstract: We study heterotic Calabi--Yau compactifications with NSNS three-form flux in view of moduli stabilisation and investigate whether the value $|W_0|$ of the flux superpotential evaluated at supersymmetric minima can be small. Unlike in type IIB string theory, heterotic compactifications lack a no-scale structure, so that a non-vanishing flux superpotential generically induces a tree-level scalar potential for all moduli. Controlled moduli stabilisation therefore requires the flux superpotential to be sufficiently small in order to compete with non-perturbative effects. Working within a four-dimensional effective field theory and exploiting the special geometry of Calabi--Yau complex structure moduli spaces, we analyse the complex structure F-term equations and derive two no-go theorems: (1) supersymmetric vacua with vanishing $|W_0|$, which would lead to a vanishing tree-level scalar potential as in type IIB, occur only at singular loci in moduli space, and (2) no supersymmetric vacua with small $|W_0|$ exist in the large complex structure limit. Motivated by these results, we analyse explicit models away from the large complex structure regime using exact period expressions and identify one- and two-parameter examples in which suitable flux choices allow for values of $|W_0|$ of order unity, with some one-parameter models admitting values moderately below unity. Our findings show that small heterotic flux superpotentials are highly constrained, with the values of $|W_0|$ found in the examples studied being only marginally compatible with moduli stabilisation.

</details>


### [13] [Consistent Scattering Amplitudes, Yang-Mills, the Higgs Mechanism and the EFTs Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04152)
*Timothy Trott*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过幺正性（unitarity）、局域性（locality）和微扰S矩阵（perturbative S-matrix）的自洽性，导出了四维时空中有质量与无质量粒子散射振幅的约束条件，涵盖胶子三粒子振幅的完整结构、自旋s≤1有质量粒子的树图振幅能标依赖行为的分类，以及超对称理论中超级振幅（superamplitude）的统一表述，并系统绘制了有效场论（EFT）全景图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找超越标准模型的基本物理约束，从散射矩阵（S-matrix）的一致性出发，系统性地推导基本粒子相互作用必须满足的数学与对称性条件。

Method: 无质量粒子情形使用2→2振幅的复因子化（complex factorisation）导出新约束；有质量粒子情形则通过在高能极限下限制幺正性破坏（unitarity-violating）的最大增长率，并采用在壳方法（on-shell methods）系统计算自旋s≤1粒子的所有树图振幅，分析其螺旋度扇区（helicity sectors）的能量依赖结构。

Result: 导出了胶子三粒子振幅的完整结构，包括李代数（Lie algebra）的几何限制及宇称（parity）、时间反演（time-reversal）对称性等细节。发现质量矢量玻色子散射在宇称守恒部分为李代数结构常数（可能非半单或非紧致）、宇称破缺部分为“广义陈-陈-西蒙斯项”（generalised Chern-Simons terms）时，高能依赖被压制但未完全幺正化；完全幺正化要求标准杨-米尔斯李代数性质及希格斯机制（Higgs mechanism）。在BPS（Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield）情形下，振幅可统一为超对称理论中的超级振幅。

Conclusion: 该工作为从S矩阵自洽性出发约束基本物理提供了系统框架，揭示了不同约束组合与耦合层级对应更广阔的有效场论景观（landscape of EFTs）。

Abstract: I study constraints on fundamental physics emerging from consistency of a unitary, local and perturbative $S$-matrix in $4d$. For massless particles, some new constraints arising from consistent complex factorisation of $2\rightarrow 2$ amplitudes are derived, leading, in particular, to the complete structure of the gluon three-particle amplitudes, including the geometric restrictions on the Lie algebra, parity and time-reversal symmetry, among other details. For massive particles, a hierarchy of constraints may be derived instead by imposing a maximum rate of unitarity-violating growth in the high energy limit. All $2\rightarrow 2$ tree-level amplitudes of massive particles with spin $s\leq 1$ are calculated in generality using on-shell methods and presented with manifest high energy dependence. The anatomy of these amplitudes' helicity sectors is dissected in order to identify conditions under which their energy growth is limited or eliminated. Using these results, it is shown that the scattering of massive vector bosons has suppressed, but not fully unitarised, high energy dependence if the parity-conserving parts of their self-couplings are Lie algebra structure constants, possibly non-semisimple or non-compact, and the parity-violating parts are ``generalised Chern-Simons terms''. Full unitarisation then requires the standard Yang-Mills Lie algebra properties and, for a gapped spectrum, the Higgs mechanism. These amplitudes are assembled, embedded and unified into elegant superamplitudes in theories with extended supersymmetry when the particles are BPS. More generally, a broader landscape of EFTs is charted through various combinations of constraints and coupling hierarchies.

### [14] [The nonlocal magic of a holographic Schwinger pair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04210)
*Sebastian Grieninger*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用全息对偶（holography）方法，结合Casini–Huerta–Myers共形映射与探针膜框架（probe-brane framework），计算精细化Rényi熵（refined Rényi entropy）及其导数，以捕捉纠缠谱的平坦性偏离（antiflatness）。

Result: 当边界时空维数d>2时，纠缠谱是非平坦的，表明对产生过程中动态生成了非定域魔术。此外，全息对偶中的非定域魔术可以从探针作用的自由能中直接获得。

Conclusion: 在强非阿贝尔电场中的Schwinger对产生过程会动态生成非定域魔术，且该量子资源可通过全息对偶中的探针自由能进行描述，为理解高能物理中的量子复杂性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We analyze the emergence of nonlocal magic in Schwinger pair creation in strong non-Abelian (chromo)electric fields using holography. The produced quark--antiquark pair is entangled into a color singlet, yet accelerates into causally disconnected Rindler wedges. Using the Casini--Huerta--Myers conformal mapping and the probe-brane framework, we compute the refined Rényi entropy and its derivative, which captures the antiflatness of the entanglement spectrum for a spherical bipartition. We find that for boundary spacetime dimension $d>2$, the entanglement spectrum is non-flat, implying the dynamical generation of nonlocal magic in the pair creation process. Interestingly, the nonlocal magic in the holographic dual can be obtained from the free energy of the probe action.

### [15] [Particle Production and Krylov Complexity of Circular Strings Near Black Hole Horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04349)
*Ai-chen Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了坠落弦（infalling circular string）在接近黑洞视界（black hole horizon）时，由量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）引发的粒子产生（particle production）、Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）、Lanczos系数（Lanczos coefficients）与算符增长（operator growth），并发现了近热化区域的标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究坠入黑洞的弦在量子涨落下是否产生显著粒子以及算符复杂度的行为，并验证复杂度-体积对应关系（complexity volume correspondence）。

Method: 采用压缩态形式（squeezed state formalism）下的正则量子化（canonical quantization）方法，并利用双模态（two mode states）下粒子数与Krylov复杂度之间的等价关系进行推导。

Result: 显著的粒子产生仅出现在弦靠近黑洞视界的径向扇区（radial sector），角向模（angular modes）几乎未被激发；在近热化区域（near-horizon, effectively thermalized regime），粒子数对探针弦（probe string）初始位置呈多项式依赖；算符增长率对初始位置呈线性依赖。

Conclusion: 近热化区域的状态趋近于热场双态（thermofield double form），粒子数与Krylov复杂度在该区域呈现非平凡标度行为；算符增长率的线性标度行为支持了复杂度-体积对应关系。

Abstract: For an infalling circular string, we study particle production, Krylov complexity, Lanczos coefficients, and operator growth induced by quantum fluctuations. Using canonical quantization in the squeezed state formalism, we show that significant particle production arises only in the radial sector as the string approaches the black hole horizon, while angular modes remain weakly excited. Exploiting the equivalence between particle number and Krylov complexity for two mode states, we find that nontrivial complexity scaling emerges only in the near-horizon, effectively thermalized regime, where the state approaches a thermofield double form. In this limit, the particle number exhibits a polynomial dependence on the initial position of the probe string. We further identify a linear dependence of the operator growth rate on the initial position of the probe string, suggesting a universal scaling behavior of operator growth and providing support for the complexity volume correspondence.

</details>


### [16] [Chiral interactions of fermions and massive gauge fields in Kaluza-Klein models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.09126)
*Joao Baptista*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文挑战了卡鲁扎-克莱因理论中规范场必须与内部空间精确 Killing 矢量场对应的传统观点，研究了与非 Killing 场相关的四维规范场，发现其具有任意轻质量玻色子、可混合不同质量费米子以及左右手费米子不对称耦合等特性，为在卡鲁扎-克莱因框架内建模弱相互作用提供了几何来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卡鲁扎-克莱因（Kaluza-Klein）理论中，传统观点认为规范场源于内部空间（internal space）的精确 Killing 矢量场（exact Killing vector fields）。本文旨在质疑这一假设，探索与非 Killing 场（non-Killing fields）相关的四维规范场的性质，以规避传统“no-go”论证并为手征相互作用（chiral interactions）提供几何解释。

Method: 本文采用旋量几何（spin geometry）和黎曼浸没（Riemannian submersions）的数学语言，研究具有非平凡背景度规（background metrics）的高维 Dirac 算符（Dirac operator）。推导针对一般内部空间 $K$ 进行，并在 $K$ 为二维球面（two-sphere）和二维环面（two-torus）的简单情形下进行显式说明。

Result: 与非 Killing 场相关的四维规范场具有以下性质：产生任意轻质量的玻色子（massive yet arbitrarily light bosons）；可混合不同质量的费米子（mix fermions with different masses）；对左右手费米子具有不对称耦合（asymmetric couplings）。这些性质均难以由与内部等距（internal isometries）相关的规范场满足。

Conclusion: 与非 Killing 场相关联的质量规范场规避了传统 no-go 论证，为费米子手征相互作用提供了几何来源，可能有助于在卡鲁扎-克莱因框架内对弱相互作用（weak force）进行建模。

Abstract: In Kaluza-Klein theory, gauge fields on $M_4$ arise as components of a higher-dimensional metric defined on $M_4 \times K$. The traditional expectation is that all the gauge fields of the Standard Model are linked to exact Killing vector fields on the internal space. This paper questions that assumption and investigates the properties of 4D gauge fields linked to non-Killing fields on $K$. It is shown that they have massive yet arbitrarily light bosons; they can mix fermions with different masses; and they can have asymmetric couplings to left- and right-handed fermions. None of these properties is easily satisfied by gauge fields linked to internal isometries. So the massive gauge fields produced in this manner circumvent traditional no-go arguments and offer a geometric source of chiral interactions with fermions. This may help to model the weak force within the Kaluza-Klein framework. Technically, the paper uses the language of spin geometry and Riemannian submersions. It studies the higher-dimensional Dirac operator with non-trivial background metrics. The results are derived for a general $K$. They are illustrated explicitly in the simpler cases where $K$ is the two-sphere and the two-torus.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类新型宇宙学吸引子（cosmological attractor）家族，通过引入非最小引力耦合（non-minimal coupling）与非正则动能项（non-canonical kinetic terms），在爱因斯坦框架（Einstein frame）下转化为指数型与多项式型吸引子。其谱指数（spectral index）$n_s$ 覆盖 $1-2/N \leq n_s < 1-1/N$ 的广泛范围，张量标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）$r$ 可在 $\xi \to \infty$ 极限下趋于零，足以匹配 Planck、BICEP/Keck、ACT、SPT 及 DESI 等全部主流观测数据，并给出了超引力（supergravity）实现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过引入非最小引力耦合与非正则动能项构建新家族；在爱因斯坦框架下进行共形变换（conformal transformation），将原拉格朗日量映射为指数型与多项式型吸引子形式，并通过超引力框架实现模型的具体嵌入。

Result: 所得模型的谱指数范围为 $1-2/N \leq n_s < 1-1/N$，张量标量比 $r$ 可在参数 $\xi \to \infty$ 时降至零。该参数空间足以同时匹配 Planck、BICEP/Keck、ACT、SPT 与 DESI 的全部观测数据。

Conclusion: 该新型吸引子家族提供了与当前所有主要宇宙学观测一致的理论框架，且其超引力实现路径表明该模型具有从基础理论（超引力）导出的完整一致性。

Abstract: We introduce a new family of cosmological attractors with non-minimal coupling of gravity and non-canonical kinetic terms. In the Einstein frame, these models transform into a class of exponential and polynomial attractors with the spectral index $n_{s}$ spanning a broad range $1-2/N \leq n_{s} < 1-1/N$, and $r$ can decrease to zero in the limit $ξ\to \infty$. This is sufficient to match any combination of Planck, BICEP/Keck, ACT, SPT, and DESI data. We present a supergravity implementation of these models.

### [18] [Bound states and deconfinement from Romans supergravity with magnetic flux](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04586)
*Ali Fatemiabhari,Maurizio Piai*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用规范-引力对偶（gauge-gravity duality）字典，研究四维强耦合禁闭场论家族中的束缚态谱。通过六维超引力背景解中的非平凡阿贝尔磁通量，计算了对应场论束缚态的涨落谱，发现最轻的两个标量粒子中较重的为与标度不变性相关的赝南布-戈德斯通玻色子（dilaton），并在参数空间接近一级相变时出现大曲率区域及标量粒子的非平凡混合与质量压制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用六维罗曼半最大超引力理论（Romans half-maximal supergravity theory）中的非超对称正则背景解，在几何紧致化方向施加非平凡阿贝尔磁通量（Abelian magnetic flux），并计算背景场涨落谱以对应场论中的束缚态。

Result: 谱中最轻的两个标量粒子质量被压制且近乎简并；其中较重的粒子被识别为与标度不变性（scale invariance）相关的赝南布-戈德斯通玻色子（pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson），即胀子（dilaton），耦合到场论应力-能量张量的迹，而最轻标量则无此耦合。在接近一级相变的参数区间，空间末端出现大曲率区域，两标量发生非平凡混合，其质量相对其他束缚态呈参数性压制。

Conclusion: 磁通量强度触发零温退禁闭一级相变（first-order phase transition），并对几何可支持的磁通量幅度设置上限。在相变附近，两最轻标量粒子的非平凡混合与质量压制机制值得进一步关注。

Abstract: We apply the dictionary of gauge-gravity dualities to study the spectrum of bound states in a special one-parameter family of strongly coupled, confining field theories in four dimensions. The top-down, holographic gravity dual description of this class of theories has been identified recently. It consists of non-supersymmetric regular background solutions of Romans half-maximal supergravity theory in six dimensions, in the presence of a non-trivial Abelian magnetic flux along a compactified direction of the geometry. A zero-temperature, deconfinement, first-order phase transition appears at one end of this branch of solutions. It is triggered by the strength of the flux, setting an upper bound on the magnitude of the magnetic flux that can be supported by the geometry. We compute the spectrum of fluctuations of the background fields in the gravity description, that correspond to field-theory bound states. Two scalar particles are the lightest in the spectrum, their masses being suppressed and almost degenerate across the whole parameter space. Away from the transition, the heaviest between these two particles is identified as a dilaton, the pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson associated with scale invariance. It couples to the trace of the stress-energy tensor of the dual field theory, while the lightest scalar does not. In the range of parameter space closest to the extremum of the one-parameter family, near the first-order phase transition, a region with large curvature appears at the end of space of the geometry of the solutions. In this range, the two scalars mix non-trivially, and their masses are parametrically suppressed, in respect to the other bound states.

### [19] [Molien--Weyl Singlet Counting and BFSS$_2$--Factorization in Gaussian Matrix QM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04621)
*Badis Ydri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过结合大d高斯约化（large-d Gaussian reduction）与Molien-Weyl投影（Molien-Weyl projection），系统研究了质量变形BFSS矩阵量子力学（mass-deformed BFSS matrix quantum mechanics）的单态区（singlet sector）结构，揭示了低温玻色子单态谱由二次Gram算子（quadratic Gram operators）普遍控制，并给出了特殊因子化（exceptional factorization）的哈密顿推导，最后将Gram计数图像（Gram-counting picture）推广到超对称情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解BFSS型矩阵量子力学在大d极限下的单态区结构，揭示低温谱的普适性规律，并解释为何某些参数区域（如d=1, N=2）不存在退禁闭相变（deconfinement crossover）这一特殊现象。

Method: 采用大d高斯约化捕获体矩阵动力学（bulk matrix dynamics），得到规范化的谐振子（gauged harmonic oscillator）；再通过Molien-Weyl积分实施高斯定律（Gauss law），将物理希尔伯特空间重组为holonomy投影的单态激发（holonomy-projected singlet excitations）。对N=2情形使用显式留数计算（residue computations）和特征标方法（character methods），对N>2情形依赖特征标分析（character analysis）。

Result: 低温玻色子单态谱由二次Gram算子Tr(X_a X_b)普遍控制，其数目为d(d+1)/2；红外谱起始于一系列BFSS_2型Gram塔（Gram towers）。在(d,N)=(2,2)处发现了BFSS_3单态配分函数（singlet partition function）等于BFSS_2单态配分函数的立方这一精确的异常因子化关系，该关系源于SU(2)不变张量结构（SU(2) invariant tensor structure）的特殊性。

Conclusion: Gram计数图像可推广至超对称BFSS/BMN模型（supersymmetric BFSS/BMN models）；Molien-Weyl形式体系（Molien-Weyl formulation）可作为基准化（benchmark）蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）的工具，既适用于X_a空间也适用于holonomy空间。

Abstract: We study the singlet-sector structure of mass-deformed BFSS$_{d+1}$ matrix quantum mechanics by combining the large--\(d\) Gaussian reduction with the Molien--Weyl projection. The Gaussian reduction captures the bulk matrix dynamics through a gauged harmonic oscillator, while the Molien--Weyl integral imposes the Gauss law and reorganizes the physical Hilbert space into holonomy-projected singlet excitations.
  We show that the very-low-temperature bosonic singlet spectrum is universally controlled by the quadratic Gram operators \(\Tr(X_aX_b)\), whose number is \(d(d+1)/2\). For \(N=2\), this result is established by explicit residue computations and character methods; for \(N>2\), it is supported by the character analysis. Thus the infrared spectrum begins as a collection of BFSS$_2$--like Gram towers, although higher invariant structures generally modify the full partition function.
  We also give a Hamiltonian derivation of the exceptional exact factorization at \((d,N)=(2,2)\), where the BFSS$_3$ singlet partition function equals the cube of the BFSS$_2$ one for all temperatures. This rigidity is special to the \(SU(2)\) invariant tensor structure and explains why \(d=1\) and \(N=2\) are exceptional regimes without a deconfinement crossover. Finally, we extend the Gram-counting picture to supersymmetric BFSS/BMN models and indicate how the Molien--Weyl formulation can benchmark Monte Carlo simulations in both \(X_a\)-space and holonomy space.

### [20] [Expectation values after an integrable boundary quantum quench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04823)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了可积边界淬火（integrable boundary quench）问题，即系统从一个可积边界条件突然切换到另一个的过程。基于体算子和边界改变算子的形状因子（form factor），发展了一个描述实时（real-time）动力学的通用框架。先在Lee-Yang模型的共形点（conformal point）处分析问题，再扩展到其有质量扰动（massive perturbation）情形，计算了淬火前真空的时间演化以及淬火后局域算符的真空-真空矩阵元，并通过截断共形空间方法（truncated conformal space approach）数值验证了分析结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边界淬火（boundary quench）是一种重要的非平衡（non-equilibrium）量子动力学问题，但此前缺乏可解析处理的可积边界淬火框架。本文旨在通过发展基于形状因子（form factor）的通用方法，填补这一空白，从而为可积边界条件下的实时动力学提供解析与数值分析工具。

Method: 采用形状因子（form factor）形式论，对体算子和边界改变算子（boundary-changing operators）的矩阵元进行解析构造；在Lee-Yang模型的共形场论（conformal field theory）点及其有质量扰动下分别处理问题；利用截断共形空间方法（truncated conformal space approach）对边界改变情形进行数值模拟以验证解析结果。

Result: 在共形点处建立了边界淬火后实时动力学的解析描述；在质量扰动下计算了淬火前真空态的时间演化，得到了局域算符的真空-真空矩阵元；数值计算结果与解析预言一致，验证了方法的正确性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个适用于可积边界淬火（integrable boundary quench）问题的通用分析框架，能够有效处理从共形点到有质量扰动下的实时动力学，且解析结果获得了数值验证。该方法为研究更广泛的可积边界非平衡问题提供了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate an integrable boundary quench, in which one integrable boundary condition is suddenly switched to another. We develop a general framework for analyzing the resulting real-time dynamics based on form factors of bulk and boundary-changing operators. We first study the problem at the conformal point of the Lee-Yang model and then extend the analysis to its massive perturbation, where we examine the time evolution of the pre-quench vacuum and compute the vacuum-to-vacuum matrix elements of local operators inserted after the quench. The analytical results are validated by numerical calculations using the truncated conformal space approach adapted to boundary-changing situations.

### [21] [Kerr/CFT Traversable Wormhole with Fermionic Double-Trace Deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05011)
*M. Zhahir Djogama,Fitria Khairunnisa,Hadyan Luthfan Prihadi,Freddy Permana Zen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文在双面克尔背景（two-sided Kerr background）中，利用费米子场（fermion fields）的双迹形变（double-trace deformation）构建可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole），在Kerr/CFT框架下分析了虫洞的可穿越性、信息传输上限及回波时间延迟等性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前的可穿越虫洞构造仅使用玻色子场（boson fields）作为微扰，本文旨在引入费米子场实现双迹形变，从而规避玻色超辐射（superradiance）在离轴区域（off-axis region）引起的不稳定性，拓展可穿越虫洞的构造范围。

Method: 在Kerr/CFT框架下，考虑近极端近视界克尔几何（near-horizon, near-extremal Kerr geometry），该几何对偶于共形场论（conformal field theory）。通过费米子双迹形变耦合左右边界，修正两点函数（two-point function），其一阶修正贡献负能量以打开虫洞。

Result: 虫洞在早期施加微扰时最可穿越，开口大小依赖于模式频率、黑洞温度和费米子质量。晚期平均零能量（average null energy）呈现阻尼振荡直至归零。低温虫洞可穿越性降低，极端极限下完全闭合；近极端旋转可将信息传输上界提高至熵量级。对称有效势垒（symmetrical effective potential bumps）通过虫洞连接可产生可观测回波（echoes），且回波时间延迟不超过黑洞的混乱时间（scrambling time）。

Conclusion: 费米子双迹形变可成功构造克尔背景下的可穿越虫洞，避免了玻色超辐射导致的不稳定性，揭示了温度、旋转及微扰时序对虫洞可穿越性的影响，并建立了回波时间延迟与黑洞混乱时间之间的上界关系。

Abstract: The construction of a traversable wormhole with double-trace deformation has been achieved so far by using boson fields as the perturbation. In this work, we study double-trace deformation with fermion fields in the two-sided Kerr background to open a traversable wormhole. We construct the fermionic double-trace deformation within the Kerr/CFT framework. We consider the near-horizon, near-extremal Kerr geometry, which is dual to a conformal field theory. The lack of fermionic superradiance let us describe the wormhole at every region, even at the off-axis region where bosonic field experiences instability due to superradiance. By choosing a certain coupling between the left and right boundaries, the two-point function is modified, and its first order correction contributes the negative energy to open the wormhole. The wormhole is most traversable when the perturbation is turned on at early times, with opening that depends on the mode's frequency, the black hole temperature, and the fermion mass. At late times, the average null energy has damped oscillation behavior until eventually reaches zero. Wormhole with lower temperature have less traversability and it is completely closed at extreme limit. On the other hand, rotation near extreme limit can increases the upper bound on information transfer up to the order of the entropy. Additionally, symmetrical effective potential bumps connected by the wormhole can produce observable echoes. We find that the echo time delay cannot exceed the scrambling time of the black hole.

### [22] [Gravitational multipoles from scattering amplitudes in higher dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05067)
*Francesco Campanella,Fabio Riccioni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统地发展了从散射振幅中提取引力多极矩（gravitational multipole moments）的方法，将其推广至任意维度时空。在四维情形下，仅存在质量和电流两类多极矩，作者分析了自旋1和自旋3/2场与引力的耦合，并推导了含非最小耦合的最一般旋转解。在五维情形下，矢量场仅产生质量四极矩，反对称张量场仅产生应力四极矩，且最小耦合理论无法复现Myers-Perry解的多极结构，揭示了高维中自旋普适性（spin universality）的失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力多极矩是刻画旋转天体时空几何的关键工具，但已有研究多局限于四维时空。随着高维引力理论（如弦论和AdS/CFT对偶）的发展，理解高维旋转解（如Myers-Perry解）的多极结构变得迫切，尤其是自旋-多极耦合的普适性是否在高维中仍然成立尚不清楚。

Method: 基于散射振幅（scattering amplitudes）框架，在四维和更高维时空中系统提取引力多极数据。在四维中，通过分析有质量自旋1和自旋3/2场与引力的最小耦合及非最小耦合，推导相应的Kerr解多极结构。在五维中，对比有质量矢量场与反对称张量场分别与引力耦合的情形，计算其应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）并提取四极矩特征。

Result: 四维情形下，仅存在质量和电流两个独立多极矩；最小耦合理论可复现Kerr解的极矩和八极矩结构。五维情形下，出现无穷多族“应力多极矩（stress multipole moments）”；矢量场耦合仅产生质量四极矩，反对称张量场耦合仅产生应力四极矩，两者的四极结构存在定性差异。最小耦合理论在五维中无法再现Myers-Perry解的多极结构。

Conclusion: 在高维时空中，自旋与多极矩之间的普适对应关系（即自旋普适性）被破坏，这是四维时空所不具备的新特征。这一发现对理解高维引力理论中的旋转解及其全息对偶具有重要启示。

Abstract: We investigate the gravitational multipole structure derived from scattering amplitudes in both four- and higher-dimensional spacetimes, with particular focus on the five-dimensional case. We develop a systematic procedure to extract multipole data from scattering amplitudes in arbitrary dimensions. In four dimensions, only two independent multipole moments exist: mass and current moments. In this setting, we analyze the coupling of massive spin-1 and spin-3/2 fields to gravity, showing how the quadrupole and octupole structure of the Kerr solution arises from minimally coupled theories. We then extend the analysis to include non-minimal couplings, deriving the most general rotating solution with spin-induced multipoles up to octupole order. In higher dimensions, an additional infinite family of ``stress'' multipole moments arises. Focusing on the five-dimensional case, we consider both a massive vector and a massive antisymmetric tensor coupled to gravity, and show that the resulting quadrupolar structure is qualitatively different: while the vector field produces only a mass quadrupole, the antisymmetric tensor generates only a stress quadrupole. By computing the corresponding stress-energy tensor, we demonstrate that minimally coupled theories fail to reproduce the multipolar structure of the Myers-Perry solution. This provides a direct manifestation of the breakdown of spin universality in higher dimensions.

</details>


### [23] [Time-Fractional Schrödinger Evolution in Coupled Double Quantum Dots: Memory Effects on Quantum Resources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05083)
*Abdessamie Chhieb,Mostafa Mansour,Mohamed Ouchrif*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了由两个双量子点（double quantum dots）构成的系统中，纠缠（entanglement）、局部量子不确定性（local quantum uncertainty）和关联相干性（correlated coherence）的时间演化。通过时间分数阶薛定谔方程（time-fractional Schrödinger equation）描述非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）记忆效应，分析了分数阶参数τ、隧穿振幅δ_A/δ_B以及点间相互作用强度𝒱对量子资源生成、稳定与衰减的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在非马尔可夫记忆效应下，双量子点系统中量子资源（纠缠、相干性等）的动力学演化规律，理解分数阶动力学参数τ、隧穿幅值和相互作用强度如何调控这些量子资源的产生与维持。

Method: 采用时间分数阶薛定谔方程（time-fractional Schrödinger equation）对系统动力学进行建模，通过调节分数阶参数τ、隧穿振幅δ_A和δ_B以及点间相互作用强度𝒱，研究了这些关键参数对量子资源演化行为的影响。

Result: 低τ的分数阶动力学快速生成纠缠，可达最大值𝒩≈1，同时产生由局部量子不确定性（local quantum uncertainty）量化的非经典关联；高τ导致纠缠生成减慢，但记忆效应使量子资源在更长时间内保持显著水平（负性≥0.6）。较高的𝒱加速关联并稳定相干性，而隧穿不对称性（tunneling asymmetry）的增强会降低纠缠和相干性。

Conclusion: 分数阶动力学参数τ和系统参数（隧穿振幅、相互作用强度）共同决定了量子资源的生成速度与持续时长，适当调控这些参数有助于在非马尔可夫体系中实现量子资源的高效生成与稳定维持。

Abstract: Our work explore the time evolution of entanglement, local quantum uncertainty, and correlated coherence, within a system modeled by two double quantum dots. The dynamics is represented using a time-fractional Schrödinger equation, which includes memory effects in a non-Markovian regime. We vary the fractional parameter $τ$, the tunneling amplitudes $δ_A$ and $δ_B$, as well as the inter-dot interaction strength $\mathcal{V}$, to investigate how these key parameters govern the generation, stabilization, and decay of quantum resources within the system. The obtained results reveal that, for both initial states, fractional dynamics with a low $τ$ rapidly generates entanglement expecting maximal values $\mathcal{LN}\approx 1$ and non-classical correlations quantified by local quantum uncertainty. Conversely, higher values of $τ$ lead to slower entanglement but memory effects allow quantum resources to remain significant for a longer time, with the negativity remaining above ($\approx 0.6$). We also find that higher interaction frequencies $\mathcal{V}$ accelerate correlations and stabilize coherence, while a strong tunneling asymmetry degrades entanglement and coherence despite the initial benefits of increasing quantum resources.

</details>


### [24] [Subleading Chern-Simons soft factors in perturbative de Sitter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05130)
*Pratik Chattopadhyay,Avi Wadhwa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在具有 $1/\ell^2$ 级微扰德西特（de Sitter）曲率修正的平直时空中，Chern-Simons 微扰对规范理论软定理（soft theorems）在次领头阶 $\mathcal{O}(\omega^0)$ 的修正。结果表明，Chern-Simons 修正与 de Sitter 曲率修正在该阶次不会混合，次领头阶的 Chern-Simons 软因子（soft factors）对 de Sitter 曲率不敏感，暗示了其拓扑本质和普适行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究 Chern-Simons 微扰对规范理论软定理在次领头阶软动量（soft momenta）下的修正，特别是在具有 de Sitter 曲率修正的平直时空中的行为。

Method: 遵循前人工作，在德西特（de Sitter）静态斑块（static patch）中的紧致区域定义微扰散射矩阵（perturbative scattering matrix），并分析 $1/\ell^2$ 级 de Sitter 修正下的 Chern-Simons 软定理。

Result: 在次领头阶 $\mathcal{O}(\omega^0)$ 上，Chern-Simons 修正与 $1/\ell^2$ de Sitter 曲率修正不会混合；次领头阶的 Chern-Simons 软因子对 de Sitter 曲率不敏感。

Conclusion: Chern-Simons 软因子的这一行为暗示了其在振幅层次上的拓扑本质（topological nature），并表明这些软因子具有普适行为（universal behavior）。

Abstract: Chern-Simons perturbations introduce corrections to soft theorems for gauge theories at subleading $\mathcal{O}\left(ω^0\right)$ order in soft momenta. We investigate these soft theorems in flat spacetime with perturbative $1/\ell^2$ de Sitter corrections. Following previous works, we define the perturbative scattering matrix in a compact region in the static patch of de Sitter. We show that Chern-Simons corrections do not mix with the $1/\ell^2$ de Sitter curvature corrections at subleading order $\mathcal{O}\left(ω^0\right)$. Alternatively, one can say that the subleading Chern-Simons soft factors are insensitive to the de Sitter curvature at this order, indicating their topological nature at the level of amplitudes. This also suggests a universal behavior of these Chern-Simons soft factors.

</details>


### [25] [Quantum Entanglement in the Dirac Field Quantization around Charged Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05143)
*Abdessamie Chhieb,Chaimae Banouni,Saliha Abdessamie,Mohamed Ouchrif*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在弯曲时空量子场论框架下，研究了带电Reissner–Nordström黑洞附近狄拉克场的量子纠缠特性，利用concurrence和Bures距离度量发现电荷Q会增强事件视界内的退相干，但反直觉地暂时增加视界外的可访问纠缠，高频模式对引力效应更具鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究带电Reissner–Nordstr&amp;ouml;m黑洞背景下狄拉克场的量子纠缠演化，特别是黑洞电荷Q和霍金辐射对量子关联的影响。

Method: 采用concurrence C和Bures distance B作为纠缠度量（entanglement measures），在弯曲时空量子场论（quantum field theory in curved spacetime）框架下分析量子关联随黑洞电荷Q、费米子模式频率ω及初始纠缠角θ的演化。

Result: 黑洞电荷Q会增强事件视界（event horizon）内的退相干，但反直觉地暂时增加视界外的可访问纠缠；霍金效应导致外部观测者观测到纠缠的表观损失，原因在于关联转移至不可达区域；高频率模式ω对引力效应具有更强的鲁棒性，在视界附近仍保持稳健的关联。

Conclusion: 这些发现揭示了弯曲时空中多体系统内纠缠的再分布机制，对相对论及引力背景下的量子信息研究具有重要启示。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum entanglement properties of the Dirac field near a charged Reissner--Nordström black hole, incorporating the effects of Hawking radiation within the framework of quantum field theory in curved spacetime. Using concurrence \( C \) and Bures distance \( B \) as measures of entanglement, we analyze how quantum correlations evolve with respect to the electric charge \( Q \) of the black hole, the frequency \( ω\) of fermionic modes, and the initial entanglement angle \( θ\). Our results show that the electric charge \( Q \) enhances decoherence inside the event horizon while, counterintuitively, temporarily increasing accessible entanglement outside. The Hawking effect induces an apparent loss of entanglement for an external observer, due to correlation transfer to inaccessible regions. High-frequency modes \( ω\) exhibit greater resilience to gravitational effects, maintaining robust correlations near the horizon. These findings highlight the redistribution of entanglement in a multipartite system in curved spacetime, with significant implications for quantum information in relativistic and gravitational contexts.

</details>


### [26] [On the generalized Komar charge of supersymmetric solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05178)
*Tomás Ortín*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明多种超引力理论（supergravity theories）的超对称解中，由Killing旋子双线性构造的超对称Killing矢量的广义Komar荷恒为零，并利用该性质以坐标无关的方式严格证明了某些解的BPS（Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield）界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有超对称解满足BPS能量下界，但缺乏坐标无关的严格证明。本文旨在建立广义Komar荷在超对称Killing矢量下的消逝性质，从而给出BPS界限的一般性证明框架。

Method: 考虑无规范$\mathcal{N}=2,d=4$超引力（ungauged $\mathcal{N}=2,d=4$ supergravity）与$\mathcal{N}=1,d=5$超引力耦合矢量超多重态，以及纯$\mathcal{N}=1,d=10$超引力。分析这些理论的超对称解，构造Killing旋子（Killing spinors）的双线性量作为超对称Killing矢量，并计算其广义Komar荷（generalized Komar charge）。

Result: 广义Komar荷在超对称Killing矢量下恒为零（vanish identically），该性质不依赖于具体坐标选取。

Conclusion: 利用广义Komar荷的消逝性质，可以以严格、坐标无关的方式证明某些超对称解的BPS界限，为理解超对称解的稳定性与能量下界提供了更普遍的理论基础。

Abstract: We consider the supersymmetric solutions of several supergravity theories (ungauged $\mathcal{N}=2,d=4$ and $\mathcal{N}=1,d=5$ supergravities coupled to vector supermultiplets and pure $\mathcal{N}=1,d=10$ supergravity) and show that their generalized Komar charges vanish identically for the supersymmetric Killing vector which is constructed as a bilinear of the Killing spinors of those solutions. This property can be used to prove the supersymmetry (``BPS'') bounds satisfied by some of those solutions in a rigorous, coordinate-independent way.

### [27] [Exact solutions, trajectories and radiation patterns in the classical relativistic Störmer problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04790)
*Tiberiu Harko,Francisco S. N. Lobo*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了经典Störmer问题的相对论推广，即在纯磁偶极场中带电粒子的相对论性运动。通过协变推导获得运动方程与守恒律，给出了平面运动的参数化解，并对非相对论与相对论区间的粒子动力学进行了数值分析。进一步计算了加速电荷产生的电磁辐射的总功率时间依赖性与频谱，发现功率谱密度中存在明显的特征峰值，表明辐射具有特定频率波段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Störmer问题仅适用于非相对论情形，而实际天体物理或高能等离子体环境中粒子运动速度可能接近光速，因此需要引入狭义相对论效应（special relativistic effects）来推广该模型，以更准确地描述高能粒子在磁偶极场中的动力学行为及其辐射特征。

Method: 从洛伦兹力定律（Lorentz force law）出发，采用完全协变（fully covariant）的方式推导相对论性运动方程及相关守恒律。对于平面运动，获得了参数形式的精确解。同时，对非相对论与相对论两个区间内多种初始条件下的粒子动力学进行了详细的数值分析，并计算了加速电荷所辐射的电磁波的总功率时间依赖性与频率谱（frequency spectrum）。

Result: 给出了平面运动的参数化精确解，揭示了轨迹的结构特征。数值分析展示了相对论修正对不同初始条件下粒子运动的影响。辐射分析提供了总辐射功率随时间的演化规律，且功率谱密度（power spectral density）中清晰呈现出若干分立峰值，指示了辐射中存在的优势频率波段。

Conclusion: 该工作系统地表征了与Störmer型运动相关的磁偶极型辐射（magnetic dipole-type radiation），证明了相对论Störmer问题的粒子会辐射出具有特定频段的电磁波，这对理解天体物理中高能带电粒子在偶极磁场中的辐射机制具有参考价值。

Abstract: We investigate the relativistic generalization of the classical Störmer problem, which describes the motion of charged particles in a purely magnetic dipole field. By incorporating special relativistic effects, the particle dynamics is governed by a strongly nonlinear system of second-order differential equations derived from the Lorentz force law. We present a rigorous and fully covariant derivation of the relativistic equations of motion, together with the associated conservation laws. An exact solution for planar motions is obtained in parametric form, providing analytical insight into the structure of the trajectories. In addition, we perform a detailed numerical analysis of the particle dynamics across both nonrelativistic and relativistic regimes, exploring a range of initial conditions and highlighting the impact of relativistic corrections. The electromagnetic radiation emitted by the accelerated charges is also examined. We compute the time dependence of the total radiated power and determine the corresponding frequency spectrum. Our results provide a comprehensive characterization of magnetic dipole--type radiation associated with Störmer-like motion. In particular, the power spectral density consistently exhibits distinct peaks, indicating the presence of preferred frequency bands in the emitted radiation.

</details>


### [28] [On the spin dependence of the emergent gravity phenomena as observed in axially symmetric black hole accretion with spatially varying adiabatic index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04156)
*Kalyanbrata Pal,Souvik Ghose,Ripon Sk,Arpan Krishna Mitra,Tapas K. Das*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文从天体物理、动力系统和涌现引力三个视角，研究了轴对称吸积黑洞系统。建立了多组分流体在伪Kerr势下的稳态方程，证明解是多跨声速的且可容纳静止激波，并在声学几何中识别出声学黑洞与白洞，计算了其表面引力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多组分流体且绝热指数空间变化（spatially varying adiabatic index）的条件下，低角动量轴对称吸积（axisymmetrically accreting）系统的动力学行为尚未被充分理解，尤其缺乏从涌现引力（emergent gravity）视角对其声学几何的研究。

Method: 利用伪Kerr势（pseudo-Kerr potential）建立多组分流体的稳态方程；采用微扰动力系统方法（perturbative dynamical systems methods）对临界点（critical points）进行分类；通过线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）检验稳态解的径向稳定性；借助Carter–Penrose图（Carter–Penrose diagram）构造声学黑洞（acoustic black hole）与声学白洞（acoustic white hole）的因果结构；使用考虑局域声速空间变化的广义表达式计算声学视界（acoustic horizon）的表面引力（surface gravity）。

Result: 稳态解是多跨声速的（multi-transonic），且可容纳静止激波（stationary shock）。临界点处的解在径向扰动下保持稳定。在声学几何中，声速点（sonic point）处形成声学黑洞，激波位置处形成声学白洞。

Conclusion: 从天体物理、动力系统和涌现引力三个视角的统一分析表明，低角动量轴对称吸积系统在伪Kerr势下存在稳定的多跨声速解和激波结构，其声学几何中同时存在声学黑洞与声学白洞，且广义表面引力公式可有效应用于空间变声速的吸积流。

Abstract: The present work addresses an axisymmetrically accreting black hole system from three perspectives: the astrophysical, the dynamical systems, and the emergent gravity standpoint. Steady-state equations governing low angular momentum axially symmetric accretion under a pseudo-Kerr potential are formulated for a multi-species flow with a spatially varying adiabatic index. The resulting transonic solutions are shown to be multi-transonic and may accommodate a stationary shock. Critical points are classified via perturbative dynamical systems methods, and linear stability analysis confirms that the stationary solutions remain stable under radial perturbation. The ensuing acoustic geometry harbours acoustic black holes at the sonic points and an acoustic white hole at the shock location, whose causal structure is constructed via the Carter--Penrose diagram. The surface gravity associated with each acoustic horizon is computed using a generalized expression that accounts for the spatial variation of the local sound speed.

Abstract: Theta-graphs are a type of spatial graph with two vertices connected by three edges. We investigate embeddings of theta-graphs in the square and simple cubic lattices, using a combination of the Wang-Landau Monte Carlo method with a variant of the BFACF algorithm which accommodates vertices of degree 3. This allows us to estimate the critical exponents governing the number of theta-graphs and the distributions of the different arm-lengths. For the cubic lattice these values can be compared to the corresponding exponents for prime knots. We also study the number of `monodisperse' theta-graphs where the three arms have the same lengths, and find evidence supporting a conjecture for the critical exponent in two dimensions.

### [30] [Finite-size scaling properties of classical random walk on various two-dimensional lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04492)
*Nimish Sharma,Tanay Nag*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了方格、Kagome、Lieb、蜂窝和骰子等多种二维有限晶格上无偏经典随机游走的统计特性，发现游走者距离的标准差对晶格剖面（lattice profile）的非均匀性不敏感，输运仍为扩散型。所有有限晶格的质量分形维数（mass fractal dimension）集中在1.50±0.03范围内，壳层分形维数（hull fractal dimension）集中在1.37±0.03范围内，且两者均随步数增加趋向布朗运动的热力学极限值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究较少系统考察晶格剖面（即最近邻数目与连接模式）对经典随机游走行为的影响。本文旨在通过多种二维有限晶格的对比，揭示晶格拓扑结构（lattice topology）差异是否以及在何种程度上改变无偏随机游走的扩散特性与分形维数。

Method: 在方格（square）、Kagome、Lieb、蜂窝（honeycomb）和骰子（dice）等有限二维晶格上实施无偏经典随机游走模拟；通过计算游走距离的标准差、质量分形维数和壳层分形维数进行量化分析，并结合置信区间（confidence intervals）与数据塌缩（data collapse）分析评估晶格剖面差异的影响。

Result: 游走距离的标准差对晶格剖面非均匀性不敏感，扩散输运特性在有限晶格中保持。质量分形维数位于1.50±0.03窗口内，Lieb晶格取最小值，方格晶格取最大值，存在与平均配位数相关的弱排序，但多对晶格的置信区间存在统计重叠（statistical overlap）。壳层分形维数位于1.37±0.03窗口内，排序趋势与质量分形维数定性一致，置信区间修正了定量顺序；方格晶格明确呈现上界，其余晶格统计重叠显著。数据塌缩分析表明，随着步数增加，两种分形维数均趋向布朗运动的热力学极限值。

Conclusion: 有限二维晶格上的无偏随机游走对晶格剖面细节具有鲁棒性（robustness），扩散行为及分形维数主要由晶格维度而非局部连接模式主导。质量和壳层分形维数分别在窄窗口内变化，且随步数增加收敛于布朗运动的热力学极限，这表明有限尺度效应（finite-size effect）在随机游走动力学中起关键作用。

Abstract: We consider various two-dimensional lattices such as square, Kagome, Lieb, honeycomb, dice lattices of finite extent, to study the effect of lattice profile in terms of the number of nearest neighbour and connectivity patterns on the classical random walk in the unbiased scenario. We find that the standard deviation of distance travelled by the walker is insensitive to the non-uniformity of the lattice profile leading to diffusive transport even in the finite size lattices. Our study indicates that the mass fractal dimension varies within a window $1.50\pm 0.03$ for all finite-size lattices. A weak ordering within the above window, correlated with the average coordination number, is observed, while Lieb and square lattices yielding the minimum and maximum values, respectively. However, confidence intervals reveal substantial statistical overlap for several lattice pairs even though the lattice profiles vary as far as the average number of connecting bonds and directionality of bonds are concerned. We also study the scaling complexity of the circumference of the closed curve traced by the walker while investigating the hull dimension. We find similar trend for hull fractal dimension as well and that was found to within the window $1.37\pm 0.03$ for finite-size lattices. Within the above window, the ordering remains qualitatively unaltered as compared to mass dimension while the confidence interval rectifies the order quantitatively. The square lattice clearly exhibits the upper bound for hull fractal dimension and the remaining lattices show extensive statistical overlap within the above window. We exhibit a tendency of the mass and hull fractal dimension to reach their thermodynamic values given by Brownian motion when we allow more number of steps within the finite size of the lattice, as confirmed by a data collapse analysis.

</details>


### [31] [The unique, universal entropy for complex systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04493)
*Kenric P. Nelson*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文为复杂系统建立了熵的公理化基础，证明了耦合拉伸指数分布（coupled stretched exponential distributions）最大化的耦合熵（coupled entropy）是唯一满足信息尺度与广延性（extensivity）要求的通用熵，并指出Tsallis q-统计在复杂系统物理建模中会导致偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去数十年的复杂系统熵研究中，缺失了两个关键要求：熵必须测量最大化分布所在信息尺度下的不确定性（该尺度下对数-对数斜率为-1），且熵必须跨Hanel-Thurner定义的全部普适性标度类（universality scaling classes）具有广延性。

Method: 采用公理化方法（axiomatic approach），推导出耦合熵是唯一满足上述要求的通用熵，该熵由耦合拉伸指数分布最大化。通过非可加性（non-additivity）刻画长程依赖（long-range dependence）或非线性统计耦合，并建立了熵匹配的广延性与耦合参数、拉伸参数及维度之间的函数关系。

Result: 证明了耦合熵的唯一性和普适性；明确了非可加性与长程依赖或非线性统计耦合的等价关系；提供了证据表明Tsallis q-统计在复杂系统物理建模中会导致失配（misalignment）。

Conclusion: 回顾了信息热力学（information thermodynamics）的应用，包括复杂性度量、温度的零阶定律（zeroth law）、耦合自由能的热力学一致性，以及非平衡态中的智能模型。

Abstract: An axiomatic foundation regarding the entropy for complex systems is established. Missing from decades of research was the requirement that entropy must measure the uncertainty at the informational scale of the maximizing distribution, where the log-log slope equals $-1$. Additionally, entropy must be extensive across the full universality scaling classes defined by Hanel-Thurner. The coupled entropy, maximized by the coupled stretched exponential distributions, is proven to be the unique, universal entropy that satisfies these requirements. The non-additivity of the entropy is equal to the long-range dependence or nonlinear statistical coupling. The entropy-matched extensivity is a function of the coupling, stretching parameter, and dimensions. Evidence is provided that the Tsallis $q$-statistics creates misalignment in the physical modeling of complex systems. Information thermodynamic applications are reviewed, including measuring complexity, a zeroth law of temperature, the thermodynamic consistency of the coupled free energy, and a model of intelligence in non-equilibrium.

</details>


### [32] [Role of mass fluctuations in the diffusion of clusters of Brownian particles with activity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04812)
*Daniela Moretti,Pasquale Digregorio,Giuseppe Gonnella,Antonio Suma*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本论文从单粒子朗之万方程出发，推导了一个描述活性布朗粒子（ABPs）团簇反常扩散的最小理论框架。该模型由团簇质心轨迹与质量演化$N(t)$两个耦合随机方程构成，解析求解得到长时扩散系数由传统项$(\propto N_0^{-1}$)与涨落驱动项$(\propto N_0^{-δ})$之和构成，当后者占主导时出现反常标度行为。模型预测$D\sim N^{-α}$，$α=0.63\pm0.06$，与大规模ABP模拟定量吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性布朗粒子团簇中观测到质心扩散系数随团簇粒子数$N$呈反常标度$D\sim N^{-1/2}$，这偏离了常规的$N^{-1}$依赖关系，亟需建立一个最小理论框架来解释这一反常扩散行为。

Method: 从单粒子朗之万方程出发，推导出两个耦合随机方程：一个描述团簇质心轨迹，另一个描述质量演化$N(t)$，其中明确考虑了粒子附着和脱离引起的随机位移。在稳态孤立团簇条件下，将$N(t)$建模为高斯过程，均值为$N_0$，方差$\propto N_0^β$，持续时间$\propto N_0^κ$。对耦合方程进行解析求解得到长时扩散系数。

Result: 长时扩散系数表达为两项之和：传统项$\propto N_0^{-1}$源自热噪声与主动力求和，涨落驱动项$\propto N_0^{-δ}$，其中指数$δ=2-2/d-β+κ$（$d$为空间维度）。当涨落驱动项占主导时，系统呈现反常标度。模型预测$D\sim N^{-α}$，$α=0.63\pm0.06$，与大规模ABP模拟定量吻合。

Conclusion: 该理论框架成功捕捉了ABP团簇反常扩散的核心机制——粒子附着与脱离引起的团簇质量涨落驱动了反常标度行为。模型预测与大规模模拟的定量一致，验证了该最小框架的有效性和预测能力。

Abstract: Motivated by the anomalous diffusion observed in clusters of active Brownian particles (ABPs), where the center-of-mass diffusion coefficient scales as $D\sim N^{-1/2}$ with respect to the number $N$ of particles in the cluster, we derive a minimal theoretical framework starting from the single-particle Langevin equations. The model consists of two coupled stochastic equations: one for the cluster center-of-mass trajectory and one for the mass evolution $N(t)$, explicitly accounting for stochastic displacements induced by particle attachment and detachment. We specialize and validate the framework against ABP simulations of isolated clusters in stationary conditions, where $N(t)$ follows a Gaussian process with mean $N_0$, variance $\propto N_0^β$, and persistence time $\propto N_0^κ$. Analytical solution of the coupled equations yields the long-time diffusion coefficient as the sum of two contributions: a conventional term $\propto N_0^{-1}$) due to thermal noise plus summation of active forces, and a fluctuation-driven term $\propto N_0^{-δ}$ with $δ=2-2/d-β+κ$, where $d$ is the spatial dimension. We demonstrate that anomalous scaling emerges whenever the second term becomes dominant. The model predicts $D\sim N^{-α}$ with $α=0.63\pm0.06$, in good quantitative agreement with large-scale ABP simulations.

</details>


### [33] [Nonequilibrium Fluctuation-Response Theory in the Frequency Domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05038)
*Euijoon Kwon,Hyun-Myung Chun,Hyunggyu Park,Jae Sung Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一套频域（frequency domain）统一涨落-响应理论（fluctuation-response theory），适用于过阻尼朗之万动力学（overdamped Langevin dynamics）和马尔可夫跳跃过程（Markov jump processes）驱动的非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady states）。该理论将一般可观测量的功率谱（power spectrum）精确表达为相同频率下局域响应的二次型，将静态非平衡涨落-响应关系推广至有限频率。由此推导出频域响应不确定关系（response uncertainty relations）、动力学与热力学不确定关系、平衡涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）及Harada-Sasa型关系，并通过随机网络与驱动扩散系统展示了该理论在分解涨落谱与揭示涨落、响应和耗散之间频域权衡方面的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非平衡涨落-响应关系主要局限于静态（零频率）情形，缺乏系统的有限频率框架。该工作旨在构建一个统一的频域涨落-响应理论，将静态结果推广至任意频率，以揭示非平衡稳态中涨落、响应与耗散之间的频率依赖性关系。

Method: 针对过阻尼朗之万动力学和马尔可夫跳跃过程两类非平衡系统，在频域中推导出一个精确的恒等式：将一般可观测量的功率谱表达为相同频率下局域响应的二次型。对于朗之万系统采用空间分解，对于马尔可夫跳跃过程采用边分解（edge-resolved）形式，统一适用于态依赖可观测量、流类可观测量及其组合。

Result: 从同一恒等式推导出频域响应不确定关系、动力学与热力学不确定关系、平衡涨落-耗散定理以及Harada-Sasa型关系。应用至随机网络和驱动扩散系统，展示了涨落谱可分解为边贡献，并揭示了涨落、响应和耗散之间的频率依赖性权衡。

Conclusion: 该理论为非平衡稳态提供了一个统一的频域涨落-响应框架，能够将涨落谱分解为局域响应贡献，并揭示频率依赖的涨落-响应-耗散权衡关系，适用于多种非平衡系统。

Abstract: We develop a unified fluctuation-response theory in the frequency domain for nonequilibrium steady states governed by overdamped Langevin dynamics and Markov jump processes. The relation expresses the power spectrum of general observables exactly as a quadratic form of local responses measured at the same frequency, thereby extending static nonequilibrium fluctuation-response relations to finite frequencies. The decomposition is spatial for Langevin systems and edge-resolved for Markov jump processes, and applies uniformly to state-dependent observables, current-like observables, and their combinations. As consequences of the same identity, we derive frequency-domain response uncertainty relations, kinetic and thermodynamic uncertainty relations, the equilibrium fluctuation-dissipation theorem, and Harada-Sasa-type relations. Applications to stochastic networks and driven diffusive systems illustrate how the theory resolves fluctuation spectra into edge-wise contributions and reveals frequency-dependent tradeoffs between fluctuations, response, and dissipation.

</details>


### [34] [Kink-kink correlations in nonlinear quenches across a quantum critical point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05106)
*Lakshita Jindal,Kavita Jain*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过研究一维横场伊辛模型（1D TFIM）在代数型淬火下的动力学，发现除了Kibble-Zurek（KZ）标度外，还存在一个退相位长度（dephasing length）来描述高阶关联函数，且关联函数以压缩指数形式衰减，其指数随淬火指数连续变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期对线性淬火下1D TFIM的研究发现，淬火动力学不仅依赖于KZ标度，还依赖于另一个由低能模有限相位差产生的长度标度，且关联函数并非指数衰减。本文旨在检验这些性质是否具有普遍性（universality），将其推广到横场在临界点附近代数变化的情形。

Method: 采用绝热微扰论（adiabatic perturbation theory）、解析论证以及对相关方程进行精确数值积分（exact numerical integration）三种方法相结合的方式，研究淬火结束时等时纵向扭结-扭结关联函数（equal-time, longitudinal kink-kink correlation function）。

Result: (i) 对于超线性淬火（superlinear quenches），关联函数仅由KZ长度决定；否则还需要一个额外的退相位长度来描述。(ii) 退相位后的关联函数以压缩指数（compressed exponential）形式衰减，其指数随淬火指数（quench exponent）连续变化。

Conclusion: 淬火动力学的非KZ标度行为及其压缩指数衰减形式具有普遍性，但对于超线性淬火情形，退相位长度不再起作用，仅KZ标度即可描述关联函数。

Abstract: When a quantum system exhibiting a second order phase transition is quenched across the critical point in large but finite time, the dynamics are not adiabatic in the critical region and the Kibble-Zurek (KZ) mechanism provides a framework to determine local observables such as the mean defect density. However, to find higher-point functions, one has to go beyond the KZ paradigm asshown in recent works on one-dimensional transverse field Ising model (TFIM) following a linear quench. It has been found that (i) besides the KZ scale, the quench dynamics depend on another length scale that arises due to the finite phase difference between the low energy modes, and (ii) contrary to the expectations based on the KZ mechanism, in general, the correlation functions do not decay exponentially with distance. Motivated by these results for the linear quench, we are interested in understanding if these properties are universal, and consider the 1D TFIM when the transverse field varies algebraically in the vicinity of the critical field. We focus on the equal-time,longitudinal kink-kink correlation function at the end of the quench from the paramagnetic to the ferromagnetic phase, and find that (i) the correlator depends only on the KZ length for superlinear quenches, otherwise an additional dephasing length is required to describe it, and (ii) the dephased correlator decays as a compressed exponential with an exponent that changes continuously with the quench exponent. Our results are obtained using an adiabatic perturbation theory, analytical arguments and exact numerical integration of the relevant equations.

</details>


### [35] [Lattice Tadpoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05137)
*S G Whittington*

TL;DR: 本文针对格点（lattice）中嵌入的蝌蚪构象（tadpoles，或称为套索 lassos）的数量渐近行为，证明了若干严格结果，涵盖头部受非结（unknotted）约束以及尾部穿透头部所张曲面等情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解格点中嵌入蝌蚪（套索）构象的计数渐近行为，特别是当头部受到拓扑约束（如无结）或尾部与头部所张曲面存在几何干涉时，这些约束如何影响构象数量的增长规律。

Method: 采用严格的数学证明方法，对格点蝌蚪构象的渐近计数进行分析，考虑头部受非结约束以及尾部穿透头部所张曲面等不同约束条件。

Result: 针对上述多种约束情形下的蝌蚪构象数量，获得了严格的渐近行为结果。

Conclusion: 证明的严格结果揭示了格点蝌蚪构象在不同拓扑与几何约束下的计数渐近性质，为理解这类复杂构象的统计行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We prove several rigorous results about the asymptotic behaviour of the numbers of tadpoles (or lassos) embedded in a lattice, including cases where the head is subject to a constraint like being unknotted, or where the tail pierces the surface spanned by the head.

### [36] [Singular Behavior of Observables at Hopf Bifurcations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05194)
*Benedikt Remlein,Massimiliano Esposito*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明，在Hopf分岔（Hopf bifurcation）驱动的自持振荡系统中，即使不存在奇异的定常态（stationary state），时间平均观测量（time-averaged observable）也会普遍出现奇异性（singularity）。该奇异性的根源是几何性的：对极限环（limit cycle）的相位平均消除了振荡振幅的奇次幂项，而振幅平方随分岔参数平滑变化，导致观测量在分岔点处呈现有限但导数不连续的行为，形成类似于埃伦费斯特（Ehrenfest）分级的奇异性层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hopf分岔是驱动系统中产生自持振荡（self-sustained oscillation）的普遍途径。传统观点认为奇异行为通常与定常态的奇异性相关，但该论文旨在揭示：即使不存在奇异的定常态，时间平均观测量在Hopf分岔的振荡起点处也能普遍表现出奇异性。

Method: 从几何角度出发，通过对分岔后出现的周期吸引子（periodic attractor）进行相位平均（phase averaging），分析振荡幅度对观测量的影响。利用振幅平方随分岔距离平滑变化、而相位平均会消除振幅奇次幂项这一特性，推导出时间平均观测量展开为整数幂级数的形式，并据此分析其导数的不连续性。

Result: 平滑的时间平均观测量超量可展开为整数幂级数；观测量在分岔点处有限，但有限阶导数出现不连续，形成埃伦费斯特式的Hopf奇异性层次。一般的观测量呈现折线型奇点（kink singularity），而对称性或几何抵消可推迟非解析性出现的位置。该机制在化学、电子和气候振荡器中均得到了验证。

Conclusion: 超临界Hopf分岔（supercritical Hopf bifurcation）是一种产生非解析观测量行为的普适机制——奇异性可以在没有奇特定常态的情况下出现。这为无发散现象的奇异行为提供了一种通用场景。

Abstract: Hopf bifurcations are a universal route to self-sustained oscillations in driven systems. Despite the absence of any singular stationary state, we show that time-averaged observables generically exhibit singularities at the onset of oscillations. The origin of this behavior is geometric: phase averaging over the emergent periodic attractor eliminates odd powers of the oscillation amplitude, while the squared amplitude varies smoothly with the distance from the bifurcation. Consequently, the excess of any smooth time-averaged observable admits an integer-power expansion; observables remain finite but display discontinuities in finite-order derivatives. This yields an Ehrenfest-like hierarchy of Hopf singularities, in which the first nonanalytic derivative is determined by the lowest-order coupling between the observable and the limit-cycle waveform that survives phase averaging. Generic observables therefore exhibit kink singularities, while symmetry or geometric cancellations can suppress lower-order couplings and shift nonanalyticity to higher derivatives. We demonstrate this mechanism in chemical, electronic, and climate oscillators. Our results identify supercritical Hopf bifurcations as a universal mechanism for nonanalytic observable behavior, where singular features arise without any underlying singular stationary state. They thus provide a generic setting for singular behavior without divergence.

</details>

### [37] [Kitaev chain in synthetic dimension with cavity-controlled Majorana modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04384)
*Adel Ali,Alexey Belyanin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于可调合成维度（synthetic dimension）的平台，用于实现Kitaev链（Kitaev chain）物理并高度可控地操纵马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）。该平台利用超导LC电路与朗道量子化二维电子系统的耦合，通过合成维度构造费米子Kitaev链，并在角动量晶格边界产生马约拉纳零模。其核心优势在于可通过LC谐振器实现非局域、鲁棒的马约拉纳态读出与控制，为拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computing）提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实现马约拉纳零模的方案在可调性和非局域读出方面存在局限，亟需一个兼具高度可控性与鲁棒读出的物理平台来推进拓扑量子计算。

Method: 基于一个通用的朗道量子化二维电子系统（Landau-quantized 2D electron system），将其与超导LC电路的磁通耦合。超导LC电感器的结构化矢量势（structured vector potential）在最下朗道能级（lowest Landau level）的电子角动量态之间诱导吸引相互作用，这些角动量态构成一个合成维度，用于实现Kitaev链，马约拉纳零模存在于该角动量晶格（angular-momentum lattice）的边界。

Result: 该平台能够通过LC谐振器对马约拉纳态进行鲁棒且非局域的读出与控制。所提出的方案依赖于成熟的电路QED（circuit QED）和半导体技术。

Conclusion: 本工作为拓扑量子计算提供了一条有前景的实现路径，兼具高可调性、非局域控制与现有技术兼容性等优势。

Abstract: We introduce a tunable synthetic-dimension platform for realizing Kitaev-chain physics with high degree of control over Majorana zero modes. It is based on a generic Landau-quantized two dimensional electron system coupled to the magnetic flux of a superconducting LC circuit. The structured vector potential of a superconducting LC inductor induces attractive interactions between electron angular-momentum states at the lowest Landau level. These states serve as a synthetic dimension for the coveted fermionic Kitaev chain, with Majorana zero modes existing at the boundaries of the angular-momentum lattice. The crucial advantage of this proposal is the possibility of a robust, nonlocal readout and control of the Majorana states by a LC resonator. The platform relies on mature circuit QED and semiconductor technologies and provides a promising pathway to topological quantum computing.

</details>


### [38] [Giant orbital-magnon conversion driven perpendicular magnetization switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04486)
