Abstract: The pursuit of beyond-Moore information technologies has stimulated the exploration of novel information carriers, such as electron spin, orbital, and magnon, beyond electron charge. Efficient interconversion among these degrees of freedom and precise control over the information states are crucial for advancing nanoelectronic devices. However, a direct coupling between orbital angular momentum (L) and magnons (M) has remained elusive, and magnetization switching through orbital-to-magnon (L-M) conversion has not yet been achieved. Here, we report the experimental demonstration of L-M conversion in an orbital metal/antiferromagnetic insulator bilayer at room temperature, with an efficiency over an order of magnitude higher than that in traditional orbital systems lacking the L-M process. Consequently, we achieved efficient room-temperature perpendicular magnetization switching in a CoFeB ferromagnetic layer mediated by this new mechanism. Our findings establish a direct link between orbitronics and magnonics, providing a new platform for the development of advanced nano-devices based on orbital-driven magnonic phenomena.

### [39] [Quantum Coherence Reshapes Thermodynamic Bounds for Thermal Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04648)
*Sergi Vidal,Alba Mayor-Fernandez,Rosa Lopez*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文分析了热力学不确定性关系（TUR）及其多维推广（MTUR）在量子热器件（双端导体，工作于热机、制冷机或热泵模式）中的表现。研究发现，即使在相干输运主导区域，经典性能极限仍受TUR约束；进一步明确了优化TUR与MTUR违背的条件，并证明在近线性响应区域，电流交叉关联可提升电荷与热流的联合精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学不确定性关系（TUR）及其多维推广（MTUR）为电流涨落与熵产生之间建立了普适界限，但它们在具体量子热器件中的适用性与优化条件尚待系统分析。本研究旨在以双端导体为范例，检验TUR/MTUR在量子热机、制冷机和热泵等不同工作模式下的约束行为，并探索提升联合精度的条件。

Method: 以双端导体（two-terminal conductor）为量子热器件（quantum thermal device）范例，考虑其分别工作于热机（heat engine）、制冷机（refrigerator）和热泵（heat pump）三种模式。通过分析电流协方差与均值满足的矩阵不等式，检验TUR与MTUR的约束行为；并在相干输运（coherent transport）和近线性响应（linear-response regime）区域中识别优化违背的条件。

Result: 在有限功率或冷热库间热流维持的条件下，即使处于相干输运主导区域，经典性能极限（效率和性能系数）仍受TUR约束。MTUR的违背可在一定条件下得到优化。在近线性响应区域，电流间的交叉关联（cross-correlations）能够增强电荷与热流联合测量的精度。

Conclusion: TUR在量子热器件中仍普遍约束经典性能极限，而MTUR的违背可通过优化条件实现；交叉关联效应为提升多参量联合精度提供了新途径。该结果对量子热力学和量子器件设计具有指导意义。

Abstract: Thermodynamic Uncertainty Relations (TURs) set universal bounds linking current fluctuations to entropy production in nonequilibrium steady states. Their multidimensional generalization (MTUR) introduces matrix inequalities connecting current covariances and mean values. We analyze these bounds in a paradigmatic quantum thermal device, a two-terminal conductor, operating as a heat engine, refrigerator, or heat pump. We show that classical performance limits on efficiency and coefficient of performance remain constrained by the TUR when finite power or heat flow from cold to hot reservoirs is maintained, even in regimes dominated by coherent transport. We further identify the conditions that optimize TUR and MTUR violations, demonstrating that cross-correlations can enhance the joint precision of charge and heat currents near the linear-response regime.

### [40] [Spin-wave bandgap engineering via mode hybridization in dipolar-coupled YIG film/CoFeB nanodisk magnonic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04774)
*Junyoung Hyun,Krzysztof Szulc,Mateusz Zelent,Nikolai Kuznetsov,Lukáš Flajšman,Maciej Krawczyk,Paweł Gruszecki,Sebastiaan van Dijken*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种由低阻尼钇铁石榴石（YIG）薄膜与CoFeB纳米圆盘周期阵列耦合构成的混合二维磁子晶体（magnonic crystal），发现其自旋波（spin-wave）能带结构中出现显著且可调的带隙（bandgap），这些带隙并非源于传统布拉格散射（Bragg scattering），而是由基模与周期性纳米盘激发的横向驻波模式之间的杂化（hybridization）所引起。通过改变几何参数和纳米盘的磁态（包括涡旋结构），可有效调控带隙的位置和宽度；在较大晶格周期下，还会出现由二维色散折叠（dispersion folding）引起的额外带隙。该工作将模式杂化确立为超越布拉格散射约束的能带工程设计机制，为基于偶极耦合混合架构的可重构磁子器件（reconfigurable magnonic devices）提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁子晶体中带隙的形成通常依赖于布拉格散射，这受限于晶格周期与波长之间的匹配条件，难以实现灵活可调的能带结构。本工作的动机在于探索一种不依赖布拉格散射的新型带隙形成机制——模式杂化（mode hybridization），以实现对自旋波能带结构更灵活的调控，并以此为基础发展可重构的磁子器件。

Method: 实验上采用了传播自旋波谱学（propagating spin-wave spectroscopy）、超奈奎斯特磁光克尔效应显微镜（super-Nyquist magneto-optical Kerr effect microscopy）以及微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）三种手段，系统研究了YIG薄膜与CoFeB纳米圆盘周期阵列耦合构成的二维混合磁子晶体中的自旋波输运特性。

Result: 观察到显著且可调的带隙，这些带隙不源于布拉格散射，而是来源于磁子晶体基模与周期性纳米盘所诱导的面内横向驻波模式（in-plane transverse standing modes）之间的杂化。带隙的频谱位置和宽度可通过几何参数及纳米盘的磁态（包括其涡旋结构（vortex configuration））进行调控。在较大晶格周期下，通过与沿自旋波传播方向横向和纵向量子化的模式杂化，出现了额外的带隙，反映了二维色散折叠效应。

Conclusion: 本工作将模式杂化确立为一种超越布拉格散射限制的自旋波能带工程设计机制，表明基于偶极耦合混合架构可以实现可重构的磁子器件，为下一代自旋波器件的发展提供了新的物理原理和设计思路。

Abstract: We investigate spin-wave transport in hybrid two-dimensional magnonic crystals comprising a low-damping yttrium iron garnet (YIG) film coupled to a periodic array of CoFeB nanodisks. Using propagating spin-wave spectroscopy, super-Nyquist magneto-optical Kerr effect microscopy, and micromagnetic simulations, we demonstrate the formation of pronounced and tunable bandgaps that do not originate from conventional Bragg scattering. Instead, these gaps arise from hybridization between the fundamental magnonic-crystal mode and in-plane transverse standing modes induced by the periodic nanodisk array. The spectral position and width of these gaps are controlled by geometric parameters and by the magnetic state of the nanodisks, including their vortex configuration, which governs both static and dynamic dipolar coupling. For larger lattice periods, additional gaps emerge through hybridization with modes quantized both transverse and parallel to the spin-wave propagation direction, reflecting dispersion folding in two dimensions. Our results establish mode hybridization as a versatile mechanism for engineering spin-wave band structures beyond the constraints of Bragg scattering and provide a pathway toward reconfigurable magnonic devices based on dipolar-coupled hybrid architectures.

### [41] [Magnetic Brightening and Nanoscale Imaging of Spin-Polarized Helical Edge Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04883)

Abstract: Efficient sub-10 nm electric transport remains a major challenge for nanoelectronics due to high losses and impedance mismatches in conventional Drude metals. In addition, the infrared edge electrodynamic response scales nearly linearly with atomic layer number, providing compelling evidence that magnetic-field-induced gaps do not disrupt individual-layer edge states at energies of around 100 meV. These results sharply contrast with microwave and DC transport, where even small magnetically induced gaps decrease edge conduction. Magnetically tunable, topologically robust high-frequency edge modes open a pathway toward ultralow-loss nanoscale interconnects and quantum logic architectures for next-generation microelectronics, spintronics and quantum information science.

### [42] [Guidelines for band gap opening in graphene superlattices with periodic π-vacancy distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04900)
*Diyan Unmu Dzujah,Hongde Yu,Thomas Heine*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于最近邻紧束缚模型（nearest-neighbor tight-binding model）研究石墨烯超晶格（graphene superlattice, GSL）中周期性π空位（π-vacancy）的对称性条件，阐明C₂型和C₃型空位构型打开能隙的对称性要求，并发现镜面对称性（mirror symmetries）的缺失会导致狄拉克锥（Dirac cone）偏离Γ点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性π空位可通过改变π带色散在石墨烯中打开能隙，但决定空位构型能否打开能隙的对称性条件尚不明确，因此需要系统研究。

Method: 采用每个碳位点一个p_z轨道的最近邻紧束缚模型，将π空位（如功能化、取代或缺失的碳位点）建模为π基组中位点的删除，并将所有与被删除位点相关的跳跃矩阵元设为零。重点分析具有C₂和C₃点群对称性的π空位构型。

Result: 3n × 3n （n=1,2,3,…）的石墨烯超晶格将K和K'点折叠到Γ点，从而能打开能隙。C₃型空位使狄拉克锥固定在Γ点；C₂型空位若保留一对垂直镜面对称性σ_v ⊥ σ_d，也能将狄拉克锥约束在Γ点；若σ_v和σ_d镜面缺失，狄拉克锥将偏离Γ点至(±Δq, ±Δq)。

Conclusion: 石墨烯超晶格中是否打开能隙以及狄拉克锥的位置由π空位构型的点群对称性（point-group symmetry）和镜面对称性共同决定，这对设计基于对称性的能带工程（band engineering）策略具有指导意义。

Abstract: Periodic $π$-vacancies in graphene superlattices (GSLs) provide a symmetry-based route to band-gap opening in graphene by modifying the $π$-band dispersion. However, the symmetry conditions that determine whether a vacancy motif can open a band gap remain unclear. Here, we investigate periodic $π$-vacancy GSLs using a nearest-neighbor tight-binding model with one $p_z$ orbital per carbon site to identify the symmetry requirements for gap opening. $π$-vacancies, representing functionalized, substituted, or missing carbon sites, are modeled as site deletions in the $π$ basis, with all hopping matrix elements to and from the deleted sites set to zero. We focus on $π$-vacancy motifs with $C_2$ and $C_3$ point-group symmetry. A $3n \times 3n$ GSL, where $n=1,2,3,\ldots$ is the integer scaling factor multiplying the honeycomb primitive-cell vectors, folds $K$ and $K'$ to $Γ$ and can therefore open a band gap. For $C_3$-type vacancies, the Dirac cones remain pinned at high-symmetry points and thus stay at $Γ$ in folded $3n$ GSLs. In contrast, $C_2$-type vacancies that reduce the global point group of the GSL to $D_{2h}$ by preserving a pair of perpendicular mirror symmetries, $σ_v \perp σ_d$, can also constrain the Dirac cones to $Γ$. When the $σ_v$ and $σ_d$ mirror planes are absent, the cones are allowed to shift away from $Γ$ to $(\pm Δq,\pm Δq)$ in the $3n$ superlattice.

### [43] [Sculpting Spin-Wave Landscapes via Curvature of 2D Magnonic Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05156)

Method: 在周期为400 nm的正方形晶格排列的三维纳米金字塔大面积曲线纳米模板上，沉积50 nm厚的坡莫合金（Permalloy）薄膜，利用模板引入的周期性退磁场景观来调控自旋波的色散关系。实验采用微聚焦布里渊光散射（micro-focused Brillouin light scattering）测量，并结合数值模拟进行验证。

Abstract: Engineering the dispersion relation is one of the key ingredients enabling the application of spin waves in computational elements. One way to engineer the spin-wave band structure is to create an artificial magnonic crystal, which can be used to design specific band gaps or dispersion branches. However, creating a two-dimensional magnonic crystal usually requires removing material, which dramatically decreases the decay lengths of spin waves. Here, we present a method to manipulate the demagnetizing field landscape by utilizing large-area curvilinear nanotemplates consisting of three-dimensional nanopyramids arranged in a square lattice with a period of 400 nm. In a 50-nm-thick Permalloy film grown on these curvilinear templates, we experimentally observe a complete in-plane band gap together with flat-band modes that exhibit strong real-space localization of the spin waves in the pyramid valleys. Micro-focused Brillouin light scattering measurements corroborate the numerically predicted dispersion and reveal the possibility of opening and closing this gap by varying the external magnetic field. Our results establish three-dimensional-templated continuous films as a versatile platform for two-dimensional signal processing and magnonic computing elements.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 菱方石墨烯（rhombohedral graphene）中存在丰富的关联相（correlated phases），且这些相对位移场（displacement field）高度敏感。实验观察到电子-空穴不对称性：空穴掺杂侧的关联态在较小位移场下出现，而分数量子反常霍尔效应（fractional quantum anomalous Hall effect, FQAHE）仅在大位移场的电子掺杂侧被观测到。这一显著不对称性突显了理解平带（flat bands）如何随位移场演变的必要性。

Method: 采用静电栅控（electrostatic gating）的纳米角分辨光电子能谱（nanospot angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）技术，直接可视化菱方五层石墨烯（rhombohedral pentalayer graphene, R5G）中位移场诱导的能带结构变化。

Result: 除能隙打开和谱权重重新分布（反映层极化）外，栅控场驱动了平带的强不对称修饰：平价带（flat valence band, FVB）在高场下演变为M形色散，而平导带（flat conduction band, FCB）随场增强逐渐展平。与计算对比识别出控制R5G能带曲率的关键参数，由此产生的有限贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和近理想量子几何（quantum geometry）支持在大场下电子掺杂时拓扑相的出现。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了不对称相图、能带结构演化与量子几何之间的直接联系，为理解菱方石墨烯中的关联相和拓扑相提供了一个微观框架。

Abstract: Rhombohedral graphene exhibits an exceptionally diverse array of correlated phases that depend sensitively on the displacement field. Compiling reported phases into a unified phase diagram reveals a pronounced field-dependent electron-hole asymmetry: correlated states on the hole-doped side emerge at small displacement fields, whereas the fractional quantum anomalous Hall effect (FQAHE) is observed exclusively on the electron-doped side under large displacement fields. This stark asymmetry highlights the need to understand how flat bands evolve with displacement fields. Here, we directly visualize the field-induced electron-hole asymmetric band flattening in rhombohedral pentalayer graphene (R5G) using nanospot angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy with electrostatic gating. Beyond gap opening and spectral weight redistribution indicative of layer polarization, the gating field drives a strongly asymmetric modification of the flat bands: the flat valence band (FVB) evolves into an M-shaped dispersion at high field, whereas the flat conduction band (FCB) progressively flattens with increasing field. Comparison with calculations identifies critical parameters governing the band curvature of R5G, from which the resulting finite Berry curvature and near-ideal quantum geometry support the emergence of topological phases under electron doping at large fields. These results establish a direct link between the asymmetric phase diagram, band structure evolution, and quantum geometry, providing a microscopic framework for understanding correlated and topological phases in rhombohedral graphene.

</details>


### [45] [Mixed-Parity Altermagnetism in Collinear Spin-Orbital Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05205)
*Zheng-Yang Zhuang,Jin-Xin Hu,Song-Bo Zhang,Lun-Hui Hu,Zhongbo Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现共线反铁磁体（collinear antiferromagnet）中可以存在混合宇称自旋劈裂（mixed-parity spin splitting），即既非纯粹偶宇称也非纯粹奇宇称，并通过对称性分析和双亚点阵双轨道模型展示了圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）在不同交错势（staggered potential）下诱导混合宇称与奇宇称交变磁性（altermagnetism）的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要将交变磁性（altermagnetism）理解为偶宇称（even-parity）或奇宇称（odd-parity）形式，尚未系统探讨是否存在混合宇称（mixed-parity）的自旋劈裂（spin splitting）情形。

Method: 通过对称性分析（symmetry analysis）识别混合宇称交变磁性的对称条件；采用双亚点阵双轨道模型（two-sublattice two-orbital model）进行理论计算，研究圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）对交错势（staggered potential）参数的调控效应。

Result: 在二维体系中，当两个反平行自旋扇区（antiparallel spin sectors）由单一镜面对称性（single mirror symmetry）关联时，混合宇称交变磁性可出现于自旋-轨道磁体（spin-orbital magnet）中。圆偏振光在有限交错势下诱导混合宇称交变磁性，在零交错势下诱导奇宇称自旋-轨道交变磁性。自旋分辨轨道埃德尔斯坦效应（spin-resolved orbital Edelstein effect）可作为探测自旋-轨道序（spin-orbital order）的互补电学探针（complementary electrical probe）。

Conclusion: 混合宇称交变磁性作为偶宇称与奇宇称交变磁性之间的中间自旋劈裂（intermediate spin-split regime）形式，在保持自旋劈裂和零净磁化（zero net magnetization）的前提下连接了两种已知宇称类型，拓展了交变磁性的理论框架。

Abstract: Altermagnetism has so far mainly been understood in its even- and odd-parity forms. We show that collinear antiferromagnets with zero net magnetization can also host mixed-parity spin splitting, namely neither purely even nor purely odd in momentum. We identify the symmetry conditions for such mixed-parity altermagnetism and show that, in two dimensions, it can arise in spin-orbital magnets when the two antiparallel spin sectors are related by a single mirror symmetry. Using a two-sublattice two-orbital model, we demonstrate that circularly polarized light induces mixed-parity altermagnetism at finite staggered potential and odd-parity spin-orbital altermagnetism at zero staggered potential. Mixed-parity altermagnetism thereby emerges as the intermediate spin-split regime between even- and odd-parity altermagnetism when spin splitting and zero net magnetization are maintained. Spin-resolved orbital Edelstein effects provide a complementary electrical probe of the underlying spin-orbital order.

</details>

### [46] [Meta-LegNet: A Transferable and Interpretable Framework for Surface Adsorption Prediction via Self-Defined Adsorption-Environment Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04102)
*Yifan Li,Arravind Subramanian,Xiaoqing Liu,Qiujie Lyu,Sergey Kozlov,Lei Shen*

TL;DR: 本文提出Meta-LegNet，一种结合SE(3)-等变消息传递、体素多尺度聚合与跨领域元学习的图学习框架，通过学习可迁移的局部吸附环境表示，实现对未探索催化剂表面的吸附位点快速、可解释地预测，无需穷举位点枚举。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算催化面临的核心挑战是高效识别低能量且化学合理的吸附构型，现有方法依赖位点枚举与迭代优化，计算成本高且难以扩展到复杂表面或多吸附质系统。

Method: Meta-LegNet采用SE(3)-等变原子级消息传递（SE(3)-equivariant atom-level message passing）结合体素多尺度聚合（voxel-based multiscale aggregation）与跨领域元学习（cross-domain meta-learning）。模型通过不变径向特征与等变方向信息编码局部化学环境，利用坐标帧体素池化、基于分配的升采样和门控特征融合整合更广的结构上下文，生成原子分辨的归因图以可解释方式识别吸附相关的局部环境。

Result: 基于学习到的表示构建了吸附环境数据库，并开发了模板匹配策略，能够在未探索表面上提出可能的吸附位点而无需穷举位点枚举。

Conclusion: 学习可迁移的吸附环境表示为加速催化剂筛选提供了一种准确、可解释且实用的途径。

Abstract: A central challenge in computational catalysis is the identification of low-energy and chemically plausible adsorption configurations, as these directly affect adsorption energies, reaction pathways, and catalytic performance. Existing approaches generally rely on enumerating candidate adsorption sites followed by iterative refinement through density functional theory calculations or machine-learning-based relaxations. However, such workflows remain computationally expensive and are difficult to scale to complex surfaces or multi-adsorbate systems. Here, we introduce Meta-LegNet, a graph learning framework that combines SE(3)-equivariant atom-level message passing with voxel-based multiscale aggregation and cross-domain meta-learning to learn transferable representations of local adsorption environments across diverse catalyst--adsorbate systems. Rather than following a conventional regression-only paradigm, Meta-LegNet encodes local chemical environments using invariant radial features and equivariant directional information, and further incorporates broader structural context through coordinate-frame voxel pooling, assignment-based upsampling, and gated feature fusion. The resulting local-global decomposition produces atom-resolved attribution maps, which are processed to identify adsorption-relevant local environments in an interpretable manner. Based on the learned representations, we further construct an adsorption-environment database and develop a template-matching strategy to propose likely adsorption sites on previously unexplored surfaces without exhaustive site enumeration. Overall, our results suggest that learning transferable adsorption environments provides an accurate, interpretable, and practical route for accelerating catalyst screening.

Result: 成功获得了V₋⁻中心激发态精细结构及赝Jahn-Teller效应的定量描述，明确了单重态-三重态准简并行为，确定了光致发光参数和系间穿越路径，并揭示了应力对精细结构和衰减参数的影响规律。

Conclusion: 研究结果不仅澄清了hBN中V₋⁻中心的基本行为，而且为改进V₋⁻中心的读出机制（readout）以推进集成二维量子传感器（integrated 2D quantum sensors）的发展奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Ensembles of negatively charged boron vacancy (V$_{\text{B}}^-$) centers in hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) have emerged as a two-dimensional spin qubit system interfaced with optics to advance nanoscale quantum sensing. In this work, we model the energetics, structural relaxation, and transition rates of the V$_{\text{B}}^-$ center using a high-level wave-function-based electron correlation method (CASSCF-NEVPT2). We provide a thorough analysis of the excited state fine structure and pseudo Jahn-Teller effects, singlet-triplet quasi-degeneracies, photoluminescence parameters, intersystem crossing pathways, and stress-dependence of the fine structure and decay parameters. Our findings not only clarify the fundamental behavior of the V$_{\text{B}}^-$ center in hBN but also establish the theoretical foundation for advancing the V$_{\text{B}}^-$ center's readout for integrated 2D quantum sensors.

### [48] [Spin Dynamics from Atomistic Quantum Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04294)
*Enrico Drigo,Marquis M. McMillan,Benjamin Pingault,Yinan Dong,F. Joseph Heremans,David D. Awschalom,Giulia Galli*

TL;DR: 本文基于久保线性响应理论（Kubo linear-response theory）推导了固态自旋缺陷（spin defects）中自旋-晶格弛豫时间 \(T_1\) 和退相干时间 \(T_2\) 的表达式，并结合分子动力学（molecular dynamics）与机器学习（machine learning）模型生成的自旋-晶格耦合时间序列进行数值计算，最终以金刚石NV色心（NV center）为例，实验与理论取得了良好一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光活性固态自旋缺陷在量子应用中前景广阔，但目前尚缺乏一个统一的理论框架来预测其在高温下的自旋动力学（spin dynamics）。

Method: 首先，利用久保线性响应理论（Kubo linear-response theory）推导出自旋-晶格弛豫时间 \(T_1\) 和退相干时间 \(T_2\) 关于自旋-晶格耦合关联函数（correlation functions）的表达式。随后，基于第一性原理（ab-initio）数据训练的先进机器学习模型生成自旋-晶格相互作用时间序列，并联合分子动力学模拟来评估 \(T_1\) 和 \(T_2\)。

Result: 通过测量金刚石NV色心（NV center）的 \(T_1\) 时间，并将实验结果与理论计算结果进行对比，两者展现出极好的一致性（excellent agreement）。

Conclusion: 该工作为预测固态自旋缺陷在高温下的自旋动力学提供了一种可行的理论框架，结合机器学习与分子动力学的方法具有较高精度与实用性。

Abstract: Optically active solid-state spin defects are promising candidates for quantum applications, however a unified theoretical framework to predict their spin dynamics at high temperatures is not yet available. Here, using Kubo linear--response theory, we derive expressions of spin-lattice and decoherence times \(T_1\) and \(T_2\) in terms of correlation functions of spin--lattice couplings. We then evaluate \(T_1\) and \(T_2\) from molecular dynamics and spin--lattice interaction time--series generated by state--of--the--art machine learning models trained on {\it ab--initio} data. Finally we measure \(T_1\) times for the NV center in diamond and compare experimental and theoretical results, showing excellent agreement.

### [49] [Hydrogen-induced volume expansion in hexagonal close-packed iron: Effects of pressure and temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04315)
*Yuichiro Mori,Masahiro Takano,Hiroyuki Kagi,Katsutoshi Aoki,Sho Kakizawa,Noriyoshi Tsujino,Yuji Higo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过高压高温实验合成了可控氢含量的六方密堆积（hcp）结构氢化铁（FeHₓ），利用原位X射线衍射测量构建了其在10–25 GPa和300–900 K条件下的状态方程，揭示了氢致体积膨胀系数对压力和温度的依赖关系，并指出基于氢致体积膨胀估算行星内部铁中氢含量时需修正压力和温度（PT）依赖性及晶体结构的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢是类地行星内核轻元素的重要候选，铁中掺氢会导致显著体积膨胀和密度亏损。然而，由于实验上难以控制氢含量，六方密堆积（hexagonal close-packed, hcp）结构氢化铁（hcp-FeHₓ）的热弹性性质（thermoelastic properties）此前尚未明确。

Method: 在高压高温条件下合成可控氢含量的hcp-FeHₓ样品；利用Kawai型多砧压机（Kawai-type mutilanvil apparatus）在10–25 GPa和300–900 K范围内进行原位X射线衍射（in situ X-ray diffraction）测量，构建其状态方程（equation of state）。

Result: 结合已有hcp-Fe的状态方程和hcp-FeHₓ中氢含量的实验测定，发现氢致体积膨胀系数（hydrogen-induced volume expansion coefficient）的差异可由其压力与温度依赖性清晰解释。hcp-Fe中氢致体积膨胀在低压下呈现强温度依赖性，但该温度效应随压力升高而显著减弱；铁的氢化致密度降低还依赖于其晶体结构。

Conclusion: 结果表明，基于氢致体积膨胀估算行星内部条件下铁中氢含量的方法，需充分考虑压力-温度（PT）依赖性及晶体结构的影响，进行相应修正。

Abstract: Hydrogen is a promising candidate for the light element in terrestrial planetary cores. Its incorporation into iron causes significant volume expansion, leading to a substantial density deficit. Although extensive studies have been conducted on iron hydride (FeH$_{x}$) with the fcc structure, the thermoelastic properties on FeHx with hcp structure (hcp-FeH$_{x}$) remain unconstrained because of the experimental difficulties to control hydrogen content. Here, we synthesized hcp-FeH$_{x}$ with controlled hydrogen contents under high-pressure and high-temperature conditions. We carried out \textit{in situ} X-ray diffraction measurements on hcp-FeH$_{x}$ at 10--25~GPa and 300--900~K using a Kawai-type mutilanvil apparatus and constructed their equations of state. By combining our results with previously reported equations of state for hcp-Fe and experimental determinations of hydrogen content in hcp-FeH$_{x}$, we demonstrated that the discrepancies in the hydrogen-induced volume expansion coefficient can be clearly explained by its pressure and temperature dependence. Our results revealed that the hydrogen-induced volume expansion of hcp-Fe exhibits a strong temperature dependence at low pressures, but its temperature effect significantly weakens with increasing pressure. We also showed that the density reduction of Fe by hydrogenation depends on its crystal structure. These findings demonstrate that estimates of hydrogen content in iron at planetary interior conditions based on hydrogen-induced volume expansion need to be revised by properly accounting for its $PT$-dependence and crystal structure.

</details>


### [50] [Magnetic influence on ion transport in concentrated solid solutions: An analytic investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04370)
*Timothy Carlson,Sanjay Govindjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文从理论上分析了磁场对固态离子导体（solid ionic conductors）中离子输运（ion transport）的影响，推导了包含磁场效应的多组分输运方程，并针对二元和单离子导体建立了具体模型。通过拟合Pb₀.₆₆Cd₀.₃₄F₂的磁阻实验数据，验证了模型的有效性，表明磁场在某些条件下可显著改变固体中的离子输运行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁场已被发现对电子导体的输运有显著影响，但对固态离子导体中类似效应的研究较少。尽管霍尔迁移率（Hall mobility）测量在离子导体中鲜有报道，近期电池等系统中的实验表明，外加磁场可以显著且有利地改变固体中的离子输运与电化学过程，这一现象无法通过简单的霍尔系数估计预测。因此，需要从理论上系统分析磁场对固体中离子输运的影响。

Method: 采用解析分析方法，推导了考虑磁场效应的通用多组分输运方程（multi-component transport equations）。在此基础上，进一步推导了固态、各向同性二元导体（binary conductors）和单离子导体（single ion conductors）的具体模型。针对受成分约束的系统，计算了磁场影响可能显著的材料性质组合。

Result: 所推导的二元导体在磁场中的模型能够很好地拟合氟离子导电固体Pb₀.₆₆Cd₀.₃₄F₂的实验磁阻（magneto-resistance）数据，前提是假设该材料近似呈简并多组分输运（near degenerate multi-component transport）行为。

Conclusion: 磁场可以显著影响固态离子导体中的离子输运，且理论模型与实验数据吻合良好，表明磁场效应在离子导体中不可忽略。该工作为理解和预测磁场下固体离子输运行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: It is well established that magnetic fields have a significant effect on transport in certain classes of electronic conductors. Less reported, however, are similar effects in solid ionic conductors. Despite the rarity of Hall mobility measurements in ionic conductors, recent experimental work in batteries and other systems has demonstrated that an applied magnetic field can significantly and beneficially alter ionic transport and electrochemical processes in solid materials in a way that would not be predicted from naïve Hall coefficient estimates. In this work, the influence of a magnetic field on ion transport in solids is investigated analytically, and general multi-component transport equations accounting for magnetic effects are presented. Specific models are then derived for solid, isotropic binary and single ion conductors. Material property combinations for which magnetic field influence may become significant are then computed for certain systems subject to compositional constraints. Finally, it is demonstrated that the derived model for binary conductors in a magnetic field fits experimental magneto-resistance data well for the fluoride ion conducting solid Pb$_{0.66}$Cd$_{0.34}$F$_2$, provided an assumption of near degenerate multi-component transport.

</details>


### [51] [Thermodynamics of stacking faults and phase stability in cobalt alloys: A combined computational and experimental study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04420)
*Zheng Zhong,Ziqi Cui,Yu Zhuo,Tianyu Yu,Jianfeng Cai,Kaibo Zou,Jiacheng Shen,Bowen Huang,Zhuoming Xie,Huiqiu Deng,Yang Yu,Hao Zhang,Wangyu Hu,Tengfei Yang,Jie Hou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理热力学（first-principles thermodynamics）与微观结构表征相结合，定量评估了有限温度下合金元素对Co合金及WC-Co硬质合金中层错能（stacking fault energy）和相稳定性（phase stability）的影响，揭示了原子错配体积和磁性贡献的关键作用，并给出了与实验相图一致的合金化效应预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层错能决定了Co合金和WC-Co硬质合金的相稳定性与变形行为，但有限温度下合金化效应的定量评估尚不完善，缺乏从原子到宏观尺度的系统理解。

Method: 将第一性原理热力学与微观结构表征相结合，在0K下分析过渡金属溶质的层错能，并引入声子（phonon）、电子（electronic）、纵向自旋涨落（longitudinal spin-fluctuation）和磁性自由能（magnetic free-energy）贡献，构建有限温度模型。

Result: 0K下过渡金属溶质的层错能主要由原子错配体积（atomic misfit volume）决定；4d和5d元素呈一致线性趋势，而特定3d溶质因磁性贡献出现显著偏差。V、Ni、Fe、Mo、W通过稳定fcc相降低相变温度，Cr和C则相反。微观分析证实，Co中溶解的W含量越高，有限温度下的层错能越高，抑制层错形成。

Conclusion: 该工作阐明了合金化调控Co基体系层错能与相稳定性的物理机制，为Co基合金和WC-Co硬质合金的设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Stacking fault energy dictates phase stability and deformation behavior in Co alloys and WC-Co cemented carbides, yet a quantitative assessment of alloying effects at finite temperatures remains poorly established. By integrating first-principles thermodynamics with microstructural characterization, we provide a rigorous evaluation of these influences across atomic and macroscopic scales. We show that stacking fault energetics at 0K for transition metal solutes are primarily governed by atomic misfit volume. While 4d and 5d elements follow a consistent linear trend, specific 3d solutes exhibit significant deviations due to non-negligible magnetic contributions. By incorporating phonon, electronic, longitudinal spin-fluctuation, and magnetic free-energy contributions, the model accurately captures the fcc-hcp transformation and quantifies how diverse solutes modulate the phase landscape. We demonstrate that V, Ni, Fe, Mo, and W lower the transformation temperature by stabilizing fcc phase, while Cr and C exhibit the opposite effect, consistent with experimental phase diagrams. Furthermore, microscopic analysis confirms that higher W content dissolved in the Co suppresses stacking-fault formation by elevating the stacking fault energy at finite temperatures. This work clarifies the physical mechanisms by which alloying regulates stacking fault energy and phase stability in Co-based systems, providing guidance for the design of Co-based alloys and WC-Co cemented carbides.

</details>


### [52] [Unveiling the Atomistic Mechanisms of Shear-Induced LDA$\leftrightarrow$HDA Transformations and Shear Banding in Amorphous Silicon under High Pressures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04521)
*Hao Chen,Valery I. Levitas,Tengyi Liu,Jingyu Lu,Rui Zhu,Zhongqiang Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模分子动力学模拟（large-scale molecular dynamics simulations），结合高斯近似势（Gaussian Approximation Potential），研究了非晶硅（amorphous silicon）在剪切变形下的低密度非晶相（LDA）与高密度非晶相（HDA）之间的压力诱导相变（pressure-induced PT），以及剪切带（shear band, SB）的形成机制。模拟揭示了剪切诱导的LDA↔HDA可逆相变动力学、剪切带内反常的HDA原子分数下降、湍流状流动促进逆相变等现象，并建立了基于机制的解析模型来描述剪切应变主导的相变动力学与稳态行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非晶材料在高压力下由塑性应变诱导的相变（plastic strain-induced PTs）的机制与动力学，这对于高压物理学和材料科学具有重要的基础研究价值和广泛的应用前景。

Method: 采用最先进的高斯近似势（Gaussian Approximation Potential）进行大规模分子动力学模拟，模拟非晶硅在恒定压力下的剪切变形，涵盖从低密度非晶相（LDA）到高密度非晶相（HDA）的相变以及剪切带（SB）的形成。同时建立了基于机制的解析模型（mechanism-based analytical model）来描述剪切应变控制的动力学过程。

Result: LDA↔HDA剪切诱导相变同时发生直至达到稳态；剪切使LDA→HDA相变起始和完成的压力分别降低4.36 GPa和5.10 GPa；低压下无相变时出现剪切带，而在9.8 GPa高压下相变部分抑制了剪切带形成；剪切带内部HDA原子分数出现意料之外的急剧下降，尽管该区域剪切更大且预期HDA比例更高；剪切带内发现湍流状流动（turbulent-like flow with swirls），更有效地促进HDA→LDA逆相变；揭示了非晶硅中的相变诱导塑性（transformation-induced plasticity）。

Conclusion: 本文揭示的塑性应变诱导相变机制与动力学，为非晶材料在高压下的变形行为提供了新的认识，具有重要的基础科学意义和广泛的应用价值。

Abstract: Large-scale molecular dynamics simulations of shear deformation under constant pressures of amorphous silicon, PT from low-density-amorphous (LDA) to high-density-amorphous (HDA) Si, and formation of shear bands (SBs) are performed using the state-of-the-art Gaussian Approximation Potential. The simulations reveal that LDA$\leftrightarrow$HDA shear-induced PTs occur simultaneously until reaching steady state. The developed mechanism-based analytical model well describes shear-strain-governed kinetics and steady states at all pressures, independent of shear stresses. Shear reduces the pressure for initiation and completion of LDA$\rightarrow$HDA PT by $4.36$ and $5.10$ GPa, respectively. Without PT at low pressure, shear-banding occurs, which is partially suppressed by PT at higher pressure with uniform deformation-PT at $9.8$ GPa. Despite the much larger shear and expected fraction of HDA, surprising sharp drop in the HDA atomic fraction within the SB was discovered. In bulk, Si deforms by atomic rearrangement in localized shear transformation zones with high nonaffine displacements, which trigger nucleation of HDA clusters within LDA and, concurrently, of LDA clusters within HDA, without growth and coalescence. In SB, a turbulent-like flow with swirls is revealed, which promotes reverse PT from HDA$\rightarrow$LDA more effectively. Transformation-induced plasticity in amorphous Si is revealed. The findings open up basic research into the mechanisms and kinetics of plastic strain-induced PTs in amorphous materials under high pressure, with numerous important applications.

### [53] [Dielectric, magnetic, and magnetodielectric behaviors of BaFe12O19 hexaferrite modulated by Mn and Ti substitutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04620)
*Xiao-Fan Zhang,Yang Yang,Ze-Qing Guo,Li Lv,Can Gao,Jian-Ping Zhou,Xiao-ming Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过固相反应法制备了Mn和Ti单掺杂及共掺杂的BaFe12O19 M型六角铁氧体，系统揭示了不同掺杂元素对离子占位、磁序、介电响应和磁介电效应的影响机制，表明通过在不同Fe³⁺位点进行取代可有效调控M型六角铁氧体的物理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过Mn和Ti元素在BaFe12O19六角铁氧体中进行单掺杂与共掺杂，以调控其磁结构、介电性质和磁介电效应，并阐明不同离子占位与物理性能之间的内在关联。

Method: 采用固相反应法（solid-state reaction）制备了Mn单掺杂、Ti单掺杂及Mn-Ti共掺杂的BaFe12O19六角铁氧体；利用拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）和形成能（formation energy）分析确定离子占位；通过磁化率、介电谱和磁介电（magnetodielectric, MD）测量表征物理性能。

Result: Mn离子优先占据4f2和2b位，Ti离子主要取代4f1和12k位的Fe³⁺离子；Ti掺杂引入低温非共线纵向圆锥自旋序（noncollinear longitudinal conical spin order），其中BaFe6Mn3Ti3O19将该自旋序保持至室温；Ti⁴⁺取代通过调节超交换作用（superexchange interaction）和降低c轴单轴磁晶各向异性来稳定圆锥自旋序；掺杂引入两个不同的转变温度；纯BaFe12O19在低温呈现量子顺电行为（quantum paraelectric behavior），Mn-Ti掺杂通过三角双锥内电偶极子的退耦破坏该行为；低温介电响应由电子跳跃和极化子效应主导，高温则由Maxwell-Wagner界面极化和电子跳跃贡献；纯样在10 K的负磁介电效应源于自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling），共掺杂样则源于磁场诱导的非共线自旋序产生的电极化；高温下磁介电效应主要来自磁场对电子跳跃和非本征界面极化的调制。

Conclusion: M型六角铁氧体的物理性能可通过在不同Fe³⁺晶格位点进行取代掺杂进行有效调控，这为设计具有可控磁电耦合特性的多功能铁氧体材料提供了策略依据。

Abstract: We prepared Mn- and Ti mono-doped and co-doped BaFe12O19 hexaferrites via solid-state reaction. Mn ions preferentially occupy the 4f2 and 2b sites, while Ti ions mainly substitute the Fe3+ ions at 4f1 and 12k sites as revealed by the Raman spectroscopy and formation energy. Pure BaFe12O19 exhibits ferrimagnetism. The hexaferrites related to Ti doping have noncollinear longitudinal conical spin order at low temperatures, where BaFe6Mn3Ti3O19 retains this spin order up to room temperature. Ti4+ substitution at 4f1 and 12k sites plays a pivotal role in stabilizing the noncollinear conical spin order through adjusting the superexchange interactions and reducing the uniaxial magnetocrystalline anisotropy along the c-axis. The magnetic response exhibits two distinct transition temperatures because Ti4+ ions interrupt the magnetic superexchange interactions with two inequivalent exchange integrals. Pure BaFe12O19 presents a quantum paraelectric behavior at low temperatures, which is disrupted by Mn-Ti doping due to the decoupling of electric dipoles within the triangular bipyramid. Electron hopping and polaronic effects dominate the dielectric response at 10 - 50 K, while Maxwell-Wagner interfacial polarization and electron hopping contribute to dielectric dispersion at higher temperatures. The negative MD effect of pure BaFe12O19 and BaFe6Mn3Ti3O19 at 10 K originates from spin-phonon coupling and electric polarization induced by noncollinear spin order under magnetic field, respectively. The Mn-Ti co-doped samples achieve relatively higher MD responses at low magnetic fields. In higher temperatures, the MD effect arises mainly from the magnetic field modulation of the electron hopping with non-intrinsic interfacial polarization. This research reveals the physical properties of M-type hexaferrite can be modulated through substituting Fe3+ ions at different sites.

### [54] [Effective long-range attraction of moiré excitons under the influence of atomic reconstructions and anisotropic screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04667)
*Nils-Erik Schütte,Carl Emil Mørch Nielsen,Niclas Götting,Alexander Steinhoff,Gabriel Bester,Christopher Gies*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在过渡金属二硫族化物双层中，小转角产生的moiré图案具有长晶格周期，其能带调制可作为层间激子的有效势，有望实现关联多体现象。现有研究缺乏对激子-激子相互作用的材料真实建模，尤其是未充分考虑晶格重构和各向异性介电屏蔽效应。

Method: 采用材料真实的建模方法，在模型中同时引入晶格重构（lattice reconstructions）以及包含二维双层和各向异性介电背景（anisotropic dielectric screening）的激子-激子势，计算on-site与长程相互作用，并将所得相互作用势和跳跃振幅（hopping amplitudes）作为Bose-Hubbard模型的参数。

Result: 晶格重构会显著改变moiré势，进而导致on-site相互作用发生强烈修正；在moiré周期尺度的长程相互作用中，各向异性介电屏蔽导致相互作用从排斥（repulsive）转变为吸引（attractive）。

Conclusion: 所得的相互作用势与hopping振幅可作为moiré晶格上Bose-Hubbard模型的参数，用于解释层间激子的关联行为。

Abstract: The moiré pattern, which emerges due to a relative rotation between two monolayers of transition metal dichalcogenides, features a long lattice period for small twist angles. The resulting band structure modulation acts as an effective potential for interlayer excitons (IXs), which can realize correlated many-body phenomena. Here, we aim for a material-realistic modelling of the exciton-exciton interaction, taking into account lattice reconstructions and an exciton-exciton potential that incorporates the highly anisotropic screening imposed by the two-dimensional bilayer and the dielectric background. We find strong modifications of the on-site interaction induced by the change of the moiré potential during lattice reconstructions, while for long-range interactions on the length scale of the moiré period, anisotropic dielectric screening leads to a crossover from a repulsive to an attractive interaction. The interaction potential and hopping amplitudes serve as parameters for a Bose-Hubbard model on the moiré lattice, which we use to explain correlated behavior of interlayer excitons.

### [55] [Plastic deformation of B19' martensite where -- where it matters in NiTi technology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04669)
*Petr Šittner,Hanuš. Seiner,Petr Sedlák,Orsolya. Molnárová,Lukáš Kadeřávek,Ondřej Tyc,Elizaveta Iaparova,Luděk Heller*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统回顾了镍钛（NiTi）形状记忆合金中B19'马氏体通过"扭折化（kwinking）"机制实现优异塑性变形的独特现象，该机制由位错滑移扭折（kinking）与变形孪晶（deformation twinning）协同构成，并讨论了其对NiTi技术及本构建模的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示并总结过去50年文献中只能用扭折化（kwinking）机制才能合理解释的诸多反常塑性变形现象，从而阐明该机制在NiTi合金技术中的核心作用。

Method: 采用文献综述方法，系统梳理了B19'马氏体通过位错滑移扭折（dislocation slip based kinking）辅助变形孪晶（deformation twinning）实现的扭折化（kwinking）塑性变形机制，并归纳了9类相关实验现象。

Result: 归纳了9类只能用kwinking机制解释的反常现象，包括：大压下量冷加工不产生裂纹、马氏体态塑性变形可达约80%应变且应力超过1 GPa、拉伸变形使奥氏体微结构细化至准非晶态、奥氏体中高密度{114}变形带的出现、强化NiTi丝在屈服点颈缩断裂、Lüders带传播导致的大局部应变（约40%）、超弹性拉伸中异常长的上应力平台（>8%应变）、单次恒应力冷热循环下产生大塑性应变（>20%）、以及已退火NiTi在外约束下加热实现形状设定。

Conclusion: 扭折化（kwinking）是NiTi马氏体塑性变形的独特机制，能解释一系列长期令人困惑的实验现象；该机制对NiTi技术的本构建模及实际应用（如冷加工、形状设定）具有重要影响。

Abstract: Nitinol technology, besides utilizing the functional thermomechanical properties derived from the B2 cubic to B19' monoclinic martensitic transformation, also exploits the excellent plastic deformability of NiTi in the martensite state. It originates from the unique mechanism of plastic deformation of the B19' martensite by kwinking involving dislocation slip based kinking assisted by deformation twinning. Although the mechanism of plastic deformation of martensite by kwinking was revealed only very recently, various unusual phenomena that can only be rationalized by kwinking, have been reported in literature in the last 50 years. These phenomena include: 1) cold working with a high degree of reduction without introducing cracks, 2) excellent plastic deformability in the martensite state (plastic deformation up to~80% strain at stresses >1GPa), 3) refinement of austenitic microstructure to a quasi-amorphous state by tensile deformation, 4) observation of high density of {114} deformation bands in austenitic microstructures, 5) systematic ruptures of strengthened NiTi wires in tensile tests via necking at the onset of plastic yielding, 6) localized plastic deformation in tensile tests via propagation of Lüders band fronts with very large localized strain (~40%), 7) unusually long upper stress plateaus in superelastic tensile tests (>8% strain), 8) large plastic strains (> 20 %) generated in a single closed-loop cooling/heating cycle under constant stress, 9) shape setting of already annealed NiTi by heating under external constraint. Finally, we discuss how kwinking deformation was considered in constitutive modelling of thermomechanical behaviors of NiTi and, particularly, what is the role of the kwinking deformation in NiTi technology.

### [56] [Dynamical pseudopotentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04673)
*Matteo Quinzi,Tommaso Chiarotti,Nicola Marzari*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种动态（能量依赖）赝势框架，通过引入广义模守恒条件和极点求和表示，显著提高了对全电子散射的再现精度，并首次在统一的多体总能泛函中一致地处理全电子原子、赝原子和固体体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 赝势理论（pseudopotential theory）通过用有效势替代化学惰性的芯电子（core electrons），极大推动了材料的第一性原理计算，但这本质上是一个嵌入问题（embedding problem）。作者受此启发，希望将芯电子的约化形式化为动态嵌入势，从而克服传统赝势在能量依赖性和多体一致性上的局限性。

Method: 首先引入动态（能量依赖）赝势（dynamical pseudopotential）框架，导出广义模守恒条件（generalized norm-conservation conditions）。然后采用极点求和表示（sum-over-poles representation），将参考能量（reference energies）的数量与投影算符（projectors）的数量解耦，从而在极宽的能量范围内高精度地再现全电子散射（all-electron scattering）行为。

Result: 该框架能在多个参考能量上以高精度重现全电子散射，且适用的能量范围显著扩展。进一步表明，这些赝势可自然纳入多体总能泛函（many-body total energy functionals），首次在同一电子结构理论中一致地处理全电子原子、赝原子（pseudo-atom）和固体体系。

Conclusion: 动态赝势框架实现了对全电子散射的高精度模拟，并在多体总能泛函层面统一了不同体系的描述，为第一性原理计算中芯电子与价电子的分离提供了更一致的理论基础。

Abstract: Pseudopotential theory has greatly driven first-principles calculations in materials, replacing the explicit treatment of the chemically inert core electrons with an effective potential acting only on the valence states. This is inherently an embedding problem, where tracing out the core electrons can be formulated in terms of a dynamical embedding potential. Motivated by this perspective, we first introduce a framework for dynamical (i.e., energy-dependent) pseudopotentials, showing how this leads to generalized norm-conservation conditions. Then, adopting a sum-over-poles representation, we disentangle the number of reference energies from the number of projectors; this allows to reproduce all-electron scattering at many reference energies with great accuracy and over very extended energy ranges. We further show that these pseudopotentials enter naturally into many-body total energy functionals, leading for the first time to a consistent and unified treatment of the all-electron atom, the pseudo-atom, and the solid within the same electronic-structure theory.

</details>


### [57] [A Two-Step Chemical Vapor Deposition Process for the Synthesis of an Ir(111)/Borophene/2D-Hexagonal Boron Nitride Heterostructure by Intrinsic Segregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04871)
*Marko A. Kriegel,Karim M. Omambac,Smruti R. Mohanty,Tobias Hartl,Stefan Schulte,Niels Ganser,Pascal Dreher,Alexandra Rödl,Steffen Franzka,Germán Sciaini,Thomas Michely,Frank-J. Meyer zu Heringdorf,Michael Horn-von Hoegen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种利用硼嗪（borazine）作为单一前驱体，通过两步超高真空化学气相沉积法合成垂直Ir(111)/硼烯（borophene）/六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride）异质结构的方法。该过程利用硼在铱中的有限溶解度，先在高温低压下建立近表面硼储层，再在高压下生长六方氮化硼单层，降温过程中硼析出形成硼烯单层，最终实现整片Ir衬底上均匀覆盖的微米级晶粒异质结构。该内禀偏析辅助生长策略为二维材料垂直异质结构的可扩展合成提供了可行路线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现高质量、可扩展的二维材料垂直异质结构（vertical heterostructure）合成方法，是当前材料科学领域的重要挑战。现有方法通常步骤复杂或难以控制界面质量，亟需开发更为简洁、可规模化且具有良好结晶质量的生长策略。

Method: 采用两步超高真空化学气相沉积法（UHV-CVD），以硼嗪为单一前驱体，利用硼在铱（Ir）衬底中的有限溶解度（finite solubility）。第一步在高温低前驱体压力下建立近表面硼储层；第二步在较高前驱体压力下促进六方氮化硼（hBN）单层生长；降温过程中硼溶解度降低，驱动硼偏析（segregation）至表面，在hBN覆盖层下方形成硼烯（borophene）单层。通过互补的斑点轮廓分析低能电子衍射（SPA-LEED）、低能电子显微镜（LEEM）和扫描隧道显微镜（STM）进行表征。

Result: 成功合成了Ir(111)/硼烯/六方氮化硼垂直异质结构，该结构具有微米级晶粒尺寸，并均匀覆盖整个Ir衬底。多种互补表面表征手段（SPA-LEED、LEEM、STM）验证了异质结构的形成与质量。

Conclusion: 该内禀偏析辅助生长（intrinsic segregation-assisted growth）概念为二维材料高质量垂直异质结构的可规模化合成提供了一条有前景的技术路线。

Abstract: We report on a two-step ultrahigh vacuum chemical vapor deposition synthesis of a vertical Ir(111)/borophene/hexagonal boron nitride heterostructure, using borazine as a single-source precursor. The process takes advantage of the finite solubility of boron in Ir: low precursor pressure at high temperature first establishes a boron reservoir in the near-surface region of the substrate, whereas subsequent growth at higher precursor pressure promotes the formation of a closed hexagonal boron nitride monolayer. During cooldown, the reduced boron solubility drives segregation to the surface, resulting in the formation of a borophene monolayer beneath the hexagonal boron nitride overlayer. The heterostructure, with micron sized grains, homogeneously covers the entire Ir substrate. The study is performed by complementary spot profile analysis low-energy electron diffraction, low-energy electron microscopy, and scanning tunneling microscopy measurements. This intrinsic segregation-assisted growth concept provides a promising route toward scalable synthesis of high-quality, vertical heterostructures of two-dimensional materials.

</details>


### [58] [Efficient Quasi-Resonant, Polarization-Selective Excitation of GaN Quantum Emitters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04927)
*Nilesh Dalla,Paweł Kulboka,Michał Kobecki,Jan Misiak,Paweł Prystawko,Tomasz Kazimierczuk,Piotr Kossacki,Henryk Turski,Tomasz Jakubczyk*

TL;DR: 通过将激发激光能量调谐至特定共振值，可显著增强GaN中缺陷单光子光源的光致发光强度（最高可达一个数量级），共振可通过线偏振光选择性激发，表明存在一种基于局域振动模式的准共振激发路径，从而提升光子产生率并揭示能级结构。

Method: 将激发激光能量调谐至特定的共振值（resonance values），并利用线偏振光（linearly polarized light）选择性激发共振，同时观测发射偶极矩（emission dipole）是否保持不变。

Result: 调谐至共振值时，光致发光强度（photoluminescence intensity）相对提升可达一个数量级；共振可被线偏振光选择性寻址，且发射偶极矩保持不变，实现了偏振控制的增强（polarization-controlled enhancement）。

Conclusion: 数据与点缺陷复合体（point-defect complexes）关联的局域振动模式（localized vibrational modes）激发机制一致，建立了一条实用的准共振（quasi-resonant）路径，以实现更明亮、偏振可寻址的GaN缺陷发射器操作，并阐明了其能级结构（energy-level structure）。

Abstract: Defect centers in GaN emerge as bright sources of single-photons which recently have been demonstrated to optically interface a localized spin. However, the structure and composition of these defects as well as their efficient excitation techniques were not a subject of thorough studies. This work presents evidence that by tuning the excitation laser energy to specific resonance values the excitation efficiency can be enhanced, resulting in relative increase of photoluminescence intensity by up to an order of magnitude. The resonances can be selectively addressed with linearly polarized light, while the emission dipole remains unchanged, enabling polarization-controlled enhancement. These results establish an efficient way of excitation for GaN-based emitters, thereby increasing the generation rate of photons. The data is consistent with excitation via localized vibrational modes associated with point-defect complexes, establishing a practical quasi-resonant route to brighter, polarization-addressable operation of GaN defect emitters and clarifying their energy-level structure.

### [59] [From Defects to Devices: Design Guidelines for High-Performance Diamond-Based Solar Cells and Single-Dopant Diodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04942)
*Matúš Kaintz,Antonio Cammarata*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理计算，研究了两种缺陷工程化金刚石光电器件架构（BVB中间带PIN结和PV缺陷PN结），建立了从吸收层厚度、结设计到载流子输运和热管理的关键技术指南，证明两类缺陷掺杂均能保持金刚石优异输运和热特性，为高性能金刚石光电器件提供了实用设计基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金刚石（diamond）具有优异的载流子迁移率和热导率，但如何通过缺陷工程（defect engineering）设计高效光电器件仍缺乏系统性技术指南。本文旨在从第一性原理出发，为两种缺陷架构（BVB-PIN结和PV-PN结）提供切实可行的器件设计准则。

Method: 采用基于GW修正的密度泛函理论（density functional theory with GW corrections）、Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）计算以及耦合泊松求解器（Poisson solver）的载流子输运建模与器件静电学模拟，分别分析BVB中间带PIN结和PV缺陷PN结的光电特性。

Result: 对PIN太阳能电池，提出四项实用设计原则：入射光对准xz平面以利用各向异性吸收、采用梯度结抑制突变界面的隧穿损耗、目标吸收层厚度约500 nm以平衡吸收与载流子提取、利用接触层高透明度实现双面（bifacial）器件配置。对PN二极管，PV掺杂金刚石通过杂质带导电（impurity-band conduction）工作，适用于简并p型应用（如隧道二极管或非对称结），且其温度依赖的塞贝克各向异性（Seebeck anisotropy）与符号反转（sign-reversal）为热管理提供新途径；与磷掺杂n型区结合可实现单掺杂剂结（single-dopant junction），简化器件制造。

Conclusion: BVB缺陷引入中间带而未降低金刚石的高载流子迁移率和热导率，PV掺杂通过杂质带输运在室温下提供高电导率。两种缺陷工程化系统均能在掺杂后保持金刚石卓越的输运和热性能，为高性能金刚石光电器件提供了可行路径。

Abstract: This work establishes key technological guidelines for designing diamond-based optoelectronic devices, derived from a first-principles investigation of two architectures: a PIN junction with a boron-vacancy-boron (BVB) intermediate-band absorber, and a PN junction based on phosphorus-vacancy (PV) defects. For the PIN solar cell, practical design principles include: i) aligning incident light in the xz-plane to exploit anisotropic absorption; ii) using graded junctions to mitigate tunnelling losses at abrupt interfaces; iii) targeting an absorber thickness of ~500 nm to balance absorption and carrier extraction; and iv) leveraging the high transparency of both contact layers for bifacial device configurations. For the PN diode, the PV-doped diamond operates via impurity-band conduction, making it suitable for degenerate p-type applications such as tunnel diodes or asymmetric junctions, while its temperature-dependent Seebeck anisotropy and sign-reversal offer opportunities for thermal management applications. When paired with phosphorus-doped n-type regions, these defects enable single-dopant junctions that significantly simplify device manufacturing. Using density functional theory with GW corrections, Bethe-Salpeter equation calculations and carrier transport modelling coupled to device electrostatics via a Poisson solver, we show that the BVB defect introduces intermediate bands without degrading diamond's high carrier mobility or thermal conductivity, while PV-doping provides high conductivity at room temperature through impurity-band transport. Overall, both defect-engineered systems preserve diamond's superior transport and thermal properties even after doping, offering viable pathways for high-performance diamond optoelectronics. These guidelines provide a practical foundation for fabricating efficient diamond-based photovoltaic and diode devices.

### [60] [Temperature dependence of the Gibbs energies of formation of point defects in B2 MoTa from ab initio calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04969)
*Xiang Xu,Fritz Körmann,Sergiy Divinski,Blazej Grabowski,Xi Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文以B2 MoTa为模型体系，通过从头算（ab initio）计算获得了3000 K以下化学计量比下空位和反位点缺陷的形成吉布斯自由能（Gibbs energy）随温度的变化，发现了空位形成吉布斯自由能随温度下降呈现显著亚晶格不对称性，并揭示了其准谐波与非谐振动两种不同起源的贡献机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解高温下B2型有序金属间化合物中点缺陷热力学性质的温度依赖性，特别是亚晶格不对称性对空位形成吉布斯自由能的影响。

Method: 以V/VI族难熔二元金属中最强B2型有序结构形成体B2 MoTa为模型，在化学计量比组成下，基于从头算（ab initio）方法计算了0至3000 K范围内空位和反位（antisite）缺陷的形成吉布斯自由能（Gibbs energy of formation），并显式考虑了热电子激发（thermal electronic excitations）、振动非谐性（vibrational anharmonicity）以及电子-振动耦合（electron-vibration coupling）。

Result: Mo位空位的形成吉布斯自由能从0 K到3000 K下降了1.1 eV，而Ta位空位下降了2.1 eV，相差近两倍。反位缺陷的形成吉布斯自由能随温度变化很弱。空位形成吉布斯自由能的温度依赖性具有两种不同起源：准谐波贡献源于两种反位结构所决定的化学势不平衡，非谐波贡献则源于空位结构的局域振动响应；其中Ta位空位的非谐振动不对称性可归因于其第一近邻原子具有更大的局域振动分布。

Conclusion: B2 MoTa中空位形成吉布斯自由能的亚晶格不对称性随温度显著增强，这是由准谐波和非谐波两种机制的共同作用导致的，而反位缺陷对温度的敏感性则远低于空位。

Abstract: Using B2 MoTa, the strongest B2 former among group V/VI refractory binaries, as a model system, we compute temperature-dependent Gibbs energies of formation of vacancies and antisites from ab initio calculations up to 3000 K at the stoichiometric composition. We explicitly account for thermal electronic excitations, vibrational anharmonicity, and electron-vibration coupling. The key finding is that the temperature dependence of the Gibbs energies of vacancy formation exhibits a pronounced sublattice asymmetry. Specifically, the Gibbs energy of formation of a Mo-site vacancy decreases by 1.1 eV from 0 to 3000 K, whereas the decrease for a Ta-site vacancy amounts to 2.1 eV, almost a factor of two larger. Two contributions of distinct origin govern the temperature dependence of this asymmetry: a quasiharmonic contribution associated with the chemical-potential imbalance set by the two antisite structures and an anharmonic contribution associated with the local vibrational response of the vacancy structures. The asymmetry in anharmonic vibrations is traced back to an enlarged local vibrational distribution of the first-nearest neighbors around the Ta-site vacancy. In contrast to the vacancies, the Gibbs energies of antisite formation vary only weakly with temperature.

</details>


### [61] [Uncovering hidden bias in neutron diffraction residual strain measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05006)
*Cole Franz,Michael B. Prime,Jeffrey Bunn,Andrew Payzant,Katharine Page*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过实验对比不同应变应力计算路径，证明中子或X射线衍射测量残余应变时，由峰拟合传播的不确定度往往不足以描述真实测量散差，建议采用过采样（oversampling）与统计分析方法获得更准确且符合实际的不确定度区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 衍射测量残余应变时，峰拟合传播的不确定度往往无法真实反映测量值的散差，因为衍射是一种选择性过程，微观结构和应变梯度会导致方向依赖的散差。本文旨在检验传播不确定度是否符合其原始意图（即均值附近的噪声）并探索更合适的估计方法。

Method: 在增材搅拌摩擦沉积（additive friction-stir deposition）构件的多个位置测量36个独立取向的应变，并比较三种应变应力计算路径：将三个测量值直接代入胡克定律（Hooke's law）、任意六个独立取向直接反演为应变状态张量（strain state tensor），以及36个测量值的最小二乘估计（least-squares estimation）。后两种路径基于应变变换律（strain transformation law）的物理约束对不确定度区间进行统计评估。

Result: 六个测量值的直接反演保留了保守的不确定度估计，但最小二乘解中传播的不确定度严重低估了真实实验散差。样本内存在细尺度梯度（约200微米）的塑性应变、织构和残余弹性应变。

Conclusion: 残余应变中不确定度的解释强烈依赖于样本内在效应，通过过采样取向并进行统计分析可以获得更精确的结果和符合实际的不确定度。

Abstract: When calculating residual strain via neutron or X-ray diffraction, uncertainties propagated from the peak fit are often inadequate to describe the true scatter of measurements about a singular strain state, such as one that should describe a macroscopic continuum. Because diffraction is inherently a selective process, orientation dependent scatter arises from the sub-sampling of strong microstructure and strain gradients. This paper investigates the appropriateness of propagated uncertainties with reference to their original intention, i.e., noise about a mean value. Thirty-six unique orientations of strain measurements are taken at multiple locations within an additive friction-stir deposition component with fine-scale gradients (~200 um) of plastic strain, texture, and residual elastic strain. Multiple strain and stress calculation pathways are compared: direct substitution of three measurements into Hooke's law, direct inversion of any six unique orientations into the strain state tensor, and thirty-six measurement least-squares estimation. For the latter two cases, the appropriateness of the uncertainty interval is statistically evaluated based on a physical constraint: common agreement under the strain transformation law. For this sample, the direct inversion of six measurements retains a conservative estimate of the uncertainty. However, propagated uncertainties in the least-squares solution greatly underestimate the true experimental scatter. A simple pathway to estimate appropriate uncertainty intervals is suggested. These results demonstrate that interpretation of uncertainty in residual strain is strongly dependent on intrinsic, sample-dependent effects, and that oversampling orientations and statistical analysis can give more accurate results with realistic uncertainties.

</details>


### [62] [Building informative materials datasets beyond targeted objectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05104)
*Rafael Espinosa Castañeda,Ashley Dale,Hongchen Wang,Yonatan Kurniawan,Hao Wan,Runze Zhang,Adji Bousso Dieng,Kangming Li,Jason Hattrick-Simpers*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种多样性感知（diversity-aware）数据集构建框架，在注重目标属性（target properties）信息量的同时，保持对非目标属性（untargeted properties）的预测性能，从而提升材料科学数据集的可复用性和长期效用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料科学数据采集成本高昂，但实际研究中常因关注特定属性而忽略其他属性，导致生成的数据集在后续学习任务（learning tasks）中信息不足、适用性差，限制了数据的复用与长期价值。

Method: 采用多样性感知选择（diversity-aware selection）策略构建材料数据集，在保证对目标属性信息量最大化的同时，维持对非目标属性的预测性能，通过扩大材料空间（materials space）的覆盖率实现这一平衡。

Result: 在含噪声的实验数据集构建中，若不使用该框架，非目标属性的预测性能相比随机采样（random sampling）最多下降40%；使用该框架后，非目标属性性能提升可达10%。对于目标属性，未引入多样性时性能最多下降12.5%，而应用框架后性能提升可达25%。

Conclusion: 多样性感知的数据集构建不仅能保留目标属性的信息量，还能提升对材料空间的覆盖率，使所构建数据集在已考虑和未考虑属性上均保持广泛信息量，从而保障数据条目质量并缓解后续建模与发现任务中的冷启动（cold-start）问题。

Abstract: Materials science data collection can be expensive, making the reuse and long-term utility of datasets critical important for future discovery campaigns. In practice, researchers prioritize a subset of properties due to research interests. However, ignoring a subset of outcomes in data collection campaigns potentially generate datasets poorly suited for future learning tasks. Here, we present a framework for dataset construction that maximizes informativeness for target properties of interest while preserving performance on untargeted ones. Our approach uses diversity-aware selection to ensure broad coverage of the materials space. In noisy experimental dataset construction, we find that without our diversity-aware framework, prediction performance on untargeted properties can degrade by up to 40% relative to random sampling, whereas applying our framework yields improvements of up to 10% . For targeted properties, performance can degrade with respect to random sampling by up to 12.5% without diversity, while our framework achieves gains of up to 25%. Incorporating diversity into dataset construction not only preserves informativeness for the targeted properties, but also improves materials coverage for potential future objectives. As a result, the constructed datasets remain broadly informative across considered and unconsidered outcomes, ensuring unbiased quality entries and mitigating cold-start limitations in subsequent modeling and discovery campaigns.

</details>

### [63] [Gravitational wave emission from nonspherical collapse in an early matter-dominated era using N-body simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04487)
*Albert Escrivà,Tomohiro Harada,Kazunori Kohri,Takahiro Terada,Chul-Moon Yoo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用自研的半相对论性N体框架，研究了早期物质主导时期非球形过密区域坍缩的动力学及其引力波产生。结果表明，非线性坍缩的后壳层交叉阶段需全数值处理，而拟合或Zel'dovich方法会错误估计引力波信号；不同随机分布（Doroshkevich与BBKS峰值理论）下的频谱形状相似、量级一致，但BBKS结果系统性偏小；主要贡献来自中等高度峰值（ν≈3），且信号可覆盖从脉冲星计时阵列到极高频率实验的广泛频段，为原初黑洞形成前的热历史提供探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非球形过密区域在早期物质主导时期的坍缩过程及其产生的引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）信号尚未得到可靠的理论预测，现有拟合或半解析方法无法准确描述后壳层交叉（post-shell-crossing）阶段的非线性演化。

Method: 开发了一个半相对论性N体框架（semirelativistic N-body framework），通过Zel'dovich形变初始化均匀球体，在爱因斯坦-德西特（Einstein–de Sitter）背景下演化，并从数值四极矩演化直接计算引力波信号。

Result: 全数值处理是可靠预测信号的前提；Zel'dovich估计和拟合方法会高估或低估引力波功率。Doroshkevich与BBKS分布下的频谱形状相似、峰值幅度量级一致，但BBKS结果系统性偏小；主导贡献来自峰值高度ν≈3的中等峰；较大方差显著增强信号。改变视界质量与再加热温度后，信号可覆盖脉冲星计时阵列到极高频率实验的灵敏区间。

Conclusion: 非球形坍缩产生的引力波能够探测到原初核合成（BBN）之前的热历史，为早期宇宙的物理过程提供新的观测窗口。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of the collapse of a nonspherical overdense patch during an early matter-dominated era and the associated production of gravitational waves (GWs) using a semirelativistic N-body framework that we develop. The collapsing patch is initialized through a Zel'dovich deformation of a homogeneous sphere and evolved in an Einstein--de Sitter background, while the emitted signal is computed directly from the numerical quadrupole evolution. We show that a reliable prediction of the signal requires a fully numerical treatment of the nonlinear collapse dynamics. In particular, fitting-based procedures and Zel'dovich-based estimates fail to capture the post-shell-crossing evolution and can over/under-estimate the emitted power of the GWs. After averaging over realizations weighted by the Doroshkevich and BBKS (peak theory) distributions, we find that the two spectra have similar shapes and remain within the same overall order of magnitude at the peak amplitude, although the BBKS result is systematically smaller. The dominant contribution arises from peaks of relatively modest height, around $ν\simeq 3$, while a larger variance significantly enhances the signal. Finally, by varying the horizon mass and reheating temperature, we map the present-day GW spectra to the sensitivity bands of different classes of detectors. In this way, the signal can populate a broad range of frequencies, from pulsar timing arrays to very high-frequency experiments, showing that GWs from nonspherical collapse can provide a probe of the pre-BBN thermal history.

</details>


### [64] [Neutrino Flavor Transformation in Collapsing Supermassive Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04360)
*Kyle S. Kehrer,George M. Fuller,Ian Padilla-Gay,Chad T. Kishimoto*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文研究超大质量恒星（supermassive stars）坍缩成黑洞过程中产生的中微子（neutrino）通量特征及其风味振荡（flavor oscillation）效应，发现MSW共振（Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein resonance）会在不同质量层级下交换不同风味的中微子通量，进而影响能量沉积和核合成过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超大质量恒星（supermassive stars, SMSs）坍缩成黑洞时会产生大量中微子，理解这些中微子的通量特征和风味振荡行为，对于探测此类极端天文事件、评估中微子能量沉积及其引发的外层核合成（nucleosynthesis）具有重要意义。

Method: 论文基于辐射主导的超大质量坍缩构型中的中微子热产生机制（热产生源于正负电子湮灭，即e⁺e⁻→νν̄），分析不同风味中微子通量比值（νₑ-ν̄ₑ对与ν_μ-ν̄_μ/ν_τ-ν̄_τ对的比值约为5:1）；利用密度分布与中微子能量，确定大气中微子质量劈裂尺度（Δm²_atm. ~ 2.4×10⁻³ eV²）对应的MSW共振条件；分别分析正常质量层级（normal mass hierarchy）和倒转质量层级（inverted mass hierarchy）下共振引起的绝热风味转换（adiabatic flavor transformation），并考察集体中微子振荡（collective neutrino oscillations）的可能性。

Result: 在正常质量层级下，MSW共振将交换νₑ与ν_{μ,τ}的通量；在倒转质量层级下，则交换反中微子通量ν̄ₑ与ν̄_{μ,τ}。这些风味振荡会改变中微子在SMS外层中的能量沉积模式以及中微子诱导的核合成过程。此外，论文还探讨了通过多种手段探测超大质量恒星坍缩的可行性。

Conclusion: 超大质量恒星坍缩产生的中微子通量呈现显著的风味比值特征（5:1），且其能量与密度分布使得MSW共振在内部发生，导致风味通量在正常/倒转质量层级下以不同方式交换。这一效应直接影响中微子能量沉积与核合成，并可能为探测此类坍缩事件提供新途径。

Abstract: The collapse of supermassive stars (SMSs, $M\gtrsim10^4\,M_\odot$) to black holes is accompanied by a prodigious flux of neutrinos of all flavors. These are produced thermally via $e^\pm$ annihilations, mostly in the core and just before gravitational trapped surface formation. There, the ratio of fluxes for $ν_e\barν_e$-pairs to $ν_μ\barν_μ/ν_τ\barν_τ$-pairs is $\sim$\,5-to-1. This is because at SMS temperature scales, $ν_e\barν_e$ pairs have both charged and neutral current production channels, whereas $ν_μ\barν_μ/ν_τ\barν_τ$-pairs only have neutral current production channels. We point out that the typical energies of these neutrinos, and the run of density in collapsing radiation-dominated supermassive configurations, leads to Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein (MSW) resonances inside these objects for the atmospheric neutrino mass splitting scale, $Δm^2_\mathrm{atm.}\sim2.4\times10^{-3}$ eV$^2$. In the normal neutrino mass hierarchy, adiabatic flavor transformation through the MSW resonances would then swap the fluxes $ν_e\leftrightharpoonsν_{μ,τ}$, whereas, in the inverted neutrino mass hierarchy, the anti-neutrino fluxes are swapped, $\barν_e\leftrightharpoons\barν_{μ,τ}$. We also examine the prospects for collective neutrino flavor oscillations in these environments. Implications for flavor oscillation's effects on neutrino energy deposition and neutrino-induced nucleosynthesis in the SMS's outer layers are examined, as are prospects for detections of SMS collapses through various means.

</details>


### [65] [Primordial black holes from inflation: on the decoupling between large and small scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04815)
*Laura Iacconi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于分离宇宙框架（separate-universe framework）及其多点传播子扩展，论证单场暴胀（single-field inflation）中产生的原初黑洞（PBH）对宇宙微波背景（CMB）大尺度统计不会造成可观测的反向反应（back-reaction），1-loop反向反应来源于非线性超视界演化或修正的初始条件，但在尺度分离和长模绝热性假设下不可观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单场暴胀模型中产生原初黑洞需要原初曲率功率谱（primordial curvature power spectrum）在短尺度上显著增强，但大尺度模（受CMB观测严格约束）可能对这些短尺度放大扰动产生反向反应，该效应在1-loop阶首次出现。本文旨在澄清该反向反应是否可观测，从而评估单场暴胀产生PBH的可行性是否受大尺度预测干扰。

Method: 采用分离宇宙框架及其推广形式——多点传播子（multi-point propagators）——对长模功率谱进行微扰展开（perturbative expansion），在1-loop阶分析反向反应的来源。通过假设尺度分离（separation of scales）和长模绝热性（adiabaticity of the long mode），检验该效应是否可观测。

Result: 1-loop反向反应源于两类机制：（i）非线性超视界演化（non-linear super-horizon evolution），或（ii）1-loop修正的初始条件。在尺度分离和长模绝热性假设下，该反向反应不可观测，大尺度模与增强的短尺度模退耦（decouple）。

Conclusion: 单场暴胀中的PBH产生不会破坏大尺度可观测量的预测；但该结论不适用于那些不满足尺度分离或长模绝热性假设的场景。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) can be produced from inflation if the primordial curvature power spectrum is strongly enhanced on scales much shorter than those probed by cosmic microwave background (CMB) experiments. In single-field models this typically requires a transient departure from slow-roll, attractor dynamics, for example realized through a brief ultra-slow-roll phase. In these scenarios, there is reasonable concern that large-scale modes, whose statistics is tightly constrained by CMB observations, might back-react to the amplified perturbations on much shorter scales. In a perturbative expansion for the long-mode power spectrum, this effect first appears at 1-loop. In these proceedings we summarize recent works on this issue, based on the application of the separate-universe framework and its general extension with multi-point propagators. We show that back-reaction at 1-loop is due to either (i) non-linear super-horizon evolution, or (ii) 1-loop-corrected initial conditions. By assuming separation of scales and adiabaticity of the long mode, we show that the 1-loop back-reaction is not observable and large scales decouple from enhanced short ones. While we demonstrate that PBH production within single-field inflation does not disrupt large-scale predictions, we close by discussing scenarios to which our results do not apply.

</details>

Method: 采用具有指数势$V_0 e^{-λφ/m_{\mathrm{pl}}}$的第五元素模型，通过解析方法推导当前态方程参数$w_\phi$与势参数$λ$之间的关系，并引入辐射主导（radiation domination）和物质主导（matter domination）时期的足够持续时间作为约束条件。

Result: 得到了从当前观测的态方程参数反推势参数$λ$的解析关系；进一步给出了当前宇宙加速膨胀（accelerated expansion）条件下势参数$λ$的解析上限，具体数值结果为$λ<1.94$（取当前第五元素密度参数$Ω_{\phi0}=0.685$）。

We derive an analytical relationship between the current equation of state parameter for the quintessence field and the potential parameter $λ$ required to realize sufficient duration of radiation and matter domination. Our results provide a useful analytical relation for inferring the potential parameter $λ$ from the observed current equation of state parameter. Furthermore, based on this framework, we provide a new analytical upper bound on the potential parameter $λ$ for current accelerated expansion. Concretely, we obtain $λ<1.94$ by adopting $Ω_{\phi0}=0.685$.

### [67] [Are PTA measurements sensitive to gravitational wave non-Gaussianities?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05157)
*Chiara Cecchini,Jonas El Gammal,Gabriele Franciolini,Mauro Pieroni*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明，在脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）的引力波背景探测中，即使在理想化的信号主导场景下，经过数据去相关处理后，传统的统计检验方法无法以模型无关的方式区分高斯与非高斯的引力波背景信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者分析了理想化的信号主导（signal-dominated）设定，在数据去相关（decorrelating）以避免虚假探测之后，运用统计检验方法评估PTA数据对高斯与非高斯引力波背景（Gravitational Wave Background, GWB）的区分能力。

Result: 研究发现，统计检验无法以模型无关（model-agnostic）的方式区分高斯与非高斯的引力波背景；对任何独特的非高斯特征的灵敏度都会被抹除（washed out）。

Conclusion: 在没有对引力波谱（GW spectrum）或源群（population）性质做出强假设的前提下，基于非高斯性来区分引力波背景的起源是不可靠的。

Abstract: Observing non-Gaussianity in the timing residuals of Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs) has recently attracted attention as a potential discriminator between astrophysical and cosmological origins of the observed Gravitational Wave (GW) signal. In this work, we show that even in an idealized signal-dominated setup, after decorrelating data to avoid spurious detections, statistical tests applied to PTA data cannot distinguish between Gaussian and non-Gaussian GWBs in a model-agnostic way. In particular, without making strong assumptions on the GW spectrum or the properties of the population, the sensitivity to any distinctive non-Gaussian feature is washed out.

### [69] [Topological subsystem bivariate bicycle codes with four-qubit check operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04151)
*Zijian Liang,Yu-An Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出子空间双变量循环（subsystem bivariate bicycle, SBB）码，通过局域权重为4的规范测量（gauge measurement）实现高码率双变量循环（bivariate bicycle, BB）码的逻辑结构，解决了BB码因稳定子校验权重较高（≥6）导致的综合征提取困难问题。SBB码在保持拓扑性的前提下，可编码比相同块长和距离的子空间表面码（subsystem surface code）多六倍的逻辑量子比特。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高码率双变量循环（bivariate bicycle, BB）码是前景良好的低开销量子存储器，但其稳定子校验（stabilizer check）权重通常为6或更高，导致综合征提取（syndrome extraction）困难。本文旨在设计一种能够保留BB码逻辑结构，同时使用更低权重局域测量实现综合征提取的量子纠错码构造。

Method: 引入子空间双变量循环（subsystem bivariate bicycle, SBB）码，这是一种平移不变的CSS子空间（CSS subsystem）构造，通过局域权重为4的规范测量（gauge measurement）实现BB码的逻辑结构；稳定子综合征通过对应规范测量结果的乘积推断得到。提出基于规范算子对易矩阵（gauge-operator commutation matrix）的行列式理想判据（determinantal-ideal criterion），用于检测平移不变CSS子空间码中的非局域稳定子。当该判据排除非局域稳定子时，可通过有限深度克利福德电路（finite-depth Clifford circuit）解耦规范量子比特，将受保护子空间识别为对应的BB稳定子码。

Result: 一个SBB码是拓扑的（即不存在非平凡局域逻辑算子）当且仅当对应的BB码是拓扑的。有限搜索找到了低开销示例，包括[[27,6,3]]、[[75,10,5]]和[[108,12,6]]码；其中[[108,12,6]]码在相同块长和距离下，编码的逻辑量子比特数是子空间表面码（subsystem surface code）的六倍。

Conclusion: 规范自由度（gauge degrees of freedom）可以使高码率BB逻辑结构与局域权重为4的综合征提取兼容，为低开销量子存储器的实现提供了新的构造途径。

Abstract: High-rate bivariate bicycle (BB) codes are promising low-overhead quantum memories, but their stabilizer checks typically have weight $6$ or higher, making syndrome extraction challenging. We introduce subsystem bivariate bicycle (SBB) codes, a translation-invariant CSS subsystem construction that realizes BB-code logical structure using local weight-$4$ gauge measurements. Their stabilizer syndromes are inferred by multiplying the corresponding gauge outcomes. We further show that nonlocal stabilizers in translation-invariant CSS subsystem codes can be detected using a determinantal-ideal criterion based on the gauge-operator commutation matrix. When this criterion excludes nonlocal stabilizers, a finite-depth Clifford circuit decouples gauge qubits and identifies the protected subsystem with a corresponding BB stabilizer code. An SBB code is topological, meaning that it has no nontrivial local logical operators, if and only if the corresponding BB code is topological. A finite search yields low-overhead examples including $[[27,6,3]]$, $[[75,10,5]]$, and $[[108,12,6]]$; the latter encodes six times more logical qubits than a subsystem surface code at the same block length and distance. These results show how gauge degrees of freedom can make high-rate BB logical structure compatible with local weight-$4$ syndrome extraction.

### [70] [Two-site Bose-Hubbard hopping and Schrödinger cat states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04598)
*Madeline Berezowski,Artur Sowa,Jonas Fransson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 通过玻色-哈伯德二聚体模型（Bose-Hubbard dimer）的跳跃项哈密顿量，利用玻色子正则对易关系（bosonic canonical commutation relations）的归纳论证，求解了k粒子子空间中的本征值和本征向量，揭示了该哈密顿量与x轴自旋投影算子（spin projection operator along the x-axis）的等价性，并发现其平方可产生薛定谔猫态（Schrödinger cat states）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 简化Bose-Hubbard模型至双格点（dimer）情形，其跳跃项哈密顿量在k粒子子空间中具有不变性，需要一种系统的方法来求解该子空间的本征问题。

Method: 发明了一种基于玻色子正则对易关系的归纳论证（inductive argument），用于求解二聚体跳跃哈密顿量在k粒子子空间中的本征值和本征向量。

Result: 该哈密顿量在k粒子子空间中的投影等价于自旋量子数s=k/2的x轴自旋投影算子（spin projection operator along the x-axis）；利用显式构造研究了二聚体跳跃哈密顿量平方诱导的相干态（coherent states）动力学，发现其可在双格点系统中生成薛定谔猫态。

Conclusion: 建立了一种计算x轴自旋投影算子本征值和本征向量的新方法，并揭示了二聚体跳跃哈密顿量平方在量子纠缠态生成中的应用价值。

Abstract: The Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonian can be simplified to have only two lattice sites, in which case the system being described is referred to as a dimer. Due to its structure, the hopping term of the dimer Hamiltonian enjoys invariance in a family of subspaces indexed by a whole number $k$, each subspace corresponding to a system of only $k$ particles. We have invented an inductive argument using the bosonic canonical commutation relations to find the eigenvalues and eigenvectors of the dimer hopping Hamiltonian in its $k$-particle subspaces. In particular, this Hamiltonian, when restricted to one of the $k$-particle subspaces, is exactly the spin projection operator along the $x$-axis, where the number of particles $k$ in the dimer system yields the projection matrix for spin quantum number $s=k/2$. Thus, a new method for computing the eigenvalues and eigenvectors of the $x$-axis spin projector has been unearthed. We use the explicit construction to study the dynamics of coherent states induced by the square of the dimer hopping hamiltonian. We find that it generates Schrödinger cat states in the two-site setting.

### [71] [Exact SU(2) Yang-Mills Waves from a Simple Ansatz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04964)
*Yu-Xuan Zhang,Jing-Ling Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种简单ansatz，用于构造(3+1)维无源SU(2)杨-米尔斯方程的精确波动解。通过将非线性场方程简化为九个代数约束，得到三个解族：嵌入非阿贝尔理论的线性电磁波（族I）、具有自相互作用且以光速传播的非线性波（族II），以及纯规范解（族III）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非阿贝尔规范场论（non-Abelian gauge theory）中波动解的精确形式，揭示非线性自相互作用（self-interaction）如何从根本上改变波传播行为。

Method: 采用依赖于y方向的旋转泡利基（rotated Pauli basis）并假设规范势具有相位θ=kz-ωt依赖形式，将非线性杨-米尔斯场方程简化为九个代数约束，通过完整求解这些约束得到三类精确波解。

Result: 族I描述嵌入非阿贝尔理论的线性电磁波，对易子项为零，色散关系为ω=kc；族II描述以光速传播的非线性自相互作用波，具有常数场偏移、非零对易子，不满足叠加原理，其能量密度节点位置由离散拓扑参数ξη=±1控制；族III为纯规范解，对任意k和ω均成立。

Conclusion: 所有解均为闭式解（closed-form），为理解非阿贝尔自相互作用如何从根本上改变波传播提供了新见解，其中常数偏移是规范不变的，可产生非零时间平均色电场。

Abstract: We propose a simple ansatz to construct exact wave solutions of the sourceless SU(2) Yang-Mills equations in (3+1) dimensions. The ansatz employs a $y$-dependent rotated Pauli basis and assumes a phase $θ=kz-ωt$ dependence for the gauge potentials. Owing to this ansatz, the nonlinear field equations reduce to nine algebraic constraints, whose complete solution yields three families of exact waves. Family I describes linear (Abelian) electromagnetic waves embedded in the non-Abelian theory; all commutator terms vanish and the dispersion relation is $ω=kc$. Family II represents genuinely nonlinear self-interacting waves that also propagate at the speed of light but exhibit a constant field offset, nonvanishing commutators, and do not obey superposition. The constant offset is gauge-invariant and gives rise to a non-zero time-averaged color-electric field. The energy density has nodes whose position ($θ=0$ or $θ=π$) is controlled by a discrete topological parameter $ξη=\pm1$, providing an observable signature. Family III is a pure gauge solution with vanishing field strengths, valid for arbitrary $k$ and $ω$ without any dispersion relation. All solutions are closed-form and provide new insights into how non-Abelian self-interactions fundamentally alter wave propagation.

### [72] [Time-resolved digital quantum simulation of cosmological particle creation in a de Sitter-radiation transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04099)
*Hamzeh Alavirad*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过时间分辨的数字量子模拟，对德西特-辐射FLRW宇宙相变中的宇宙学粒子产生进行了研究。采用Trotter化时序电路而非一次性Bogoliubov变换，在四量子比特单激发编码下，对比了矩阵Trotter演化、无噪声态矢量模拟、有限采样Qiskit Aer模拟及IBM硬件实验，结果与解析突变基准吻合，但当前NISQ硬件误差仍限制定量重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将共形时间演化离散化，实现为Trotter化短时电路块序列（Trotterized sequence of short-time circuit blocks）。采用四量子比特单激发编码（single-excitation encoding）表示动量对$(+\mathbf{k},-\mathbf{k})$。对比了四种实现方式：矩阵Trotter演化、无噪声态矢量模拟（statevector simulation）、有限采样Qiskit Aer模拟以及浅层$N=1$的IBM硬件实现。

Result: 在受控单激发区间（controlled single-excitation regime）内，所有模拟器结果均与解析突变基准（analytic sudden-transition benchmark）$n_k=1/[4(k\eta_e)^4]$一致。IBM硬件实验成功执行了浅层电路块，但残留硬件误差约为$10^{-2}$量级。

Conclusion: 时间分辨的数字量子模拟可以超越单次电路的限制，提供对宇宙学粒子产生动力学的更完整描述。然而，定量重建粒子谱（particle spectrum）仍超出当前NISQ（Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum）硬件的性能范围。

Abstract: We present a time-resolved digital quantum simulation of cosmological particle creation in a de~Sitter--radiation FLRW transition. Instead of compiling only the final Bogoliubov transformation into a one-shot circuit, we discretize the conformal-time evolution and implement the dynamics as a Trotterized sequence of short-time circuit blocks. This formulation gives access not only to the late-time particle number, but also to the build-up of fixed-basis pair occupation during the non-adiabatic transition. Using a four-qubit single-excitation encoding for a momentum pair $(+\mathbf{k},-\mathbf{k})$, we compare matrix-Trotter evolution, noiseless statevector simulation, finite-shot Qiskit Aer simulation, and a shallow $N=1$ IBM hardware implementation. The simulator results are consistent with the analytic sudden-transition benchmark $n_k=1/[4(kη_e)^4]$ in the controlled single-excitation regime. The IBM experiment demonstrates execution of the shallow circuit block, but exhibits a residual hardware error of order $10^{-2}$, indicating that quantitative hardware reconstruction of the particle spectrum remains beyond current NISQ performance.
