### [73] [Tunneling from an oscillating initial state in quantum mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04139)
*Oliver Janssen,Matthew Kleban,Cameron Norton*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文研究量子力学中亚稳态势阱（metastable potential well）中一般初始态的衰变，给出了隧穿概率流的闭式表达式，在半经典极限（semiclassical limit）下解析计算到第一子主导阶，并以相干振荡初始态为例推导了含时衰变率近似，通过与薛定谔方程数值解对比验证了其准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚稳态势阱中的量子隧穿衰变是量子力学的基本问题，现有研究多局限于特定初始态。本文旨在建立适用于一般初始态的、基于共振态（resonant states）分解的闭式衰变描述，并量化半经典极限下的子主导阶修正。

Method: 将初始态在共振态基下展开，推导概率流（probability current）的闭式表达式；所有计算量在半经典极限下解析计算到第一子主导阶。针对相干振荡初始态（coherently-oscillating initial state），进一步推导含时衰变率的近似公式，并与薛定谔方程数值解进行对比验证。

Result: 得到了以共振态表示的概率流闭式表达式，其中所有成分在半经典极限下均解析计算至第一子主导阶。相干振荡初始态下的含时衰变率近似与薛定谔方程数值解吻合良好。

Conclusion: 所建立的共振态分解框架能够统一描述亚稳态势阱中一般初始态的量子隧穿衰变，半经典子主导阶解析计算具有足够精度，为含时衰变过程的解析研究提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: We study the decay of general initial states out of a metastable potential well in quantum mechanics. We provide a closed-form expression for the probability current that tunnels through the barrier in terms of the resonant states into which the initial state can be decomposed. All ingredients in the equation are computed analytically to first subleading order in the semiclassical limit. Specializing to a coherently-oscillating initial state, we derive an approximation to the time-dependent decay rate and demonstrate its accuracy by comparing it to a numerical solution of the Schrödinger equation.

</details>


### [74] [Hierarchical entanglement transitions and hidden area-law sectors in quantum many-body dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04540)
*Tarun Grover*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了局域量子淬火（local quantum quenches）中一种复杂的分层纠缠结构（hierarchical entanglement structure）：完整态呈现Rényi指标调谐的相变（Rényi-index-tuned transition），且主导Schmidt扇区（dominant Schmidt sector）内部存在自身的面积-体积律转变，该分层结构可递归持续，并在电路模型中得到解析推导和数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌多体动力学通常从低纠缠初态产生体积律纠缠（volume-law entanglement）。本文旨在探索局域量子淬火这一特定设置中是否隐藏着比简单体积律更精细、分层的纠缠结构，并理解其机制。

Method: 研究了两类系统：局域淬火吉布斯态（locally quenched Gibbs states）的规范纯化（canonical purification）及其伴随的纯态电路模型（pure-state circuit model）。运用解析推导证明面积律，并通过随机电路和混沌自旋链的局域淬火吉布斯态的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）提供数值支持。

Result: 完整态存在Rényi指标调谐的相变：长时间下，$S_{α>1}$ 满足面积律（area law），$S_{α\le 1}$ 满足体积律（volume law）。淬火强度的线性响应仅由O(1)维度的主导Schmidt扇区承载；该扇区内部在临界指标 $α_c<1$ 处经历自身的面积-体积律转变。该分层结构可递归重复，在一维下具有多项式键维数可近似性（polynomial-bond-dimension approximability）。

Conclusion: 局域量子淬火中的纠缠结构并非简单的体积律，而是具有递归、分层性质。该结构可通过电路模型解析推导，并在混沌自旋链中通过数值方法得到验证。这一发现对理解多体量子系统的纠缠结构和张量网络近似具有启示意义。

Abstract: Chaotic many-body dynamics typically generates volume-law entanglement from initially low-entangled states. We reveal an intricate, hierarchical entanglement structure in local quantum quenches, both in the canonical purification of locally quenched Gibbs states and in a companion pure-state circuit model. In either setting, the full state exhibits a Renyi-index-tuned transition: at long times, $S_{α>1}$ obeys an area law, while $S_{α\le 1}$ is volume-law. More strikingly, the response linear in the quench strength is carried by only an O(1)-dimensional dominant Schmidt sector; the corresponding states exhibit their own area-to-volume-law transitions at critical indices $α_c<1$, implying polynomial-bond-dimension approximability in one dimension. We provide evidence that this hierarchy persists recursively: upon bipartitioning the dominant Schmidt states, their leading Schmidt sectors exhibit analogous structure. We derive the mechanism analytically in the circuit model, prove the $S_{α>1}$ area law for locally quenched Gibbs states, and support the hierarchy by exact diagonalization of random circuits and locally quenched Gibbs states of chaotic spin chains.

</details>


### [75] [Nonstabilizerness Mpemba Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04155)
*Zhenyu Xiao,Hao-Kai Zhang,Shuo Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在 U(1) 对称性随机量子线路中发现了量子魔法（quantum magic）的 Mpemba 效应：初始魔法更小的态反而能更快地生成魔法，且该效应与守恒荷分布及初态空间结构有关，并在 SU(2) 对称性线路和非可积哈密顿量动力学中同样存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示量子态制备中违反直觉的动力学现象：最快到达目标态的最优路径未必始于最接近的初始条件。

Method: 在 U(1) 对称性随机量子线路中以倾斜乘积态（tilted product state）为初态，利用稳定子雷尼熵（stabilizer Rényi entropy）量化量子魔法（nonstabilizerness），并对比不同初始魔法态的生长动力学。

Result: 初始魔法较低的态生成魔法的速度反而快于初始魔法较高的态；该加速效应不仅由守恒荷分布决定，还同时依赖于初态在每个荷扇区（charge sector）内部的空间结构。

Conclusion: 在 SU(2) 对称性线路和非可积哈密顿量动力学中也观测到类似的魔法 Mpemba 效应，表明该现象既不依赖于阿贝尔对称性（Abelian symmetry），也不局限于随机线路动力学，从而将量子魔法确立为 Mpemba 物理的一个独特领域。

Abstract: Quantum state preparation can be strikingly counterintuitive: the fastest route to a target state need not start from the apparently closest initial condition. We uncover such a quantum Mpemba effect in the dynamical generation of quantum magic (nonstabilizerness), quantified by the stabilizer Rényi entropy, in $\mathrm{U(1)}$-symmetric random circuits initialized from tilted product states. States with lower initial magic can generate magic faster than states with higher initial magic. The acceleration is not determined solely by the conserved-charge distribution. Two initial-state families with identical initial magic and identical charge distribution exhibit qualitatively different magic-growth dynamics, depending also on the spatial structure of the initial state within each charge sector. Analogous magic Mpemba effects in $\mathrm{SU(2)}$-symmetric circuits and under nonintegrable Hamiltonian dynamics further show that the phenomenon is tied neither to Abelian symmetry nor to random-circuit dynamics, establishing quantum magic as a distinct arena for Mpemba physics.

</details>

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究首次将神经量子态（neural quantum states）应用于光-物质耦合系统的耗散动力学模拟，实现了超越精确对角化和张量网络方法的大尺度计算，并对一维和二维密集原子阵列中约40个原子的多体发射动力学进行了模拟，揭示了亚辐射（subradiant）动力学行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用神经量子态作为变分拟设（variational ansatz），首次将其应用于光-物质耦合系统的耗散动力学模拟，克服了精确对角化和张量网络（tensor-network）计算在系统尺寸上的限制。

Result: 成功模拟了约40个原子在一维和二维密集阵列中的多体发射动力学（many-body emission dynamics），该方法能够捕捉后期时间尺度上显著的亚辐射动力学行为。

Conclusion: 神经量子态方法为研究光-物质耦合系统中由结构化耗散（structured dissipation）和长程相互作用（long-range interactions）驱动的新奇现象提供了一种可扩展的数值模拟工具，且该模拟系统可通过冷原子量子模拟器（cold atomic quantum simulators）在实验上实现。

Abstract: There is significant interest in exploring novel phenomena in quantum light-matter interfaces, which are driven by the combination of structured dissipation and long-range interactions that are typical in such systems. To this end, it is important to develop new general numerical simulation techniques, which can access large system sizes and are not based on semi-classical approaches. Here, we report the first application of neural quantum states to obtain the dissipative dynamics of light-matter-coupled systems beyond what is accessible with exact and tensor-network calculations. We specifically apply this method to simulate the many-body emission dynamics of approximately 40 atoms, arranged in dense arrays in one and two dimensions. These systems have been chosen because they can support prominent subradiant dynamics at late times and could be realized with cold atomic quantum simulators.

</details>


### [77] [Finite steps optimise dissipation in stochastically controlled quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04681)
*Theodore McKeever,Harry J. D. Miller,Ahsan Nazir*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了经典随机控制场下量子逐步平衡过程的热力学代价，发现确定性协议耗散随步数反比下降，而弱高斯噪声导致耗散随步数线性增长，并利用量子热力学长度（quantum thermodynamic length）推导出最优步数与最小平均耗散功及其方差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了设计精确、节能且实验可行的量子控制协议，需要理解经典随机控制场对量子逐步平衡过程热力学成本的影响。

Method: 研究对比了确定性协议与受弱高斯噪声（Gaussian noise）干扰的随机控制协议在逐步平衡过程中的耗散行为，并利用量子热力学长度推导出有限最优步数与最小可达平均耗散功及其方差。

Result: 确定性协议的耗散随步数呈反比下降，而控制变量中的弱高斯噪声导致耗散贡献随步数线性增长，从而存在有限的最优步数。

Conclusion: 通过一个与热浴强耦合的量子比特（qubit）的Landau-Zener扫场以及横向伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model）的擦除过程两个范例，验证了上述理论结果。

Abstract: Motivated by the need for precise, energy-efficient, and experimentally realistic quantum control protocols, we investigate the thermodynamic cost of performing quantum step-equilibration processes under the influence of classical stochastic control fields. Whereas purely deterministic protocols exhibit dissipation that scales inversely with the number of steps, we show that weak Gaussian noise in the control variables induces dissipative contributions that grow linearly with the number of steps. Consequently, we derive the finite optimal number of steps and minimal achievable average dissipated work and its variance using the quantum thermodynamic length. These results are demonstrated using two paradigmatic examples: a Landau-Zener sweep of a qubit strongly coupled to a thermal bath and the erasure of a transverse-field Ising model.

</details>

### [78] [Scattering-Induced Loss in Ferroelectric Photonic Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04353)
*Jonah Townsend,Enzo Conceição Picinini,Rogério de Sousa*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种微扰理论（perturbative theory），将非吸收性（弹性）光子散射导致的损耗表达为介电常数空间涨落谱密度的泛函，并应用于平板波导中界面粗糙度（interface roughness）与铁电畴无序（ferroelectric domain disorder）两种损耗机制的对比分析。研究表明，畴的平均长度与光波长可比时损耗最大（Mie区），而对于通信波长，亚微米畴（Rayleigh区）或单畴波导均可有效降低损耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电材料（ferroelectric materials）具有巨大的光学非线性，有望用于量子光子芯片，但其引入的额外损耗机制阻碍了实际集成。因此，有必要建立能够统一描述并定量比较不同非吸收性损耗来源的理论框架，以指导低损耗铁电波导的设计。

Method: 发展了一种微扰理论，将非吸收性（弹性）光子散射损耗表达为介电常数（electric permittivity）空间涨落谱密度（spectral density）的泛函。将该理论应用于平板波导（slab waveguides）中衰减系数（attenuation coefficients α）的计算，用于对比界面粗糙度与铁电畴无序两种损耗机制。该理论无需特殊对称性假设即可处理真实的粗糙度，并展示了如何利用铁电畴的电子显微镜图像获得α的显式数值预测。

Result: 损耗在畴的平均长度与光波长可比时达到最大值（Mie区）；对于通信波长（telecom wavelengths），采用亚微米畴（Rayleigh区）或单畴波导（single domain waveguides）均可实现等效的损耗降低策略。

Conclusion: 所提出的理论能够统一处理铁电波导中两种主要的非吸收性损耗机制，并利用实验图像数据给出具体的数值预测。在通信波长下，亚微米畴或单畴波导均可作为降低损耗的有效设计策略。

Abstract: Ferroelectric materials have colossal optical nonlinearities, but their integration into quantum photonic chips is made challenging by the additional loss mechanisms that they introduce. Here we present a perturbative theory that expresses non-absorptive (elastic) photon scattering-induced loss as a functional of a general spectral density for spatial fluctuations of electric permittivity. We apply the theory to calculations of attenuation coefficients $α$ in slab waveguides in order to compare two distinct loss mechanisms: Interface roughness and ferroelectric domain disorder. our theory can account for realistic roughness without special symmetry considerations, and it demonstrates how to use electron microscoopy images of ferroelectric domains to obtain explicit numerical predictions for $α$. Loss is maximum when the mean domain length is comparable to the wavelength of light (Mie regime), indicating that, for telecom wavelengths, sub-micron domains (Rayleigh regime) or single domain waveguides provide equivalent strategies for reducing loss.

</details>


### [79] [Emergence of Localized Surface Plasmons in Unpatterned Hyperdoped Polycrystalline Silicon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04854)
*Mohamad Bahsoun,Jesse Groenen,Gonzague Agez,Sébastien Joulié,Cécile Marcelot,Robin Cours,Sébastien Kerdiles,Mathieu Opprecht,Caroline Bonafos,Jean-Marie Poumirol*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文发现未图案化的多晶硅薄膜（晶粒尺寸5-50 nm）在无需外部纳米结构的情况下，可产生中红外局域表面等离激元共振（LSPR），并证明该现象源于晶界处自然形成的金属-介质界面，且可推广至任意掺杂半导体体系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非平衡退火条件（out-of-equilibrium annealing conditions）制备过掺杂多晶硅（hyperdoped polysilicon）薄膜，结合先进电子显微镜、红外光谱（infrared spectroscopy）和时域有限差分（finite-difference time-domain, FDTD）电动力学模拟，系统表征材料的结构与光学性能。

Result: 过掺杂多晶硅薄膜表现出增强的光-物质相互作用（light-matter interactions），且可在中红外范围内调谐。这些光学特性源于晶界（grain boundaries）处自然形成的金属-介质界面（metal-dielectric interfaces），它们支持局域表面等离激元共振。

Conclusion: 该现象具有普适性，可推广至任意掺杂半导体体系（仅需晶粒尺寸保持在纳米量级）。本研究开创了以多晶半导体为核心的新等离激元学（plasmonics）领域，为实现与微电子和光伏技术完全兼容的低成本红外光-物质相互作用调控系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: The ability to engineer localized surface plasmon resonances at large scale usually relies on precise nanoscale patterning. Here, we demonstrate that mid-infrared plasmonic responses can instead emerge in unpatterned polysilicon films composed of nanometric (5-50 nm) grains, challenging established design paradigms and eliminating the need for external nanostructuring. Using tailored out-of-equilibrium annealing conditions, we show that hyperdoped polysilicon layers exhibit enhanced light-matter interactions that can be tuned across the mid-infrared range. By combining advanced electron microscopy, infrared spectroscopy and finite-difference time-domain electrodynamic simulations, we demonstrate that these remarkable optical properties originate from naturally formed metal-dielectric interfaces at grain boundaries, which support localized surface plasmon resonances. Importantly, this result is universal and can be extended to any doped semiconductor system, regardless of the synthesis technique, provided that the grain size remains in the nanometric range. This work opens up a new field in plasmonics centered on polycrystalline semiconductors, paving the way for cost-effective systems that are fully compatible with microelectronic and photovoltaic technologies, and capable of significantly reshaping light-matter interactions in the infrared range.

</details>


### [80] [Unraveling the Defect Physics of SiC Micropipe Sidewalls by Non-Line-of-Sight Confocal Spectromicroscopy: Amphoteric Giant Traps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04865)
*Irwan Saleh Kurniawan,Russel Cruz Sevilla,Ruth Jeane Soebroto,Hsiu-Ying Huang,Hsiu-Ming Hsu,Ji-Lin Shen,Sheng Hsiung Chang,Wen-Chung Li,Chi-Tsu Yuan*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种非视域共聚焦多次反射光谱显微术（non-line-of-sight confocal multiple-reflection spectromicroscopy），结合直接缺陷光电离技术，揭示了SiC晶圆中微管（micropipe）侧壁的缺陷物理机制。研究发现侧壁存在高密度的施主型和受主型深能级态，产生由本征施主-受主对（DAP）型复合与脱陷介导的自由-束缚跃迁构成的超宽带发射，且DAP型发射在室温及所有激发功率下仍占主导。侧壁缺陷表现为两性巨型陷阱和载流子库，通过陷阱辅助输运促进漏电流。该工作为高纵横比扩展缺陷提供了非破坏性光学探测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微管（micropipes）是SiC晶圆中极具破坏性的缺陷，与器件灾难性失效密切相关，但其内部侧壁的微观缺陷本质及相关的漏电流机制由于高纵横比（high-aspect-ratio）几何结构严重限制直接光学探测而至今尚未明确。

Method: 开发了非视域共聚焦多次反射光谱显微术（non-line-of-sight confocal multiple-reflection spectromicroscopy）结合直接缺陷光电离（direct defect photoionization）技术，以克服高纵横比侧壁的光学探测难题。

Result: 侧壁存在高密度的施主型（donor-like）和受主型（acceptor-like）深能级态（deep-level states），产生由本征DAP型复合（DAP-like recombination）与脱陷介导的自由-束缚跃迁（detrapping-mediated free-to-bound transitions）构成的超宽带发射（ultrabroad emission bands）。DAP型发射在室温及所有激发功率下仍占主导，归因于侧壁缺陷的快速载流子捕获，表现为快上升和纳秒级衰减动力学。侧壁缺陷表现为扩展的两性巨型陷阱（amphoteric giant traps）和载流子库（carrier reservoirs），通过陷阱辅助输运（trap-assisted transport）促进漏电流。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种非破坏性光学方法，可直接探测高纵横比扩展缺陷（high-aspect-ratio extended defects），并揭示了微管侧壁缺陷物理及漏电机制的深层机理。

Abstract: Micropipes are among the most detrimental defects in SiC wafer and are closely linked to catastrophic device failure. However, the microscopic defect nature of their internal sidewalls and the mechanism of the associated leakage current remain poorly understood, because their high-aspect-ratio geometry severely restricts direct optical probing. Here, we develop a non-line-of-sight confocal multiple-reflection spectromicroscopy technique combined with direct defect photoionization to unravel the defect physics of micropipe sidewalls. We show that these sidewalls host a high density of donor-like and acceptor-like deep-level states, giving rise to ultrabroad emission bands composed of intrinsic DAP-like recombination and detrapping-mediated free-to-bound transitions. Unlike conventional defect luminescence, the DAP-like emission remains dominant even at room temperature across all excitation powers. This behavior is attributed to rapid carrier capture by the sidewall defects, as evidenced by fast-rising and nanosecond-scale decay dynamics, along with coupled carrier kinetics. These results suggest that micropipe sidewalls can serve as extended amphoteric giant traps and carrier reservoirs, facilitating leakage current through trap-assisted transport. Our work provides a nondestructive optical approach for directly probing high-aspect-ratio extended defects and offers deep mechanistic insight into their defect physics and leakage mechanisms.

</details>


### [81] [Band-Selective LDOS Engineering of Yb/Er Upconversion: an Electromagnetic-Kinetic Diagnostic Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04872)
*Yuxiang Zhang,Mayte Gómez-Castaño,Agustín Mihi,Serge Ravaine,Xiaogang Liu,Renaud A. L. Vallée*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论框架研究等离激元上转换（plasmonic upconversion）中泵浦波长近场工程与发射波长光学态密度（LDOS）工程之间的耦合问题。实验采用NaYF4:Yb,Er上转换纳米粒子（UCNP）单层涂覆的波纹SU8/Au/Al2O3光栅结构，实现了红/绿波段发射速率的选择性调控；理论方面建立耦合电磁-动力学框架，定量解释了实验结果并诊断出绿带偏差需要超越半椭圆模型的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等离激元上转换中的一个核心挑战在于泵浦波长的近场工程（near-field engineering）与发射波长的局域光学态密度（local-density-of-optical-states, LDOS）工程之间存在耦合，难以单独调控发射端。现有研究往往难以干净地分离泵浦端和发射端的影响，从而无法准确理解LDOS调控对发射动力学的独立作用。

Method: 实验上制备了波纹SU8/Au/Al2O3光栅结构，涂覆密排NaYF4:Yb(20%),Er(5%)上转换纳米粒子单层膜；通过改变Al2O3间隔层厚度d（5–25 nm）和调节光栅结构的脊尖圆滑程度（h_round = 0, 5, 10 nm），测量不同发射波长的衰减速率变化。理论上建立了耦合电磁-动力学框架（coupled electromagnetic-kinetic framework），结合全波时域有限差分（FDTD）泵浦增强计算、取向平均Purcell因子（orientation-averaged Purcell factors）以及六能级Yb/Er速率方程模型（six-level rate-equation model），区分辐射、本征非辐射和环境诱导非辐射通道。

Result: 实验结果显示：与Er³⁺红色跃迁（4F₉/₂→4I₁₅/₂，约670 nm）对齐的宽等离激元共振（broad plasmonic resonance）使红色衰减速率随d变化呈现±15%的调制，而绿色跃迁（²H₁₁/₂/⁴S₃/₂→⁴I₁₅/₂）的衰减速率在实验上几乎不变（|k/k_ref−1|<1%）。980 nm泵浦场被单调抑制（相对自由空间参考的<f_exc>在d=5–25 nm范围内为0.27–0.48），使得观测结果能够干净地探测发射端LDOS。理论框架重现了670 nm消光共振、红带±10–15%衰减速率调制以及绿/红比随d单调下降的趋势，但未能捕捉到红带在d=15 nm处的实验凹陷，且过预测了绿带衰减速率的降低（k/k_ref^550≈0.73 vs. 1.00）。脊尖圆滑处理对Purcell因子影响仅1–3%，排除了尖端形状为主要原因。

Conclusion: 该耦合电磁-动力学框架可作为诊断工具，成功分离泵浦和发射端贡献并完成半定量预测。结果明确将绿带偏差归因于超出半椭圆模型的修正——可能源于蒸发金薄膜中的晶界阻尼（grain-boundary damping）或在550 nm处存在六能级动力学模型未包含的额外非辐射通道。这为未来进一步优化等离激元上转换平台中的LDOS工程提供了理论方向和实验基准。

Abstract: A central challenge in plasmonic upconversion is coupling between near-field engineering at the pump wavelength and local-density-of-optical-states (LDOS) engineering at the emission wavelengths. Here we show that a corrugated SU8/Au/Al2O3 grating coated with a dense NaYF4:Yb(20%),Er(5%) upconversion nanoparticle (UCNP) monolayer realises a band-selective platform: a broad plasmonic resonance near 670 nm aligned with the red 4F9/2 -> 4I15/2 Er3+ transition modulates the red decay rate by +/-15% as a function of the Al2O3 spacer thickness d, while the green 2H11/2 / 4S3/2 -> 4I15/2 transition is experimentally invariant (|k/k_ref - 1| < 1% across all d). The pump field at 980 nm is monotonically suppressed below the free-space reference (<f_exc> from 0.27 to 0.48 between d = 5 and 25 nm), so observables cleanly probe the emission-side LDOS without pump-side interference. We rationalise these results with a coupled electromagnetic-kinetic framework combining full-wave FDTD pump enhancement and orientation-averaged Purcell factors with a six-level Yb/Er rate-equation model separating radiative, intrinsic nonradiative and environment-induced nonradiative channels. The framework reproduces the 670 nm extinction resonance, the +/-10-15% red-band decay-rate modulation, and the monotonic decrease of the green/red ratio with d, but predicts a monotonic red-band trend that misses the experimental dip at d = 15 nm and over-predicts a green-band reduction (k/k_ref^550 approx. 0.73 vs. 1.00). Ridge-tip smoothing (h_round in {0, 5, 10} nm) shifts Purcell factors by only 1-3%, ruling out apex shape as the dominant cause. The framework thus serves as a diagnostic tool, isolating the green-band discrepancy as needing corrections beyond the half-ellipse model - likely grain-boundary damping in the evaporated gold or extra non-radiative channels at 550 nm not in the six-level kinetic model.

</details>


### [82] [Characterization of Photopolymerized Microscopic Chiral Structures Using Photonic Orbital Angular Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04953)
*Jing Xu,Rik Strobbe,Yovan de Coene,Renaud A. L. Vallée,Koen Clays*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合数字微镜器件（DMD）无掩模光刻与毛细自组装的手性微结构制备方法，并利用液晶空间光调制器生成涡旋光束进行螺旋二色性（HD）表征。在约15微米尺度的聚合物微结构上，利用532 nm激光观察到约30%的HD信号，并通过FDTD模拟验证了结构手性对轨道角动量（OAM）微分响应的决定性作用。该平台完全基于标准光学实验室设备，无需飞秒光源或等离激元基底，为OAM驱动的手性传感与光子逻辑器件提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微尺度手性结构（microscale chiral structures）的可控制备与手性光学表征仍是光子学、传感及超材料（metamaterial）工程中的核心挑战。现有方法往往依赖昂贵的飞秒激光、等离激元基底或特殊光刻胶，缺乏低成本、易获取的平台。

Method: 采用数字微镜器件（digital micromirror device, DMD）实现无掩模光刻，并结合毛细作用诱导自组装（capillarity-induced self-assembly）制备具有确定手性（handedness）的聚合物微结构；同时使用液晶空间光调制器（liquid-crystal spatial light modulator）生成涡旋光束（vortex beams），通过螺旋二色性（helical dichroism, HD）进行表征。

Result: 在特征直径约15微米的聚合物微结构上，利用标准532 nm激光观察到约30%的HD信号。基于高分辨率扫描电子显微镜（SEM）数据重建的三维几何结构进行严格时域有限差分（finite-difference time-domain, FDTD）模拟，成功复现实验HD谱，并证实结构手性驱动了轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum, OAM）微分响应。对映体（enantiomers）的HD谱近似镜像对称，非手性对照样本响应消失，表明OAM可作为鲁棒且空间选择性的手性探针（chiral probe）。

Conclusion: 该平台的制备与表征均依赖光学实验室标准设备，无需飞秒光源、等离激元衬底或昂贵光刻胶，为OAM驱动的手性传感、对映体选择性检测（enantioselective detection）及光子逻辑器件（photonic logic devices）开辟了实用化途径。

Abstract: The controlled fabrication and chiroptical characterization of microscale chiral structures remain central challenges in photonics, sensing, and metamaterial engineering. Here we demonstrate an accessible, low-cost platform that combines digital micromirror device-enabled maskless photolithography with capillarity-induced self-assembly to produce polymer chiral microstructures of deterministic handedness, and a liquid-crystal spatial light modulator to generate vortex beams for their characterization via helical dichroism (HD). Using a standard 532 nm laser, we observe HD signals of approximately 30% for microstructures with a characteristic diameter of about 15 micrometers. Rigorous finite-difference time-domain simulations performed on three-dimensional geometries reconstructed from high-resolution Scanning Electron Microscopy data reproduce the experimental HD spectra and confirm the role of structural handedness in driving the differential orbital angular momentum (OAM) response. Near-mirror-symmetric HD spectra for opposite-handed enantiomers, combined with a vanishing response for achiral controls, establish OAM as a robust and spatially selective chiral probe at the microscale. Crucially, both fabrication and characterization rely on equipment standard in an optics laboratory, without recourse to femtosecond sources, plasmonic substrates, or costly photoresists. These results open practical pathways toward OAM-driven chiral sensing, enantioselective detection, and photonic logic devices.

</details>


### [83] [Planar chiral nanoantenna for excitation-chirality-controlled hot spot modulation and emitter-coupled circularly polarized emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05065)
*Abhik Chakraborty,Xiaofei Wu,Ankit Kumar Singh,Fabian Scheidler,Min Jiang,Jürgen Popp,Bert Hecht,Jer-Shing Huang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文数值研究了一种平面手性等离激元纳米天线（planar chiral plasmonic nanoantenna），其纳米间隙中存在依赖于激发手性的热点（hot spot）。通过改变激发圆偏振光（circularly polarized light, CPL）的手性，可开关该热点；改变激发椭圆度和手性，则可连续调谐热点强度，调制深度接近100%。在间隙中放置量子发射器（quantum emitter）可产生近乎完美的圆偏振发射，为实现纳米级圆偏振单光子源（circularly polarized single-photon source）提供了简洁有效的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种依赖于激发光手性来控制等离激元纳米天线近场热点的方法，并建立普适性设计框架，以实现对手性纳米天线的工程化调控。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究平面手性等离激元纳米天线。通过控制几何不对称性或模式不对称性来工程设计手性纳米天线，利用圆偏振光正交线偏振分量激发的等离激元模式（plasmonic modes）的干涉效应实现热点调控。

Result: 热点可随CPL手性切换而开关；在842 nm波长处，热点具有最大近场不对称因子（near-field dissymmetry factor），约为-2。改变激发椭圆度（ellipticity）和手性可连续调制热点强度，调制深度（modulation depth）接近100%。在间隙中放置量子发射器后，可产生近乎完美的圆偏振发射。

Conclusion: 该设计实现了手性和椭圆度依赖的等离激元近场开关与动态调制，并为构建纳米级圆偏振单光子源提供了一种简洁有效的途径。

Abstract: A planar chiral plasmonic nanoantenna exhibiting an excitation-chirality-dependent hot spot in a nanogap is numerically investigated. Additionally, the underlying design principles are examined, providing a broadly applicable framework for engineering chiral nanoantennas through controlled geometrical or modal asymmetry. The hot spot can be turned on and off by changing the handedness of the exciting circularly polarized light (CPL). This effect stems from the rationally designed interference of plasmonic modes excited by the linearly polarized orthogonal components of CPL. The hot spot exhibits maximal near-field dissymmetry factor (about -2) at a wavelength of 842 nm. The intensity at the hot spot can also be continuously modulated by varying the excitation ellipticity and handedness, approaching a modulation depth of 100%. These attributes enable chirality- and ellipticity-dependent switching and dynamic modulation of the plasmonic near field. Moreover, placing a quantum emitter in the gap generates almost perfectly circularly polarized emission, offering a simple yet effective avenue to realize nanoscale circularly polarized single-photon sources.

</details>

### [84] [Medium Characterization with Hard Probes: From Cherenkov Light in QED to Jet Drift in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04393)
*Hasan R. Rahman*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一个统一的硬探针（hard probe）介质表征框架，涵盖从量子电动力学（QED）中的切伦科夫光到量子色动力学（QCD）中的喷注漂移（jet drift）。在切伦科夫部分，首次在折射率色散拟合中引入106.6 nm共振处的反常色散，并展示切伦科夫辐射角分布对折射率峰值的敏感性；在核碰撞部分，利用喷注漂移作为夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的层析探针，通过各向异性部分子演化（APE）蒙特卡洛模拟揭示了喷注修饰对介质尺寸、温度和几何的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨介质类型的硬探针表征缺乏统一的框架，且现有方法对介质精细结构的解析能力不足。具体而言，液态氩（LAr）折射率在真空紫外波段的反常色散效应此前未被纳入考虑，而高能核碰撞中喷注漂移的层析潜力也尚未被系统解耦于传统能量损失机制。

Method: 在QED部分，采用色散拟合方法对液态氩的折射率$n(\lambda)$进行建模，首次纳入106.6 nm共振处的反常色散。在QCD部分，使用各向异性部分子演化（Anisotropic Parton Evolution, APE）蒙特卡洛模拟，在PbPb、AuAu和UU等多种碰撞系统中分析喷注漂移行为。

Result: 切伦科夫辐射的角分布对折射率峰值高度敏感，在特定角度区间内显著超出各向同性闪烁光本底，该结果对DUNE和CCM等实验的粒子鉴别（Particle Identification, PID）具有重要意义。喷注漂移在椭圆流（$v_2$）和二强子共面性缺失（dihadron acoplanarity, $\Delta\phi$）等可观测量中展现出清晰的系统性，有助于将其与传统能量损失机制区分开来。

Conclusion: 硬探针的角分布和运动学特征能够显著提升对物质基本性质的解析能力。该工作为跨能标（从低能QED到高能QCD）的介质表征提供了统一的理论框架和实用的实验工具。

Abstract: This dissertation presents a unified framework for medium characterization with hard probes spanning from Cherenkov light in quantum electrodynamics (QED) to jet drift in quantum chromodynamics (QCD). We first develop a dispersive fit to the refractive index $n(λ)$ of liquid argon (LAr) by incorporating anomalous dispersion at the 106.6 nm resonance for the first time. We show that the angular distribution of Cherenkov radiation is highly sensitive to the peak of the refractive index and contributes a significant excess over isotropic scintillation in certain angular bins. This work is important for precision Particle Identification (PID) for experiments like DUNE and CCM. Transitioning to high-energy nuclear collisions, we utilize ``jet drift'' -- the flow-induced deflection of partons -- as a tomographic probe of the Quark-Gluon Plasma (QGP). Using the Anisotropic Parton Evolution (APE) Monte Carlo simulation across various collision systems (PbPb, AuAu, and UU), we disentangle how the jet modification depends on medium size, temperature, and geometry. We show that jet drift exhibits distinct systematics in observables like the elliptic flow ($v_2$) and dihadron acoplanarity ($Δφ$), which helps disentangle it from conventional energy loss. Together, these studies demonstrate how the angular and kinematic signatures of hard probes revolutionize our ability to resolve the fundamental properties of matter.

</details>

### [85] [Shaping the future of Global Interferometric Arrays: Imaging Strong Gravity and Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04133)
*Venkatessh Ramakrishnan,Violette Impellizzeri,Chi-Kwan Chan,Mariafelicia De Laurentis,Thomas Krichbaum,Andrei Lobanov,Laurent Loinard,Freek Roelofs,Eduardo Ros,Hannah R. Stacey*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文探讨了利用ALMA2040项目大幅提升的灵敏度和多频率方法，在强引力（strong-gravity）区域对广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）及其替代理论进行最严格检验，并研究相对论性喷流（relativistic jets）的形成与发射机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，甚长基线干涉测量（Very Long Baseline Interferometry, VLBI）结合阿塔卡马大型毫米/亚毫米波阵列（ALMA）的突破性进展，极大地推动了广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）的观测验证。本文旨在展望ALMA2040在强引力（strong-gravity）区域进一步约束GR及替代理论、理解相对论性喷流（relativistic jets）的潜力。

Method: 通过ALMA2040项目预期实现的大幅提升灵敏度以及多频率（multi-frequency）观测方法，对强引力（strong-gravity）区域进行观测。

Result: ALMA2040有望在强引力（strong-gravity）区域对广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）及其替代理论施加迄今为止最严格的约束（most stringent constraints），并推动对相对论性喷流（relativistic jets）形成与发射（formation and launching）机制的理解。

Conclusion: ALMA2040将显著变革现有的广义相对论（GR）观测验证研究，并在强引力（strong-gravity）物理和喷流（jet）天体物理学中发挥关键作用。

Abstract: The observational validation of General Relativity (GR) has been propelled in recent years by recent breakthroughs in Very Long Baseline Interferometry (VLBI) augmented by ALMA. We explore ALMA2040 opportunities to transform these studies through greatly improved sensitivity and a multi-frequency approach. The focus will be on placing most stringent constraints on GR and alternative theories in the strong-gravity regime, and on understanding the formation and launching of relativistic jets.

### [86] [Comprehensive Design Validation of serially powered CMS Phase-2 Pixel Modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04095)
*Giorgia Bonomelli*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文针对大型强子对撞机（LHC）升级为高亮度大型强子对撞机（HL-LHC）后更严苛的运行环境，介绍了CMS探测器Phase-2升级中像素模块的质量控制（QC）测试流程，包括原型模块表征、设计调整验证、功耗与漏电流稳定性测试，以及针对不同凸点键合（bump bonding）技术的热应力破坏性测试，以评估模块的鲁棒性与耐久性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHC升级为HL-LHC后，瞬时亮度将高达7.5×10^34 cm²/s，导致辐射环境更恶劣且数据速率显著增加，现有CMS径迹探测器（Tracker）无法在此条件下运行，因此需要开发升级版Phase-2探测器并进行设计验证。

Method: 建立了一套质量控制（Quality Control, QC）测试流程，对第一代像素模块原型进行表征并评估其性能；开展了合格性测试（qualification tests），检查功耗和漏电流稳定性等指标是否满足升级规范；进行了应力测试（stress tests）以探明设计极限，其中特别包括热应力测试（thermal stress tests），评估不同凸点键合（bump bonding）技术下凸点键合界面的强度和耐久性。

Result: 测试结果为高密度互连（High Density Interconnect, HDI）等组件的小幅设计调整提供了起点；热应力破坏性测试揭示了因HDI铜层与硅传感器、读出芯片材料热膨胀系数差异导致的机械应力问题，并评估了不同凸点键合技术的性能差异。

Conclusion: 该QC测试流程有效验证了CMS Phase-2像素模块设计的性能与鲁棒性，为后续设计优化提供了实验依据，确保升级后的探测器能够满足HL-LHC环境下的运行要求。

Abstract: After the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) upgrade into High Luminosity LHC (HL-LHC), the instantaneous luminosity is expected to reach values up to 7.5x10^34cm^2/s, causing a harsher radiation environment as well as a significant increase in data rate. The current CMS Tracker detector would not be able to operate under these conditions and it will be replaced by an upgraded version known as Phase-2. In view of the detector upgrade and as part of the design validation process, a Quality Control (QC) test flow has been developed to characterize the first pixel modules prototypes and evaluate their performance. The results of this procedure were the starting point for small design adjustments, especially for the the High Density Interconnect or HDI, the flexible low mass PCB that distributes power and signals to the module and controls the readout through a high speed data transmission channel. This talk includes qualification tests performed on the CMS Phase-2 design to ensure that all the pixel module components satisfy the upgrade specifications, for example in terms of power consumption and leakage current stability. Additionally, stress tests were conducted to probe the limits of the design, demonstrating the robustness and endurance of the module layout. Due to the differing material properties of the HDI copper layers and the silicon sensor and readout chip, temperature gradients induce different thermal expansion and contraction, resulting in mechanical stress on the bump-bond interface. For this reason, among the destructive measurements, dedicated thermal stress tests were carried out to evaluate the bump-bond strength and durability for different bump bonding techniques.

### [87] [Study of Particle Fluence Effects on Collected Charge and Depletion Voltage of the ATLAS IBL Planar Pixel Sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05030)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文基于ATLAS像素探测器最内层桶面的平面像素传感器在LHC运行十年后累积的体损伤注量（bulk damage fluence）数据，通过偏置电压扫描实验并结合TCAD与ATLAS蒙特卡洛模拟，研究了辐射损伤对传感器漏电流、电荷收集效率及耗尽电压的影响，并分析了收集电荷与耗尽电压随积分亮度的演化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHC运行十年后，ATLAS像素探测器最内层桶面的平面像素传感器已累积超过$2\times10^{15}$ 1 MeV中子等效/cm$^2$的体损伤注量，辐射损伤导致的宏观效应（漏电流增加、电荷收集效率下降、耗尽电压升高）直接影响探测器性能，亟需系统评估。

Method: 在每次数据采集周期的开始和结束时执行常规偏置电压扫描（bias voltage scans），据此研究像素簇电荷（pixel cluster charge）和体耗尽（bulk depletion）随粒子注量（particle fluence）的演化。结果通过包含辐射损伤效应的独立TCAD仿真和ATLAS蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）进行建模解释。

Result: 辐射损伤导致传感器漏电流增加、电荷收集效率（charge collection efficiency）损失以及耗尽电压（depletion voltage）升高。收集电荷和耗尽电压随积分亮度的依赖关系在整个运行周期内得到了系统分析。

Conclusion: 通过实验与模拟相结合的方式，明确了辐射损伤对ATLAS像素探测器关键性能参数的长期影响，验证了TCAD和ATLAS蒙特卡洛模拟在描述辐射损伤效应方面的有效性。

Abstract: After ten years of operation at the LHC, the planar pixel sensors of the innermost barrel layer of the ATLAS Pixel detector have accumulated an average bulk damage fluence in excess of $2\times10^{15}$ 1 MeV-neutrons equivalent/cm$^2$. The macroscopic effects of this radiation are an increase of the sensor leakage current, a loss of charge collection efficiency and an increase of the depletion voltage. Using regular bias voltage scans performed at the beginning and end of each data taking campaign the evolution of the pixel cluster charge and bulk depletion is studied as a function of particle fluence. Results are interpreted with the modelling provided by standalone TCAD and ATLAS Monte Carlo simulation including radiation damage effects. The dependence of the collected charge and the depletion voltage with integrated luminosity are studied through the full period of operation.

</details>


<div id='math.DS'></div>

# math.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [88] [Programming sequential deployment of origami via kinematic transition fronts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04473)
*Rinki Imada,Tomohiro Tachi*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于离散动力学系统中异宿轨道（heteroclinic orbits）的通用设计框架，用于在折纸（origami）结构中实现由纯几何约束驱动的运动学传播前沿（kinematic transition fronts），从而实现可编程的序列展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然传播前沿已在自然界与工程系统中广泛存在，且基于能量驱动的前沿传播已有研究，但纯几何约束下的前沿传播缺乏通用设计框架；尤其是如何通过运动学传播在折纸中实现可编程的序列部署，仍是一个开放挑战。

Method: 基于运动学传播前沿与离散动力系统中异宿轨道之间的对应关系建立系统化设计框架。以可展开且可平折的四度顶点（degree-4 origami vertices）折纸条带为研究对象，通过分析相邻折痕间的非对称耦合产生非线性递推关系（recurrence relation），从而生成连接展开态与平折叠态的异宿轨道。

Result: 非对称耦合产生的非线性递推关系组合后形成异宿轨道，实现多米诺骨牌式的序列展开；宏观形状可通过利用递推关系中的不变性独立于传播行为进行编程；通过厚板折纸原型验证了该方法的可行性。

Conclusion: 该工作为折纸中的序列部署提供了可编程传播前沿的设计方法，同时也为几何约束系统中的运动学传播前沿建立了通用理论框架。

Abstract: Propagating transition fronts, in which local interactions sequentially trigger state changes, are widely observed across natural, biological, and engineered systems. While such propagation has been engineered using energy-driven instabilities, front propagation governed purely by geometric constraints remains underexplored and lacks a general design framework. In particular, how to program sequential deployment in origami through such kinematic propagation remains an open challenge. Here, we develop a systematic design framework for kinematic transition fronts based on their correspondence with heteroclinic orbits in discrete dynamical systems. Focusing on strips of developable and flat-foldable degree-4 origami vertices, we show that asymmetric coupling between adjacent creases produces nonlinear recurrence relations whose composition generically gives rise to heteroclinic orbits connecting developed and flat-folded states, enabling domino-like sequential deployment. We further show that macroscopic shape can be programmed independently of propagation behavior by exploiting invariances in the recurrence relation, and illustrate the approach through a representative thick-panel origami prototype. These results enable programmable sequential deployment in origami via transition fronts, while also establishing a general framework for kinematic transition fronts in geometrically constrained systems.

</details>


<div id='nlin.AO'></div>

# nlin.AO [[Back]](#toc)

### [89] [Thermodynamic efficiency of self-organisation in nonequilibrium steady states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04508)
*Qianyang Chen,Mikhail Prokopenko*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文通过信息论度量——熵减与广义功之比，研究了非平衡自组织系统（持续伊辛模型与活性伊辛模型）将消耗能量转化为宏观有序的效率，发现热力学效率在相变点最大，并在非平衡条件下热力学效率与推断效率发生分离，其差距反映了系统偏离平衡态的程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性物质（active matter）通过非平衡动力学产生有序或模式，一个开放性的研究挑战是确定非平衡自组织系统将消耗能量转化为宏观有序的效率。

Method: 使用信息论（information theory）量——通过估计由小控制参数扰动（control-parameter perturbation）引起的熵减（entropy reduction）与扰动所需的广义功（generalized work）之比，并将该框架应用于两个非平衡自组织系统：持续伊辛模型（persistent Ising model）与活性伊辛模型（active Ising model）。

Result: 非平衡系统的热力学效率（thermodynamic efficiency）在相变（phase transition）处达到最大，与平衡系统一致；在非平衡条件下，热力学效率与推断效率（inferential efficiency）发生分离，其差距反映了系统偏离平衡态的程度。

Conclusion: 非平衡自组织系统的热力学效率在相变点最大化；在平衡系统中二者相等的热力学效率与推断效率，在非平衡条件下会分离，且分离程度可作为系统远离平衡态的度量。

Abstract: Active matter generates order or patterns through nonequilibrium dynamics. An open research challenge is to determine how efficiently a nonequilibrium self-organising system can convert consumed energy into macroscopic order. We study an information-theoretic quantity that directly addresses this challenge by estimating the entropy reduction induced by a small control-parameter perturbation, relative to the generalised work required for the perturbation. This quantity has previously been considered mainly in an equilibrium or near-equilibrium context, and here we extend this framework and apply it to two nonequilibrium self-organising systems: persistent and active Ising models. We observe that the thermodynamic efficiency of nonequilibrium systems maximises at phase transitions, as in equilibrium systems. Furthermore, we compare thermodynamic efficiency and inferential efficiency across control parameters. While these two quantities are equal in equilibrium as a consequence of the fluctuation-dissipation theorem, we report that they diverge out of equilibrium, and the gap reflects how far the system is from equilibrium.

</details>

Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用LHCb实验在质心能量13 TeV、积分亮度6.0 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，首次观测到无粲纯重子衰变Λₛ⁰ → Λ p p̄，显著度为5.1标准差，并相对拓扑类似衰变Λₛ⁰ → Λ K⁺ K⁻测得其分支比为(5.1 ± 1.3(stat) ± 0.3(syst)) × 10⁻²。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无粲纯重子衰变（charmless purely baryonic decay）是检验重子衰变机制和强相互作用理论的重要探针，但此前实验上尚未观测到该过程。本研究旨在首次寻找Λₛ⁰ → Λ p p̄衰变并测定其分支比（branching fraction）。

Method: 使用LHCb探测器记录的质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量√s = 13 TeV，对应积分亮度6.0 fb⁻¹。通过要求伴强子系统的不变质量m(h h̄) < 2.85 GeV，明确排除中间粲偶素共振（charmonium resonance）衰变到p p̄和K⁺ K⁻末态的贡献。

Result: 信号衰变以5.1标准差的统计显著度被观测到。相对分支比B(Λₛ⁰ → Λ p p̄)/B(Λₛ⁰ → Λ K⁺ K⁻) = (5.1 ± 1.3(stat) ± 0.3(syst)) × 10⁻²，为首次测量。

Conclusion: 该结果为理解无粲纯重子衰变提供了首个实验观测，并对相关强相互作用理论模型构成约束。测量中系统误差（systematic uncertainty）远小于统计误差（statistical uncertainty），表明未来更大数据样本有望进一步改善精度。

Abstract: A search for the charmless purely baryonic decay $\mathinner{\mathitΛ^0_b\!\to \mathitΛ p \overline{p}}$ is performed using proton-proton collision data recorded by the LHCb experiment at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13\,\text{TeV}$ and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $6.0\,\text{fb}^{-1}$. The signal decay is observed with a significance of 5.1 standard deviations. Its branching fraction is measured for the first time, relative to that of the topologically similar decay $\mathinner{\mathitΛ^0_b\!\to \mathitΛ K^+ K^-}$. Contributions from intermediate charmonium resonances decaying to the $p \overline{p}$ and $K^+ K^-$ final states are explicitly excluded with a requirement on the invariant mass of the companion hadron system, $m(h\bar{h}) < 2.85\,\text{GeV}$, where $h$ stands for a proton or a charged kaon. The relative branching fraction is found to be $$ \frac{B(\mathinner{\mathitΛ^0_b\!\to \mathitΛ p \overline{p}})}{B(\mathinner{\mathitΛ^0_b\!\to \mathitΛ K^+ K^-})} = (5.1 \pm 1.3_{\text{(stat)}} \pm 0.3_{\text{(syst)}}) \times 10^{-2} \,. $$

</details>

Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用BESIII探测器采集的约1.009×10¹⁰个J/ψ事例，通过两个衰变道J/ψ→γη和J/ψ→γη'，η'→π⁺π⁻η，以5.9σ和7.8σ的统计显著性观测到η→e⁺e⁻e⁺e⁻稀有双达利兹衰变（double Dalitz decay）信号，测得分支比为(2.63±0.34_stat±0.16_syst)×10⁻⁵，结果与先前测量一致并进一步约束了标准模型之外的新物理（physics beyond the standard model）


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究η介子极为罕见的双达利兹衰变η→e⁺e⁻e⁺e⁻，以检验标准模型（Standard Model）对稀有衰变过程的预言精度，并探索可能的新物理信号

Method: 基于BESIII探测器采集的(1.0087±0.0044)×10¹⁰个J/ψ事例样本，通过J/ψ→γη和J/ψ→γη'，η'→π⁺π⁻η两个产生道重建η→e⁺e⁻e⁺e⁻信号，在e⁺e⁻e⁺e⁻不变质量谱中提取信号并合并两个模式进行联合分析

Result: 在两个衰变道中分别以5.9σ和7.8σ的统计显著性观测到清晰η信号；合并后测得η→e⁺e⁻e⁺e⁻的分支比为(2.63±0.34_stat±0.16_syst)×10⁻⁵

Conclusion: 测量结果在不确定度范围内与先前实验测量一致，进一步缩小了标准模型之外的物理空间，增强了对稀有衰变过程的约束能力

Abstract: Using a data sample of $(1.0087 \pm 0.0044) \times {10^{10}}$ $J/ψ$ events collected with the BESIII detector, we study the rare double Dalitz decay of $η\rightarrow e^+e^-e^+e^-$ through the processes $J/ψ\rightarrow γη$ and $J/ψ\rightarrow γη' ,η' \to π^+π^-η$. Clear $η$ signals are observed in the $e^+e^-e^+e^-$ invariant mass spectrum, with statistical significances of 5.9$σ$ and 7.8$σ$ for the two channels, respectively. By combining both modes, we determine the branching fraction of $η\rightarrow e^+ e^- e^+ e^-$ to be $(2.63~\pm~0.34_{\rm stat}~\pm~0.16_{\rm syst}) \times10^{-5}$. The result is consistent with the previous measurements within uncertainties and further constrains physics beyond the standard model.

</details>


### [92] [Geant4 Optical Simulation without C++](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04907)
*Ariestotle Raj Maharjan,Jianchen Li,Jing Liu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文扩展了Geant4的纯文本几何描述语法，新增光学属性支持（:prop和:surf标签），使用户无需编写C++代码即可配置和运行完整的光学模拟，并通过切伦科夫辐射、闪烁、瑞利散射和吸收等关键光学过程验证了该扩展的有效性，同时展示了UNIFIED模型配置复杂光学边界的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始Geant4的光学模拟需要用户编写C++代码并频繁重新编译，学习门槛高、开发效率低。为简化光学模拟的配置流程，降低使用难度，本文提出在纯文本几何描述语法中直接集成光学属性定义。

Method: 在Geant4的纯文本几何描述语法中新增":prop"和":surf"两个标签，分别用于定义体材料（bulk materials）和表面界面（surface interfaces）的光学属性。用户通过文本配置文件即可设置光学模拟参数，无需编写C++代码或重新编译。

Result: 该扩展成功实现了对切伦科夫辐射（Cherenkov radiation）、闪烁（scintillation）、瑞利散射（Rayleigh scattering）和吸收（absorption）等关键光学过程的模拟验证。此外，通过实际场景展示了使用UNIFIED模型配置复杂光学边界的完整流程。

Conclusion: 该语法扩展显著降低了光学模拟的门槛，消除了频繁重新编译的需求，为快速原型设计（rapid prototyping）和仿真研究提供了高效、易用的工具。

Abstract: The plain text geometry description syntax in Geant4 has been extended to incorporate optical properties for bulk materials and surface interfaces. This extension enables users to configure and execute comprehensive optical simulations without writing C++ code, significantly lowering the learning curve and eliminating the need for frequent recompilation. In this paper, we detail the implementation of the new ":prop" and ":surf" tags and validate them through examples of key optical processes, including Cherenkov radiation, scintillation, Rayleigh scattering, and absorption. Furthermore, we provide a thorough demonstration of configuring complex optical boundaries using the UNIFIED model. These capabilities are contextualized through practical scenarios, showcasing the extension's potential for rapid prototyping and simulation studies.

</details>

### [93] [Regulating oxygen content and superconductivity in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7+δ}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04562)
*Peiyue Ma,Jingyuan Li,Xing Huang,Yixing Zhao,Yifeng Han,Mengwu Huo,Deyuan Hu,Chaoxin Huang,Hengyuan Zhang,Sihao Deng,Lunhua He,Juan Rodriguez-Carvajal,Abhisek Bandyopadhyay,Alessandro Puri,Devashibhai Adroja,Xiang Chen,Tao Xie,Zhen Chen,Hualei Sun,Meng Wang*

TL;DR: 本研究通过精确调控La₃Ni₂O₇₊δ中的氧含量，实现了对Ruddlesden-Popper（RP）镍酸盐微结构的定制，并建立了超导转变温度（T_c）和上临界场（H_c2）随氧含量变化的相图，揭示了氧含量对相纯度和超导性质的直接调控作用。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高质量Ruddlesden-Popper（RP）镍酸盐的合成因氧含量变化和共生相（intergrown phases）的普遍存在而面临挑战，精确控制化学计量比并表征随之产生的物理性质对于理解该类材料中的高温超导（high-T_c superconductivity）机制至关重要。

Method: 本文合成了一系列氧含量系统可控的La₃Ni₂O₇₊δ样品，进行了全面的结构与成分分析，并通过高压输运测量（high-pressure transport measurements）对不同微结构样品的超导性质进行了表征。

Result: 精确氧调控可获得纯双层相（bilayer phase）、双层与杂化单层-双层相（hybrid single-layer-bilayer phase）的混合物、以及含三层共生（trilayer intergrowths）的以双层为主的相；这些相表现出具有不同T_c值的超导转变。氧含量不仅决定共生相的存在与否，还直接调控双层超导的上临界场（H_c2）。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了La₃Ni₂O₇₊δ中T_c和H_c2随氧含量变化的相图，推进了RP镍酸盐的合成控制，并为其超导机制提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The synthesis of high-quality Ruddlesden-Popper (RP) nickelates remains challenging due to variations in oxygen content and the prevalence of intergrown RP phases. Precisely controlling the stoichiometry and characterizing the resulting physical properties are essential for understanding the mechanism of high-$T_c$ superconductivity in these materials. In this work, we synthesize a series of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7+δ}$ samples with systematically controlled oxygen content and perform comprehensive structural and compositional analyses. Precise oxygen tuning enables us to tailor the microstructure, yielding a pure bilayer phase, a mixture of bilayer and hybrid single-layer-bilayer phases, and a predominantly bilayer phase containing trilayer intergrowths. High-pressure transport measurements reveal distinct superconducting transitions with contrasting $T_c$ values, corresponding to the bilayer phase, the hybrid phase, and trilayer inclusions. Notably, we find that oxygen content not only governs the phase purity$-$i.e., the presence of intergrowth phases$-$but also directly modulates the upper critical field ($H_{c2}$) of the bilayer superconductivity. By establishing a phase diagram of $T_c$ and $H_{c2}$ as functions of oxygen content in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7+δ}$, this work advances synthetic control and provides new insights into the superconducting mechanism of RP nickelates.

### [94] [Superconductivity in moiré transition metal dichalcogenide bilayers: comparison of two distinct theoretical approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04693)
*Waseem Akbar,Michał Zegrodnik*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过负U-Hubbard模型和t-J-U模型两种互补理论方法，研究了扭曲WSe₂双层中的超导态，对比了常规s波配对与非常规强关联配对场景，并结合实验观测讨论了两种框架的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近在莫尔过渡金属二硫族化物（moiré transition-metal dichalcogenide）双层中观测到了超导电性，但其配对机制和间隙对称性（gap symmetry）尚未明确，亟需理论分析来解释实验观测。

Method: 采用两种互补的理论方法：(1) 负U-Hubbard模型（negative $U$-Hubbard model），代表相对常规的配对场景；(2) $t$-$J$-$U$模型，允许非常规的间隙对称性并通过库仑排斥（Coulomb repulsion）引入强关联重整化（renormalization）效应。

Result: 负U-Hubbard模型下得到各向同性的s波（$s$-$wave$）能隙，强电子-电子排斥不直接影响配对态；t-J-U模型则允许非常规间隙对称性，强关联效应通过库仑排斥产生显著重整化。

Conclusion: 两种框架预测的超导态关键性质存在差异，需结合现有实验观测来判定哪种配对场景更符合扭曲WSe₂的真实超导机理。

Abstract: Superconductivity has recently been observed in moiré transition-metal dichalcogenide bilayers. Here, we investigate the superconducting state in twisted WSe$_2$ using two complementary theoretical approaches. The first is based on the negative $U$-Hubbard model and represents a relatively conventional pairing scenario, in which strong electron-electron repulsion does not directly affect the paired state and an isotropic $s$-$wave$ gap emerges. The second approach employs the $t$-$J$-$U$ model, allowing for unconventional gap symmetries and incorporating strong correlation effects via substantial renormalization induced by Coulomb repulsion. We compare the key properties of the superconducting states obtained within these two frameworks and discuss their implications in light of available experimental observations.

</details>


### [95] [Nonlocal transport phenomena in coupled quasiperiodic Kitaev chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04710)
*Koki Mizuno*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过准周期Kitaev链模型研究耦合一维p波超导Fibonacci准晶中的拓扑相，运用Keldysh形式论和递归格林函数方法揭示了Majorana边缘模的存在及其波函数渗漏现象，并发现了一种由准周期性诱导的新型拓扑相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明耦合系统可以承载包含Majorana费米子（Majorana fermions）的拓扑边缘模（topological edge modes），并增强其拓扑保护，但这种效应依赖于准周期性（quasiperiodicity）的具体模式。因此，需要进一步阐明该耦合系统中的拓扑相及其输运性质。

Method: 采用Keldysh形式论（Keldysh formalism）和递归格林函数方法（recursive Green's function method），分析微分电导（differential conductance）对连接引线模式的依赖关系。

Result: 在耦合系统中发现了拓扑相的存在，其标志是Majorana边缘模的出现以及Majorana波函数的渗漏（seepage）。此外，识别出了一种由准周期性诱导的新型拓扑相变（topological phase transition）。

Conclusion: 耦合准周期Kitaev链系统能够呈现丰富的拓扑相，且准周期性可诱导新的拓扑相变，这为调控Majorana费米子的拓扑性质提供了新的机制。

Abstract: We investigate the topological phases in a coupled one-dimensional p-wave superconducting Fibonacci quasicrystal modeled by the quasiperiodic Kitaev chain. Recent studies have shown that the coupled system can host topological edge modes with Majorana fermions and enhance their topological protection, depending on the pattern of quasiperiodicity. In this work, we elucidate the topological phases of the coupled system and demonstrate the dependence of differential conductance on the lead connecting pattern employing the Keldysh formalism and the recursive Green's function method. Our findings reveal the emergence of topological phases in the coupled system, which are characterized by the presence of Majorana edge modes and the seepage of the Majorana wave function. Furthermore, we identify a new topological phase transition induced by quasiperiodicity in the coupled system.

### [96] [Response tensor for the superconducting (Josephson) diode effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04928)
*Qiong Qin,Jie Wu,Congjun Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一个响应张量（response tensor）$\mathbf{\hat χ}$ 来表征超导（约瑟夫森）二极管效应中的非互易临界电流响应。该张量描述了临界电流角分布偶极矩与外磁场的耦合，是正常态霍尔响应的超导类比。在不同对称性体系中，该张量呈现全反对称、对称或对角无迹等不同形式，可用于检测超导态中的向列序（nematic order）、预测二极管效应的对称条件，并为探测超导相内部的向列相变和电子结构信息提供新工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管效应中的非互易临界电流响应缺乏统一的张量描述框架，现有理论难以系统刻画临界电流角分布与外加磁场的耦合机制。

Method: 提出一个响应张量 $\mathbf{\hat χ}$，通过将临界电流的角分布偶极矩分量与外磁场耦合，类比正常态霍尔响应，并结合不同点群对称性（$C_{3v}$、$C_{4v}$、$C_{6v}$、$D_{2d}$）以及向列序的存在性进行分析。

Result: 在具有Rashba自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的$C_{3v}$、$C_{4v}$或$C_{6v}$对称性准二维体系中，该张量呈全反对称（fully antisymmetric）形式；引入向列序后出现对称贡献。在$D_{2d}$对称性的Dresselhaus自旋轨道耦合体系中，张量为对角无迹（diagonal traceless）形式，向列序引入迹部分（trace part）。

Conclusion: 该张量不仅能描述外场或内禀有效磁场下的超导二极管效应，还能预测磁场平行于电流时实现二极管效应的对称条件，为探测超导相内部的向列序及向列相变提供了有力工具，并可能揭示更深层的电子结构和对称性破缺序信息。

Abstract: We propose a response tensor $\mathbf{\hat χ}$ to characterize the non-reciprocal critical current response of the superconducting (Josephson) diode effect. It describes the coupling between the dipole component of the angular distribution of the critical current and the applied magnetic field -- an analogue to the Hall response in the normal state. In quasi-2D systems with Rashba spin-orbit coupling and point group symmetries $C_{3v}$, $C_{4v}$ or $C_{6v}$, this tensor takes a fully antisymmetric form. When nematicity is present, a symmetric contribution emerges, providing an indicator of the nematic order in the superconducting state. In contrast, for systems exhibiting Dresselhaus spin-orbit coupling with the $D_{2d}$ symmetry, the tensor becomes diagonal traceless, and nematicity brings in a trace part. Our analysis not only accounts for the superconducting diode effect under external applied or intrinsic effective magnetic fields, but also predicts the symmetry conditions for realizing the diode effect when the magnetic field is aligned with the current. Beyond this, the proposed tensor provides a promising tool for detecting nematicity and potential nematic transitions deep within the superconducting phase. It may also encode additional information about the underlying electronic structure and symmetry-breaking orders, warranting further experimental investigation.

</details>

### [97] [Differential measurements of $γγ\toττ$ and constraints on $τ$-lepton electromagnetic moments in Pb+Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{_\text{NN}}} = 5.02$ TeV with ATLAS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04584)
*The ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ATLAS探测器记录的1.93 nb⁻¹ Pb+Pb对撞数据（质心能量 \(\sqrt{s_{_\text{NN}}} = 5.02\) TeV），首次实现了 \(\gamma\gamma\to\tau\tau\) 过程的微分标定测量（differential fiducial measurement），并通过对未去卷（unfolding）前三个区域中缪子横动量分布的最大似然拟合（maximum-likelihood fit），提取了τ轻子的反常磁矩 \(a_\tau\) 和电偶极矩 \(d_\tau\)，后者为重离子碰撞中的首次测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用重离子对撞中的光子-光子相互作用（photon–photon interactions）为研究τ轻子的电磁性质提供了独特的探针。本文旨在首次对 \(\gamma\gamma\to\tau\tau\) 过程进行微分标定测量，并首次在重离子碰撞中提取τ轻子的电偶极矩 \(d_\tau\)，以检验标准模型并寻找新物理信号。

Method: 选取其中一个τ轻子衰变为缪子和两个中微子（\(τ\toν_τ\barν_μμ\)）的事例，根据另一个τ轻子衰变产物中存在电子、一条或三条带电粒子径迹（track）将事例分为三个区域。测量在铅离子均保持完整且无中子发射的事例中进行。在粒子层级（particle level）的三个标定区域（fiducial region）中对七个变量测量微分截面，并与不同光子通量模型和自旋关联效应的理论预言进行比较。采用最大似然拟合对三个区域未去卷前的缪子横动量分布进行拟合，提取 \(a_\tau\) 和 \(d_\tau\)。

Result: 测量了衰变缪子的横动量（\(p_\text{T}\)）、另一τ轻子可见衰变粒子的 \(p_\text{T}\)、双τ系统可见粒子的总 \(p_\text{T}\)、不变质量（invariant mass）和赝快度（pseudorapidity），以及单个τ轻子可见衰变粒子的快度（rapidity）和非共面性（acoplanarity）。在95%置信水平下给出约束区间：\(-0.057 < a_\tau < 0.035\) 和 \(|d_\tau| < 2.7 \times 10^{-16}~e\text{cm}\)。

Conclusion: 本文提供了 \(\gamma\gamma\to\tau\tau\) 过程的首个微分标定测量结果，并在重离子碰撞中首次测量了τ轻子的电偶极矩。实验结果对不同的理论模型具有区分能力，并为 \(a_\tau\) 和 \(d_\tau\) 设定了新的实验约束，对标准模型检验和新物理搜索具有重要意义。

Abstract: This paper presents the first differential fiducial measurements of $γγ\toττ$ using 1.93 nb$^{-1}$ of Pb+Pb data at $\sqrt{s_{_\text{NN}}} = 5.02$ TeV recorded by the ATLAS detector. Events in which one of the $τ$-leptons decays into a muon and two neutrinos $τ\toν_τ\barν_μμ$ are selected and are categorized into three regions by the presence of an electron or either one or three charged-particle track(s) from the second $τ$-lepton decay. The measurement is performed in events where both Pb ions remain intact and no neutrons are emitted. Differential cross-sections are measured for seven variables in three fiducial regions at particle level. The measurements are compared to theory predictions with different photon flux models and spin correlation effects. For the fiducial region with one muon and one electron in the final state, comparisons to next-to-leading-order electroweak predictions are also made. The transverse momentum ($p_\text{T}$) of the decay muon, the $p_\text{T}$ of the visible decay particles of the other $τ$-lepton, the total $p_\text{T}$, invariant mass, and pseudorapidity of the visible particles from the di-$τ$ system, and the rapidity and acoplanarity of the visible decay particles from either $τ$-lepton are measured. A maximum-likelihood fit to the muon transverse-momentum distributions in the three regions before unfolding is performed to extract the $τ$-lepton anomalous magnetic moment $a_τ$ and electric dipole moment $d_τ$, the latter for the first time in heavy ion collisions. The observed 95% confidence level intervals are $-0.057 <a_τ< 0.035$ and $|d_τ|< 2.7 \times 10^{-16}~e\text{cm}$.}

</details>

### [98] [Solar photocatalytic disinfection of well water using immobilized TiO$_2$: A comparative field study with SODIS in Antananarivo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04089)
*Jean Odilon Andrianirina,Philippe Manjakasoa Randriantsoa,Georgette Ramanantsizehena,Domohina Raharinirina*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种简易、低成本的太阳能光催化反应器（solar photocatalytic reactor），通过在玻璃板上涂覆商用二氧化钛（TiO₂）薄膜，在自然阳光下仅需10分钟即可完全灭活马达加斯加农村井水中的粪大肠菌群（fecal coliforms），显著优于传统SODIS方法，为资源匮乏地区提供了一种有前景的家用级水处理技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展中国家农村地区获取安全饮用水仍面临重大挑战，亟需开发简单、低成本的水消毒技术。

Method: 采用丙酮浆料法（acetone slurry method）将商用TiO₂薄膜沉积于玻璃板上，在马达加斯加首都塔那那利佛（Antananarivo）的自然阳光下进行光催化消毒实验，并与传统SODIS方法（无催化剂太阳能消毒）进行对比；对来自十口不同井的水样进行理化参数（physicochemical parameters）和细菌学质量（bacteriological quality）表征。

Result: 光催化反应器在仅10分钟的太阳曝晒后，所有十份水样的粪大肠菌群均被完全灭活（0 CFU/100 mL），而SODIS对照组在代表性样品中仅将初始菌量减少约51%；消毒动力学随水浊度（turbidity）和pH值略有变化，但完全灭活始终得以实现。

Conclusion: 即便是不均匀、低纯度的TiO₂涂层，也能在太阳辐射下显著加速细菌灭活，为低资源环境提供了一种有前景且可负担的家用级水处理技术。

Abstract: Access to safe drinking water remains a major challenge in rural areas of developing countries. This study investigates the feasibility of a simple, low-cost solar photocatalytic reactor coated with commercial titanium dioxide (TiO$_2$) for the disinfection of well water contaminated with fecal coliforms. A TiO$_2$ film was deposited on a glass plate using a straightforward acetone slurry method and exposed to natural sunlight in Antananarivo, Madagascar. The efficiency was compared to the conventional SODIS method (solar disinfection without catalyst). Water samples from ten different wells were characterized for physicochemical parameters and bacteriological quality. After only 10 minutes of solar exposure, the photocatalytic reactor achieved complete inactivation (0 CFU/100 mL) of fecal coliforms for all ten samples tested, whereas the SODIS control only reduced the initial count by approximately $51\%$ in a representative sample. While disinfection kinetics varied slightly with water turbidity and pH, complete inactivation was consistently achieved. The results demonstrate that even a non-uniform, low-purity TiO$_2$ coating significantly accelerates bacterial disinfection under solar radiation, offering a promising and affordable household-scale treatment technology for low-resource settings.

</details>

### [99] [Composite top partners in exotic colour representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04143)
*Giacomo Cacciapaglia,Rosy Caliri,Aldo Deandrea,Benjamin Fuks,Mark Goodsell,Jan Hadlik,Manuel Kunkel,Werner Porod*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了部分复合（partial compositeness）复合希格斯模型（Composite Higgs models）中存在的颜色六重态（colour-sextet）费米子共振态，构建了其低能有效相互作用并推导了特征衰变模式。通过重解译ATLAS和CMS实验的高多重数末态搜索，给出当前LHC对单个六重态分量的质量排除上限为2–2.5 TeV，全多重态时约束更强，HL-LHC外推可达约3 TeV，表明色六重态费米子是复合希格斯模型尚未充分探索的重要探测渠道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复合希格斯模型中的部分复合机制通常会预言有色费米子共振态，以往唯象研究集中于色三重态（colour-triplet）和色八重态（colour-octet）顶伙伴（top partners），但若干超色（hypercolour）紫外完备构造也包含色六重态（colour-sextet）费米子，这类态尚未被系统研究。

Method: 在色六重态出现的最小模型类中构建低能有效相互作用（low-energy effective interactions），推导其特征衰变模式。重解译（reinterpret）ATLAS和CMS已有的高多重数末态搜索数据，以导出对这些共振态的专用约束（dedicated constraints）。

Result: 色六重态主要通过带色的赝南部-戈德斯通玻色子（coloured pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone bosons）衰变，产生富顶夸克（top-rich）末态；含b喷注（b-jets）和丢失横能量（missing transverse energy）的额外道也重要。当前LHC数据对单个六重态分量排除质量上限为2–2.5 TeV，包含完整六重态多重态（sextet multiplet）时约束更强；保守外推至HL-LHC，排除能力接近3 TeV。

Conclusion: 色六重态费米子为部分复合复合希格斯模型提供了一个强大且尚未充分探索的探测途径（probe），现有LHC数据已给出显著的质量约束，未来HL-LHC将进一步提升探测灵敏度。

Abstract: Composite Higgs models with partial compositeness generically predict coloured fermionic resonances associated with the strong dynamics responsible for electroweak symmetry breaking. While most phenomenological studies have focused on colour-triplet and colour-octet top partners, several UV-complete hypercolour constructions also contain fermionic colour sextets. We present a systematic study of these states in the minimal model classes where they arise, constructing the relevant low-energy interactions and deriving their characteristic decay patterns. The sextets predominantly decay through coloured pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone bosons, leading to top-rich final states, while additional channels with $b$-jets and missing transverse energy can be important. We reinterpret existing ATLAS and CMS searches for high-multiplicity final states to derive the dedicated constraints on these resonances. For the benchmark spectra considered, current LHC data exclude individual sextet components up to masses in the $2-2.5$ TeV regime, with stronger bounds when the full sextet multiplet is included, while conservative extrapolations to the HL-LHC indicate a reach close to $3$ TeV. Our results therefore show that colour-sextet fermions provide a powerful and largely unexplored probe of composite Higgs models with partial compositeness.

</details>


### [100] [Proton-Proton to Antinucleon Cross Sections for Cosmic Ray Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04150)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙线（cosmic ray）与星际物质相互作用会产生反质子,其准确预测对理解宇宙线传播和暗物质间接探测至关重要。现有实验（如NA49）初步报告了反中子相对于反质子的显著过剩，需要理论验证。

Method: 采用QCD共线因子化框架，在次领头阶精度下计算质子-质子碰撞中的反质子和反中子产生截面，并结合数据驱动模型（data-driven model）与实验测量结果进行比较。

Conclusion: NA49实验报告的大幅反中子过剩缺乏理论支持；当前框架下的过剩仅为温和的百分之几，且进一步厘清该问题需要更精确的低横向动量区域数据。

Abstract: We present predictions of inclusive antiproton and antineutron production cross sections in proton-proton collisions relevant to primary and secondary antiproton production in cosmic ray interactions with interstellar matter. Our predictions are based on collinear factorisation in Quantum Chromodynamics and are accurate to next-to-leading order in the perturbative expansion of the strong coupling. We assess the relevance of cross sections measured at collider experiments, such as NA49 at the CERN SPS and ALICE at the LHC, to the kinetic energy ranges accessed by cosmic ray detectors. We characterise the associated uncertainties due to the input parton distribution and fragmentation functions, and to missing higher orders. We critically examine the ~30% excess of antineutron over antiproton production in proton-proton collisions preliminarily reported by the NA49 experiment by combining our predictions with a data-driven model. Our results do not support the NA49 finding, and point to a mild excess of a few percent. We finally show that the NA49 result could only be reconciled with our framework by invoking sizeable differences between antiproton and antineutron production in the poorly constrained region of small transverse momenta of the produced hadron.

Method: 基于实验数据的过量（excess）迹象，分析约95 GeV和约152 GeV两个候选新希格斯玻色子在双光子（di-photon）通道及其他衰变模式中的显著性；通过产生机制（如Drell-Yan过程）和衰变特征（如与轻子、b喷注及缺失能量的关联）推断其可能的SU(2)_L三重态（Y=0）属性；并检验新物理对顶夸克微分分布中标准模型预测与测量之间张力的贡献。

Conclusion: 电弱能标下约95 GeV和约152 GeV处存在新希格斯玻色子的实验迹象，其中152 GeV候选者与SU(2)_L三重态（Y=0）模型相符；这两个标量粒子可能解释顶夸克微分分布中的标准模型张力，表明标量扇区的扩展是超越标准模型物理（BSM physics）的一个重要方向。

Abstract: After the Higgs discovery, the question of whether particles beyond those of the Standard Model exist is more pressing than ever. These excesses are most significant in the di-photon channel but are supported by weaker-than-expected limits in other decay modes. While for the 95 GeV candidate the production mechanism is mostly unknown, the (hypothetical) 152 GeV Higgs is dominantly produced in association with leptons, $(b)$ jets and missing energy, pointing towards the Drell-Yan production of an $SU(2)_L$ triplet with $Y=0$. Interestingly, this model predicts $t\to H^\pm b$ with $H^\pm\to WZ$, which resembles the signature of $t\bar{t}Z$ production in the Standard Model and is in fact preferred by current data. Abstract: Spontaneous CP violation (SCPV) provides a promising solution to the strong CP problem, explaining the smallness of the QCD $θ$-angle while generating the Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa (CKM) phase. In the present work, we review and discuss the realization of SCPV in the supersymmetric framework, which addresses critical issues such as the naturalness of the scale of SCPV and the presence of problematic higher dimensional operators and radiative corrections spoiling the mechanism. It is explicitly shown that SCPV is realized along flat directions and stabilized through supersymmetry-breaking effects and a non-perturbative dynamics, predicting light SCPV sector particles feebly coupled to the Standard Model particles. Furthermore, we discuss the issue of baryon asymmetric Universe in the SCPV framework and point out that the Affleck-Dine mechanism can successfully generate the observed baryon asymmetry with a low reheating temperature compatible with the gravitino dark matter. Our framework predicts a nonzero neutron electric dipole moment which is within the reach of near-future experiments.

Abstract: The discovery of the Higgs boson by the ATLAS and CMS experiments concluded a glorious century of experimental particle physics discoveries, from Rutherford's discovery of the nucleus in 1911, through the discoveries of quarks and leptons from the 1950s to the 1970s, to the discoveries of the weak vector bosons in the 1980s. It cemented the Standard Model of particle physics as providing the viable parameterisation of all sub-atomic observables up to the TeV scale and possibly up to the GUT and Planck scales. The experimental determination of the Higgs properties and parameters will shed light on these fundamental theories. A particularly pertaining question from the point of view of String Phenomenology is whether the Higgs boson is a fundamental or composite particle. The fermionic Z2xZ2 orbifolds provide bench mark models to explore how the parameters of the Standard Model can arise from a theory of quantum gravity, as well as for physics Beyond the Standard Model. Observation that the Higgs is composite will nullify much of the work that have gone into heterotic string model building over the past 40 years and will indicate the relevance of other classes of string vacua or possibly other approaches to quantum gravity. In the Dirac setup, the standard model is extended by three generations of complex scalars ($φ_i$) and right-handed Dirac partners ($ν_{R_i}$) of SM neutrinos ($ν_{L_i}$), along with a pair of singlet-doublet fermions $χ$ and $Ψ$. The \textit{CP}-violating out-of-equilibrium decays of the scalar fields $φ_i$ generate baryon asymmetry via the Dirac leptogenesis route. We show that in the Majorana setup, successful leptogenesis is possible even in the sub-TeV regime, while in the Dirac setup, the scale of leptogenesis is at a few TeV. With the particle mass at the TeV scale, the model remains promising for collider experiments, particularly through signatures such as prompt decays and displaced vertex searches. ### [106] [New Predictions for the Lifetimes of Doubly Heavy Baryons and the $B_c$ Meson](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04967)
*Lovro Dulibić,Blaženka Melić,Ivan Nišandžić*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文更新了所有弱衰变双重重子（包括 $bb$、$cc$、$bc$ 重子）及 $B_c$ 介子的寿命预测，纳入了 NNLO 修正、NLO 色磁项修正以及完整的 NLO 重-轻夸克旁观者贡献（含企鹅项），并在多种质量方案下给出了不同自旋组态下的寿命层级关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用算符乘积展开（OPE, operator product expansion）框架，计算了领头维数三贡献的次次领头阶（NNLO）修正、色磁项（chromomagnetic term）的次领头阶（NLO）修正，以及维数六重-轻夸克旁观者贡献（heavy-light quark spectator contributions）的完整 NLO 修正（包括企鹅项）。在 $\overline{\rm MS}$、动能（kinetic）以及 $\Upsilon$ 质量方案中进行了比较计算。对 $bc$ 重子考虑了两种可能的基态双夸克自旋组态 $S_{bc}=0$ 和 $S_{bc}=1$。

Abstract: We present updated predictions for the lifetimes of all weakly decaying doubly heavy baryons, including $bb$, $cc$, and $bc$ baryons, as well as for the $B_c$ meson. The analysis includes NNLO corrections to the leading dimension-three contribution, NLO corrections to the chromomagnetic term, and the complete set of currently known NLO corrections to the dimension-six heavy-light quark spectator contributions, including penguin terms. We also compare the results in the $\overline{\rm MS}$, kinetic, and, where applicable, $Υ$ mass schemes. For the $bc$ baryons, we present predictions for both possible ground-state diquark-spin assignments, $S_{bc}=0$ and $S_{bc}=1$. In the kinetic scheme we obtain the lifetime hierarchies $τ(Ξ^0_{bb})<τ(Ξ^-_{bb})\simeqτ(Ω^-_{bb})$, $τ(Ξ^+_{cc})<τ(Ω^+_{cc})<τ(Ξ^{++}_{cc})$, $τ(Ξ^0_{bc})\lesssimτ(Ω^0_{bc})<τ(Ξ^+_{bc})$ for $S_{bc}=0$, and $τ(Ξ^{\prime\, 0}_{bc})<τ(Ω^{\prime\, 0}_{bc})<τ(Ξ^{\prime\, +}_{bc})$ for $S_{bc}=1$. We also revisit the $B_c$ lifetime and discuss the impact of the newly included Darwin term.

</details>


### [107] [The $T_{bc}$ tetraquarks near the $B\bar{D}$ threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05150)
*Halil Mutuk*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在动力学双夸克模型（dynamical diquark model）框架下，利用格点QCD导出的Σ_g^+(1S) Born–Oppenheimer势，研究了双重味开风味四夸克态（doubly heavy open-flavor tetraquarks）T_{bc}^{(0)}和T_{bc}^{(1)}，求解径向薛定谔方程给出了其质量、超精细劈裂与空间尺度，并分析了阈值附近的共振或束缚态性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究双重味开风味四夸克态（doubly heavy open-flavor tetraquarks）T_{bc}^{(0)}与T_{bc}^{(1)}的质量、超精细结构及其与开味阈值的相对位置，以判断其作为束缚态或共振态的存在性。

Method: 采用动力学双夸克模型（dynamical diquark model），将系统描述为重反双夸克–轻双夸克对（heavy antidiquark–light diquark pair），并利用格点QCD（lattice QCD）计算得到的Σ_g^+(1S) Born–Oppenheimer势描述两者之间的相互作用，进而求解径向薛定谔方程（radial Schrödinger equation）。

Result: 标量态（scalar state）T_{bc}^{(0)}的质量为7.143–7.158 GeV，轴矢态（axial-vector state）T_{bc}^{(1)}的质量为7.217–7.222 GeV，超精细劈裂（hyperfine splitting）Δ_{HF}约为59–79 MeV。平均分离距离⟨r⟩≈0.45–0.46 fm，逆半径⟨1/r⟩^{-1}≈0.33–0.34 fm。标量态基本位于B\bar D阈值处，轴矢态位于B^{*}\bar D阈值之上23–28 MeV，低于B\bar D^{*}约70 MeV。

Conclusion: 超精细劈裂主要由对称与反对称重反双夸克构型之间的质量差主导，色磁相互作用（chromomagnetic interaction）的贡献满足∂Δ_{HF}/∂κ_{\bar b\bar c}=2，与重反双夸克自旋代数（heavy-antidiquark spin algebra）一致。空间尺度较弱依赖参数，支持紧凑的双夸克–反双夸克图像。标量态可能表现为弱衰变束缚四夸克或窄的近阈值共振，轴矢态则被一致预测为S波共振，其线型受B^{*}\bar D阈值的强烈影响。

Abstract: We study the doubly heavy open-flavor tetraquarks $T_{bc}^{(0)}$ ($J^{P}=0^{+}$) and $T_{bc}^{(1)}$ ($J^{P}=1^{+}$) in the dynamical diquark model, describing the system as a heavy antidiquark--light diquark pair interacting through the lattice-QCD $Σ_g^+(1S)$ Born--Oppenheimer potential. Solving the radial Schrödinger equation yields $M(T_{bc}^{(0)}) = 7.143$--$7.158$ GeV and $M(T_{bc}^{(1)}) = 7.217$--$7.222$ GeV, with hyperfine splittings of $Δ_{HF}\simeq 59$--$79$ MeV. The splitting is driven mainly by the mass difference between symmetric and antisymmetric heavy-antidiquark configurations, while the chromomagnetic interaction contributes linearly with $\partialΔ_{HF}/\partialκ_{\bar b\bar c}=2$, consistent with heavy-antidiquark spin algebra. The mean separation, $\langle r\rangle\simeq 0.45$--$0.46$ fm, and inverse radius, $\langle 1/r\rangle^{-1}\simeq 0.33$--$0.34$ fm, exhibit weak parameter dependence and support a compact diquark--antidiquark interpretation. Relative to open-flavor thresholds, the scalar state lies essentially at the $B\bar D$ threshold and may appear either as a weakly decaying bound tetraquark or as a narrow near-threshold resonance. In contrast, the axial-vector state is consistently predicted as an $S$-wave resonance located $23$--$28$ MeV above $B^{*}\bar D$ and about $70$ MeV below $B\bar D^{*}$, implying a line shape strongly influenced by the nearby $B^{*}\bar D$ threshold.

</details>


### [108] [On the magnetic counterpart of the Uehling correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04125)
*T. Azevedo,F. A. Barone,C. Farina,R. de Melo e Souza,G. Zarpelon*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在量子电动力学（QED）框架下研究了量子真空的磁性质，计算了虚粒子-反粒子对（virtual particle-anti-particle pair）产生对经典理想点磁铁场的量子相对论修正，发现真空极化（vacuum polarization）诱导的电流使真空表现出顺磁性（paramagnetic medium），并揭示了经典点电偶极子与磁偶极子场之间的对称性在量子层面被打破。最后，将这些修正应用于简单类氢原子超精细结构（hyperfine structure）的计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子真空在经典磁场下的磁性质，特别是量子电动力学（QED）中虚粒子对产生对经典磁场的修正效应。

Method: 在量子电动力学（QED）框架下，计算虚粒子-反粒子对（virtual particle-anti-particle pair）产生对理想点磁铁场的量子相对论修正，进而分析真空极化（vacuum polarization）诱导的电流及相应的电偶极势修正。

Result: 发现真空极化（vacuum polarization）产生的诱导电流使真空表现为顺磁性介质（paramagnetic medium）；经典点电偶极子与磁偶极子场之间的对称性在量子层面被打破；获得了对类氢原子超精细结构（hyperfine structure）的修正贡献。

Conclusion: 量子真空在磁场下表现出顺磁响应，经典的电磁偶极子对称性在量子电动力学（QED）修正下不再成立；该修正可应用于原子超精细结构（hyperfine structure）的理论计算。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the magnetic properties of the quantum vacuum in the context of QED. We calculate the quantum relativistic correction of virtual particle--anti-particle pair creation to the field of a classical point-like idealized magnet. Using such correction, we find the induced currents stemming from the effect of the polarization of the vacuum, which behaves like a paramagnetic medium. We also calculate the correction to the electric dipole potential and show that the well-known symmetry between the classical fields of point electric and magnetic dipoles is broken at the quantum level. Lastly, we apply the corrections to calculate the contributions of the hyperfine structure in a simple hydrogen-like atom.

</details>


### [109] [Pressure-Energy Equations of State of the Nucleon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04163)
*Keh-Fei Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从引力形状因子（gravitational form factors）和能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor, EMT）守恒出发，推导了核子（nucleon）中的压力-能量状态方程，识别出静态和动态两种不同的压力-能量分量，并指出这些关系在第二类超导体（type-II superconductors）中的涡旋（vortices）以及宇宙学的ΛCDM模型中也同样成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在从量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）的基本框架出发，系统建立核子内部压力与能量密度之间的精确状态方程，并探究这些关系在不同物理系统中的普适性。

Method: 该方法基于引力形状因子对能量-动量张量（EMT）矩阵元的参数化，结合EMT守恒定律，将压力（pressure）和能量密度（energy density）分解为Lorentz迹部分（trace part）和无迹部分（traceless part），分别导出对应的状态方程。

Result: 论文发现两种不同的压力-能量分量：静态部分源自EMT的Lorentz迹部分，空间应力1/3 T^{ii}等于负的相应迹部分能量密度；动态部分源自空间应力张量的无迹部分，其压力等于1/d（d为空间维度）倍的相应无迹部分能量密度。总压力由这两部分平衡。此外，这些状态方程同样适用于第二类超导体的涡旋（对应Cooper对凝聚体耗散引起的静态关系）以及宇宙学ΛCDM模型（对应宇宙学常数引起的静态关系）。

Conclusion: 论文指出，由迹反常（trace anomaly）和σ项（sigma-term）诱导的压力在QCD的禁闭动力学（confinement dynamics）中起基础性作用；同时，压力-能量状态方程在核子、超导体和宇宙学系统中的一致性表明，这类关系可能具有超越具体体系的普适性。

Abstract: The pressure-energy equations of state in the nucleon are derived from the gravitational form factors, which parameterize matrix elements of the energy-momentum tensor (EMT), together with EMT conservation. There are two distinct components in the pressure and energy densities. The static pressure distribution arising from the Lorentz trace part of the EMT, as manifested in the spatial stress 1/3 $T^{ii}$, is equal to minus the corresponding trace part of the energy density. This relation may be interpreted as resulting from the depletion of the gluon and quark condensates through the stress-volume relation. This trace-anomaly and sigma-term induced pressure plays a fundamental role in the confinement dynamics of QCD. In contrast, the dynamic pressure distribution from the traceless part of the spatial stress tensor equals 1/d of the corresponding traceless part of the energy density, where d is the spatial dimension. The total pressure is balanced by these two components of the pressure. We point out that the same pressure-energy relations also hold for vortices in type-II superconductors, where the static pressure-energy relation arises from the depletion of the Cooper-pair condensate. Furthermore, these equations of state are identical to those in the $Λ$CDM model of cosmology, where the static pressure-energy relation arises from the cosmological constant.

</details>


### [110] [Emergence of conformal properties in Finite Grand Unified Theories via reduction of couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04378)
*Luis Enrique Reyes Rodríguez,Myriam Mondragón*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了Zimmermann耦合约化（Reduction of Couplings, RoC）方法在超对称（SUSY）规范场论中的应用，证明满足全阶有限性条件的SUSY模型会表现出共形（conformal）行为，并发现软破缺（soft-breaking）扇区中由RoC导出的标量质量求和规则（sum rule）可避免速子（tachyonic）质量谱，进而为维度ful软超对称破缺（SSB）扇区中的参数约化与反常介导（anomaly-mediated, AMSB）模式之间的关联提供了新证据，并指出此类全阶有限模型需具备与无标度超引力（no-scale SUGRA）中一致的Kähler势形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 场论中过多的自由参数影响可预测性，Zimmermann的RoC方法可建立重整化群（renormalization group）不变的耦合关系以减少参数。将其应用于超对称大统一理论（SUSY GUT），特别是构建可全阶避免紫外发散（UV-divergence）的可预测模型，是本文的主要动机。

Method: 基于RoC方法，在尺度不变（scale-invariant）框架下分析满足全阶有限性（all-loop finiteness）条件的SUSY模型；考察超势（superpotential）算符如何与RoC兼容并诱导共形（conformal）行为；进一步分析软破缺扇区中由RoC导出的尺度不变关系，特别是标量质量求和规则，并将这些关系与反常介导超对称破缺（anomaly-mediated SUSY breaking, AMSB）模式进行对比；最后假设有限大统一理论（finite GUT）与有效N=1、d=4 Weyl不变超引力（Weyl-invariant SUGRA）之间存在联系。

Result: RoC方法在软破缺扇区导出了无标度软耦合与无量纲参数之间的一组关系，其中的标量质量求和规则与典型的AMSB关系高度相似，但因求和规则的存在避免了速子质量谱。这为维度ful SSB扇区中的参数约化与AMSB-like模式之间的内在联系提供了新证据。此外，具备该性质的全阶有限模型要求Kähler势（Kähler potential）具有特定形式，该形式与无标度超引力（no-scale supergravity）中研究的结构一致。

Conclusion: RoC方法不仅可在尺度不变框架下有效减少SUSY模型的参数，还可将软破缺扇区的参数约化与AMSB-like模式联系起来，同时通过求和规则解决速子质量问题。该研究进一步揭示了全阶有限SUSY GUT与Weyl不变超引力及无标度超引力之间的深层结构关联。

Abstract: Zimmermann's Reduction of Couplings (RoC) method is a powerful tool for addressing the problem of the excess of parameters in a field theory, as it yields relations among couplings that are invariant under the renormalization group. Its usefulness becomes particularly evident when constructing predictive supersymmetric GUT models that are free of UV-divergences to all orders. Within this scale-invariant framework, we show that a SUSY model satisfying the conditions of all-loop finiteness exhibits a conformal regime induced by superpotential operators compatible with the RoC. In the soft-breaking sector, the method was shown to lead to a set of scale-invariant relations between the soft couplings and the parameters of the dimensionless sector, among which a sum rule for the scalar masses is particularly notable. These relations closely resemble the typical AMSB relations, while avoiding the tachyonic mass spectrum thanks to the sum rule. Based on this observation, we provide new evidence for a connection between the reduction of parameters in the dimensionful SSB sector and the emergence of an anomaly-mediated (AMSB-like) pattern, under the assumption that the finite Grand Unified Theory is connected to an effective $N=1$, $d=4$ Weyl-invariant SUGRA theory. In this process, we find that an all-order finite model with this property requires a specific form of the Kähler potential, whose structure coincides with that studied in no-scale supergravity scenarios.

</details>

### [111] [A framework for modeling and inferring tracer diffusion in crowded environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04216)
*Jinseok Lee,Tong Lin,Mengyang Gu,Yimin Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验、模拟和机器学习相结合的方法，研究了软颗粒悬浊液及活细胞内刚性示踪粒子的扩散行为，建立了一个基于几何结构变量快速预测均方位移（MSD）的并行部分高斯过程（PPGP）模型，揭示了示踪粒子输运主要由可及孔径（accessible pore size）决定，且不同的全局结构可能产生难以区分的MSD。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拥挤环境中的示踪粒子扩散对生物及软物质系统至关重要，但目前缺乏将示踪粒子运动与环境结构联系起来的定量框架。

Method: 通过实验观测刚性示踪粒子在软颗粒悬浊液和活细胞中的输运行为；开发包含空间排斥（steric exclusion）和水动力学阻碍（hydrodynamic hindrance）的最小模拟模型；利用模拟输出训练并行的部分高斯过程（parallel partial Gaussian process, PPGP）模型，以从矩阵几何变量（面积分数、粒子尺寸、多分散性）快速预测均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）。

Result: PPGP模型的预测速度比模拟和实验快数个数量级；示踪粒子输运主要由可及孔径（accessible pore sizes）控制；不同的全局结构可能产生无法区分的MSD；该最小模型也能捕捉细胞内吞示踪粒子的MSD。

Conclusion: 所建立的框架能够实现对拥挤环境（包括细胞内环境）中结构性质的快速推断，为连接结构-输运关系提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Tracer diffusion in crowded environments is central to many biological and soft matter systems, but quantitative frameworks for linking tracer motion to environmental structure remain limited. Here, we study the transport of rigid tracers in suspensions of soft particles and within living cells. Experiments reveal a transition from diffusive to confined motion as the matrix area fraction increases. We develop a minimal simulation that incorporates steric exclusion and hydrodynamic hindrance to reproduce the observed mean-squared displacements (MSDs). Using simulation outputs, we train a parallel partial Gaussian process (PPGP) model that rapidly predicts MSDs from matrix geometric variables, including area fraction, particle size, and polydispersity. The PPGP model accelerates predictions by several orders of magnitude relative to simulation and experiments. Analysis reveals that tracer transport is primarily governed by accessible pore sizes and that distinct global structures can produce indistinguishable MSDs. We find that the minimal model can also capture the MSDs of internalized tracer particles in cells. The framework enables rapid inference of structural properties in crowded environments, including transport in the intracellular environment.
