### [112] [Polyamorphism in Glassy Network Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04273)
*Max Hall-Brown,Peter Guy Wolynes*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过一个简化的微观模型，结合随机一阶跃迁（RFOT）理论，研究了网络液体（network liquids）中多态性（polyamorphism）与玻璃态行为之间的相互作用，揭示了热力学反常与玻璃态动力学反常之间的联系，并预测了近玻璃化转变温度（T_g）下的非经典纳米成核动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络液体在低温高压下会出现多态性现象，但以水为代表的多态性相变因过冷水快速结晶和低温玻璃化效应而难以直接研究。本文旨在通过构建一个可直接计算玻璃态与热力学性质的微观模型，阐明多态性与玻璃态性质之间的相互影响。

Method: 提出一个简单的微观模型，通过调节微观参数使液-液相变（liquid-liquid phase transition）位于玻璃化转变（glass transition）之上、附近或之下，并应用随机一阶跃迁（Random First Order Transition, RFOT）理论分析模型的玻璃态动力学与热力学性质。

Result: 模型在参数调节至类似水的相图时，液-液相变在玻璃化转变温度附近以"纳米成核（nanonucleation）"机制发生，导致极小的畴尺寸和非经典成核动力学，该预测由RFOT理论导出。同时揭示了水类似的热力学反常与玻璃态动力学反常之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 该微观模型及其与RFOT理论的结合，为理解网络液体中多态性与玻璃态行为的相互作用提供了关键细节，展示了玻璃态动力学如何改变相变动力学路径。

Abstract: One dramatic feature of network liquids is the emergence at low temperatures and high pressures of polyamorphism, where multiple distinct liquid phases are accessed in a single material. Polyamorphism can arise from the competition between distinct local inherent structures corresponding to bonded and nonbonded ordering. Thermal bond breaking thus can lead to a phase transition often accompanied by thermodynamic anomalies away from the transition itself, such as the familiar density maximum in water at atmospheric pressure and $4^\circ$ C. Water exhibits network interactions in the form of hydrogen bonding between water molecules. The polyamorphic transition in water, however, is difficult to study due to the rapid crystallization of supercooled water and due to glassy effects at low temperatures. In the present work, we propose a simple microscopic model where the glassy and thermodynamic properties are both calculated directly from the microscopic potentials. The model contains a liquid-liquid phase transition, which, after tuning the microscopic parameters, may be located either above, near, or below the glass transition. By applying the Random First Order Transition theory of the glass transition to this simple microscopic model, we shine light on the interplay of polyamorphism and glassy properties in network liquids. We show the connection between the thermodynamic water-like anomalies and corresponding anomalies in the glassy kinetics. The analysis unveils key details on the way glassy dynamics modifies the phase transition kinetics. When the parameters of the model are tuned to produce a phase diagram resembling that of water, the liquid-liquid phase transformation near $T_g$ occurs via ``nanonucleation'', resulting in extremely small domains sizes and nonclassical nucleation kinetics which are predicted from the RFOT theory.

</details>

*Frank Smallenburg*

Method: 采用标准模拟方法（standard simulation methods）对单分散硬球体系进行模拟，以再现亚稳态流体自发成核（spontaneous nucleation）并演化为稳定流体-晶体共存（fluid-crystal coexistence）的完整过程。

Result: 标准模拟方法能够成功模拟单分散硬球体系中亚稳态流体向稳定流-晶共存态的自发成核过程。

Abstract: In a recent article [J. G. Wang, U. Dhumal, M. E. Zakhari, and R. N. Zia, AIChE Journal 72, e70275 (2026).], the authors discuss the absence of simulations of monodisperse hard spheres in which a metastable fluid spontaneously nucleates into a stable fluid-crystal coexistence. Here, we show that such a simulation can be readily accomplished with standard simulation methods.

### [114] [Macromolecular tribology at flowing solid/liquid interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04318)
*Malo Velay,Jean Comtet*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 结合宽场单分子显微镜（wide-field single-molecule microscopy）与微流控输运（microfluidic transport），直接追踪单个荧光标记PEG大分子在固液界面上的纳米尺度动力学，揭示其在不同表面上的平衡与非平衡输运行为，并解析分子级摩擦、流体滑移与构象异质性之间的耦合机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大分子/表面相互作用在宏观层面已得到广泛表征，但在分子尺度、特别是非平衡条件下的理解仍然有限。本研究旨在直接观测单个大分子在固液界面上的纳米动力学，以揭示其与界面水力学流动的微妙耦合。

Method: 将宽场单分子显微镜与微流控输运技术相结合，对单个荧光标记的PEG大分子吸附物进行直接追踪，分析其在平衡态和流动条件下的纳米尺度动力学行为。

Result: 在平衡态下，大分子在亲水玻璃表面呈现异质性非布朗扩散（non-Brownian diffusion），在疏水自组装单分子层表面则表现为二维类布朗输运（bidimensional Brownian-like transport）。在疏水表面上，外加流动导致一种混合摩擦模式：吸附链在固体壁上摩擦的同时，被近表面流体通过界面滑移（interfacial slippage）持续拖曳。此外，个体链间摩擦系数分布广泛，归因于构象异质性（conformational heterogeneities）与缓慢的重组时间尺度。

Conclusion: 通过联合分析平衡与非平衡输运，精细解析了大分子与固体表面及界面液体之间的分子级摩擦相互作用。所建立的方法为流动固液界面处的大分子摩擦和吸附物/表面相互作用提供了新颖的分子层面图像。

Abstract: Molecular-scale interactions between solvated macromolecules and solid surfaces govern a large number of processes, from biology to engineering. Yet, despite extensive characterization at the macroscopic level, our molecular understanding of polymer/surface interactions remains limited, particularly under out-of-equilibrium conditions. Here, we combine wide-field single-molecule microscopy with microfluidic transport to directly track the nanoscale dynamics of individual fluorescently tagged macromolecular PEG adsorbates, and investigate their subtle couplings with interfacial hydrodynamic flows. At equilibrium, we evidence marked surface dependence, with macromolecular dynamics switching from heterogeneous non-Brownian diffusion on hydrophilic glass to bidimensional Brownian-like transport in an interfacial physisorbed state on hydrophobic self-assembled monolayers. While for hydrophilic glass, the effect of the flow is restricted to an advective contribution during solvent-mediated flights, we uncover for the hydrophobic surfaces a peculiar regime of mixed macromolecular friction, whereby the adsorbed chain rubs on the solid wall while being continuously dragged by the near-surface hydrodynamic flow through interfacial slippage. Through joint analysis of equilibrium and out-of-equilibrium transport, we finely disentangle these molecular level frictional interactions with both the solid surface and the interfacial liquid. Beyond population-averaged dynamics, we further unveil a broad distribution of friction coefficients associated to individual chains, which we attribute conformational heterogeneities with sluggish reorganization timescale. By enabling direct observations of molecular-scale interfacial dynamics, our approach provides a novel molecular picture of macromolecular friction and adsorbate/surface interactions at flowing solid/liquid interfaces.

</details>


### [115] [Pattern Formation and Stick-Slip Dynamics in Binary Particle Assemblies with Rotating Drives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04322)
*C. Reichhardt,C. J. O. Reichhardt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了一个由两种粒子组成的二元排斥相互作用系统，其中一种粒子受旋转驱动，另一种受恒定驱动或异相旋转驱动。研究发现，随着旋转频率变化，系统呈现出多种有序-无序相变（order-disorder transition）和图案形成态（pattern forming state），包括密度调制条纹、部分堵塞态、相分离流体和混合流体，并表现出显著的模式切换行为和传输曲线的跳跃式变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究二元排斥系统中不同驱动方式（旋转驱动与恒定驱动/异相旋转驱动）下，旋转频率如何调控系统的有序-无序相变、图案形成态及输运特性，并揭示拓扑序（topological order）变化与传输行为之间的关联。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，对一个具有排斥相互作用的二元粒子系统进行研究。系统中一种物种受旋转驱动（rotating drive），另一种受恒定方向驱动或与之异相的旋转驱动。通过改变旋转频率并引入有限温度（finite temperature）条件，观察系统的相行为和模式切换。

Result: 发现了多种有序-无序相变与图案形成态，包括密度调制条纹（density-modulated stripe）、部分堵塞态（partially jammed state）、相分离流体（phase separated fluid）和混合流体（mixed fluid）。低频率时出现模式切换的相分离通道，通道趋向于旋转净方向；传输曲线在相变处出现跳跃，并与拓扑序变化对应。高频时若旋转轨道小于粒子平均间距，系统再次出现图案化流动。有限温度削弱切换行为，但部分堵塞态仍可通过局部密度增强引发再结晶（recrystallization）。

Conclusion: 旋转驱动的频率是调控二元排斥系统有序-无序转变和图案形成的关键参数；模式切换行为在不同排斥相互作用势下具有普适性，且即使在高温液态背景下，部分堵塞态仍能诱导局部再结晶。

Abstract: We numerically examine a binary system of particles with repulsive interactions, where one species is driven by a rotating drive and the other is subjected either to a constant drive in a fixed direction or to a rotating drive that is out of phase with the first species. As a function of rotation frequency, we find a variety of order-disorder transitions and pattern forming states, including density-modulated stripes, partially jammed states, phase separated fluids, and mixed fluids. When one species has a constant drive and the drive on the other species is rotated at low frequencies, the system switches between different pattern forming phase-separated lanes including density-modulated stripes and partially jammed states, similar to what is observed for oppositely driven colloids. The lanes tend to align with the net direction of rotation, resulting in a series of order-disorder switching transitions. The transport curves show abrupt jumps up or down at the transitions, which also correspond with changes in the topological order. We find similar switching transitions when both species rotate out of phase with each other. For intermediate driving frequencies, the system becomes increasingly fluid-like and the laning behavior is lost. At high frequencies, however, the system can again exhibit patterned flow when the rotation orbits become smaller than the average spacing between particles. The switching is reduced when a finite temperature is included, but even for temperatures at which the uniform equilibrium bulk system is liquid, the partially jammed state can generate local density enhancements that lead to recrystallization. We demonstrate the pattern switching behavior for systems with different screened repulsive interaction potentials.

### [116] [Diffusiophoretic dispersion of a colloidal blob in porous media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04424)
*Aditya R. Pujari,Amir A. Pahlavan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验与模拟发现，在多孔介质中，扩散泳（diffusiophoresis）对胶体宏观分散（dispersion）的影响与直觉预期相反：吸引（attractive）条件下纵向分散增强，排斥（repulsive）条件下分散反而被抑制。这一反转源于胶体在快慢流线间的扩散泳交换，并通过一个简化的两层模型加以解释。研究还探讨了几何无序（geometric disorder）对该机制的调节作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预测和控制胶体（colloid）在多孔介质（porous media）中的输运对污染物修复和药物递送等应用至关重要。溶质梯度（solute gradient）普遍存在且可能驱动扩散泳迁移，但其对宏观胶体分散的影响尚不明确。

Method: 采用实验与数值模拟相结合的方法，研究扩散泳如何改变胶体团块（colloidal blob）在二维有序/无序多孔介质中的扩散行为。通过引入高浓度胶体与盐的混合团块进入低浓度盐介质并施加背景流动（background flow），观察吸引和排斥条件下的分散变化，并构建了一个最小两层模型（minimal two-layer model）来捕捉快慢塞状流（plug flow）之间的粒子交换。

Result: 吸引条件下纵向分散（longitudinal dispersion）增强，排斥条件下分散被抑制，与直觉预期相反。数值模拟揭示该反转源于粒子在快慢流线间的扩散泳交换。几何无序程度对上述机制具有调节作用。

Conclusion: 扩散泳能显著调节多孔介质中胶体的宏观分散行为，对地下环境和生物环境中的输运过程具有重要启示意义。

Abstract: Predicting and controlling the transport of colloids in porous media is essential for applications ranging from contaminant remediation to drug delivery. In these complex environments, solute gradients are ubiquitous and could drive diffusiophoretic particle migration, yet their impact on macroscopic colloid dispersion remains poorly understood. Here we combine experiments and simulations to quantify how diffusiophoresis alters the spreading of a colloidal blob in a 2D ordered/disordered porous medium. A joint blob of colloids and salt at high concentration is introduced into a medium filled with salt at low concentration and advected by a background flow. Intuition suggests that when colloids are attracted toward or repelled from the solute-rich blob, dispersion should be suppressed or enhanced, respectively. Instead, we observe the opposite trend: longitudinal dispersion is enhanced in the attractive case, whereas dispersion is suppressed in the repulsive case. Numerical simulations reveal that this striking reversal arises from diffusiophoretic exchange of particles between slow and fast streamlines, which we capture using a minimal two-layer model of coupled fast and slow plug flows. Finally, we probe how geometric disorder in the medium modulates this mechanism. Our results demonstrate that diffusiophoresis can strongly modulate macroscopic dispersion of colloids in porous media with implications for transport in subsurface and biological environments.

### [117] [Loop Extrusion Reversal by Condensin Motor is Mediated by Catch Bonds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04482)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单分子磁镊实验发现SMC家族成员凝聚蛋白（condensin）在环挤压过程中存在偶然的反向步进（backward step）现象，导致已挤出的环长缩短。为了同时揭示正向与反向步进的机制，需要发展相应的理论模型。

Method: 采用随机动力学模型（stochastic kinetic model）并结合环挤压的收缩机制（scrunching mechanism），建立了描述正向与反向步进的理论框架。

Result: 该理论定量再现了实验中测得的力依赖的步长（step size）和停留时间分布（dwell time distribution）。预测了一个由ATP驱动的中间态（intermediate state）的存在，该中间态被平衡于正向或反向步进之间，其寿命随外力增加先上升至临界值后下降。

Conclusion: 在亚皮牛顿（sub-piconewton）力作用下，主动马达（active motor）的寿命不降反升，这一现象是捕获键（catch bond）的特征。凝聚蛋白中存在类似捕获键的中间态，不仅扩展了对环挤压机制的理解，也强调了机械力在基因组组织调控中的重要性。

Abstract: Structural Maintenance Complexes (SMC) are energy consuming motors that are important in folding the genome by loop extrusion (LE) in all stages of the cell cycle. Single molecule magnetic tweezer pulling experiments have revealed that condensin, a member of the SMC family involved in mitosis, takes occasional backward steps, thus coughing up the gains in the length of the extruded loop. To reveal the mechanism of the forward and backward steps simultaneously, we developed a theory using the stochastic kinetic model and the scrunching mechanism for LE. The calculations quantitatively account for the measured force-dependent step size and dwell time distributions in both the directions. By postulating the existence of an intermediate state in the ATP-driven cycle that is poised to take a forward or a backward step, we predict that its lifetime increases as the external mechanical force increases till a critical value and subsequently decreases at higher forces. The surprising finding of lifetime increase in an active motor, at sub-piconewton forces, is the characteristic of catch bonds, known in force-induced rupture of several passive protein complexes. The identification of catch bond-like states in condensin not only expands our understanding of LE but also highlights the significance of mechanical forces in regulating genome organization.

### [118] [Predicting the Brittle-to-Ductile Transition in Amorphous Polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04753)
*Valeriy V. Ginzburg,Oleg Gendelman,Alessio Zaccone*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脆-韧转变（BDT）是非晶和半结晶聚合物的重要特性，但目前缺乏一个能同时关联聚合物化学、样品历史、变形类型和应变率的简单模型来统一描述BDT。

Method: 构建了一个标量模型（scalar model）来描述粘-弹-塑性（visco-elasto-plastic）剪切应力-应变曲线随温度和应变率的变化；基于该模型推导出均匀粘塑性流动（uniform viscoplastic flow）存在的应变率上限，并将该上限定义为BDT；进一步假设该上限与Johari-Goldstein β-弛豫时间（beta-relaxation time）成反比；利用“广义Sanchez-Lacombe两态两时间尺度”（SL-TS2）模型计算了三种聚合物的BDT。

Result: 对于聚苯乙烯（polystyrene）、聚甲基丙烯酸甲酯（poly(methylmethacrylate)）和聚氯乙烯（poly(vinylchloride)）三种聚合物，模型计算的BDT与实验数据吻合良好。

Conclusion: 所提出的简单标量模型能有效描述聚合物的BDT行为，且BDT的应变率上限与β-弛豫时间存在直接的物理关联。

Abstract: Brittle-ductile transition (BDT) is an important characteristic of amorphous (and semicrystalline) polymers. For a given strain rate, at temperatures above BDT, the polymers exhibit strain softening followed by yield and strain hardening, while at temperatures below BDT, the same materials exhibit brittle failure at relatively low strains. Surprisingly, today there is no simple model describing BDT as a function of polymer chemistry, sample history, deformation type, and strain rate. Experimental data suggest that BDT is often, though not always, associated with the beta-transition. We formulate a simple scalar model to describe the visco-elasto-plastic shear stress-strain curves as functions of temperature and strain rate. We also show that within this model, there is always an upper bound on the strain rate where the material can have a uniform viscoplastic flow; this upper bound is taken to represent the BDT. We stipulate that this upper bound is inversely proportional to the Johari-Goldstein beta-relaxation time. Using our "general" Sanchez-Lacombe "two-state, two-(time)scale" (SL-TS2) model, we compute the BDT for three polymers (polystyrene, poly(methylmethacrylate), and poly(vinylchloride)) and found a good agreement with experimental data.

TL;DR: 本文通过耦合格子玻尔兹曼方法（lattice Boltzmann method）与离散元方法（discrete element method），模拟了蒸发驱动下球形胶体颗粒（colloidal particles）的自组装过程，揭示了流体与颗粒动力学的复杂相互作用，构建了关于蒸发速率、颗粒间摩擦系数和颗粒数的相图，并发现尽管摩擦力在量级上远小于其他力，却对最终堆积构型具有不成比例的重大影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 构建了覆盖广泛参数范围的相图（regime diagram），识别出开放（open）、闭合（closed）和最小转动惯量（minimal moment of inertia）三类团簇构型对应的参数区域。定量揭示了颗粒间摩擦力在量级上虽远小于其他作用力，却能对最终堆积结果产生不成比例的强烈影响。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过调控蒸发过程中胶体颗粒的动态演化轨迹，有望实现对团簇构型的有效调控。该工作为理解蒸发驱动自组装中多力耦合机制提供了深层理论依据，并为先进胶体材料的理性设计提供了指导。

Abstract: Complex colloidal cluster morphologies are desirable for the fabrication of advanced materials, such as photonic crystals and meta-materials, and can be formed through evaporation-driven packing. By coupling lattice Boltzmann and discrete element methods, here we elucidate the rich interplay between fluid and particle dynamics during evaporation-driven self-assembly of spherical colloidal particles. We construct a regime diagram for a wide range of evaporation rates, interparticle friction coefficients, and particle numbers, identifying parameter regimes for open, closed, and minimal moment of inertia cluster configurations. Analyzing the competition between capillary, hydrodynamic, normal, and friction forces, we show that interparticle friction can exert a disproportionately strong influence on the final packing outcome despite being considerably smaller in magnitude than other forces at play. Our simulation results further highlight the potential for tuning colloidal cluster configurations via their dynamic trajectories.

Abstract: Isolated microscopic magnetic particles are used to induce local perturbations in dense colloidal suspensions by rotating an external magnet. ### [121] [Nonlinear phonon dispersion in disordered solids and non-Debye vibrational spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04986)
*Edan Lerner,Eran Bouchbinder*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文揭示，无序固体（包括弹性网络和多种玻璃）中声子色散的非线性源于一种介观尺度的无序诱导长度尺度，该长度尺度同时控制波衰减；并定量确定了非线性声子软化与非声子振动对非德拜反常和玻色峰的相对贡献，发现二者比重强烈依赖于无序强度（如玻璃形成的热历史），对于真实实验室玻璃，两种机制共同显著贡献于玻色峰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析（analysis）和大规模计算机模拟（large-scale computer simulations）相结合，研究弹性网络（elastic networks）和多种玻璃（glasses）中的声子行为。

Result: 发现非线性的声子色散源自一种介观尺度（mesoscopic）的无序诱导长度尺度（disorder-induced lengthscale），该尺度也控制波衰减（wave attenuation）；非线性声子软化（nonlinear phonon softening）与非声子振动（non-phononic vibrations）对非德拜反常和玻色峰的贡献大小强烈依赖于无序强度（strength of disorder），例如玻璃形成的热历史（thermal history）。

Conclusion: 对于实际实验室玻璃，非线性声子色散与非声子振动两者均显著贡献于玻色峰，这一发现是对理解无序固体的基本进展。

Abstract: All solids, whether crystalline or disordered, support elastic wave propagation with a linear dispersion relation in the long-wavelength limit. These waves, corresponding to low-frequency phonons, feature a vibrational density of states that follows Debye's classical model. Deviations from Debye's predictions with increasing frequency can emerge from phonon dispersion nonlinearity and from non-phononic vibrational modes, which exist in non-crystalline solids due to structural disorder. Both nonlinear phonon dispersion in disordered solids and its relative contribution to non-Debye anomalies, most notably manifested by the controversial boson peak, remain poorly understood. Here we show that nonlinear phonon dispersion in a broad range of disordered solids, including elastic networks and various glasses, emerge from a mesoscopic, disorder-induced lengthscale, which also controls wave attenuation. We subsequently use analysis and large-scale computer simulations to quantitatively determine the relative contributions of nonlinear phonon softening and non-phononic vibrations to the onset of non-Debye anomalies and to the boson peak. We show that the relative magnitude of the two contributions strongly depends on the strength of disorder of the solid, e.g., controlled by the thermal history upon glass formation, and that for realistic laboratory glasses both pieces of physics significantly contribute to the boson peak. These findings constitute basic progress in understanding disordered solids.

</details>


<div id='physics.chem-ph'></div>

# physics.chem-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [122] [Angular Gausslets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04517)
*Steven R. White*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了球面上的广义高斯小波（generalized gausslets），并将其与径向高斯小波（radial gausslets）逐层组合，构建了一种以原子为中心（atom-centered）的基组，使得电子-电子相互作用具有双指标积分对角形式（two-index integral-diagonal form）。通过多个数值测试验证了其系统收敛性，并结合DMRG方法，在Be原子计算中通过角向函数外推达到约0.1 mH的精度，证明了对第一行原子同时处理静态和动态关联的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始高斯小波（gausslets）在电子结构计算中具有局域性（locality）、正交归一性（orthonormality）、可变分辨率（variable resolution）以及电子-电子相互作用的精确对角近似等优点，但仅适用于一维情形。径向高斯小波将这一思想扩展到原子体系，但由于角向自由度仍由球谐函数（spherical harmonics）描述，原子相互作用在组合基组中仅部分对角化。因此，需要构建一种在球面上也保持上述优良性质的基组，以实现电子-电子相互作用的全对角化。

Method: 在球面上从局域化球面高斯函数出发，利用注入（injection）方法使低角动量（low-$\ell$）子空间精确；再将球面高斯小波与径向高斯小波按壳层（shell by shell）组合，形成以原子为中心的基组。同时，针对该基组发展了DMRG方法，包括紧凑型矩阵乘积算符（compact MPOs）、关联小空间起始态（correlated small-space starting states）、Givens旋转在不同角向大小间的转移（Givens-rotation transfers），以及嵌入式采样方差外推（embedded sampled variance extrapolation, ESVE）。

Result: 动能谱（kinetic spectrum）、低$\ell$ Coulomb矩阵元、球电子（spherium）、第一行原子Hartree-Fock计算以及He原子的精确对角化等测试结果均显示，随着角向分辨率的提高，系统收敛性得到验证。在Be原子的DMRG计算中，固定径向分辨率、仅对角度函数数量进行外推，能量精度达到约0.1 mH，接近完备基组极限（complete basis set limit）的精确能量。

Conclusion: 球面高斯小波与径向高斯小波的组合能够在原子体系中将电子-电子相互作用简化为双指标积分对角形式，并保持优异的收敛性。结合所发展的DMRG技术，该方法可以实现对第一行原子中静态关联（static correlation）和动态关联（dynamic correlation）的同等处理，具备实际应用可行性。

Abstract: Gausslets are one of the few basis constructions for electronic structure that combine locality, orthonormality, variable resolution, and an accurate diagonal approximation for the electron-electron interaction, but the original construction is tied to one dimension. Radial gausslets extended this idea to atoms while leaving the angular degrees of freedom in spherical harmonics, so the atomic interaction remained only partially diagonal in the combined basis. Here we introduce generalized gausslets on the sphere and combine them shell by shell with radial gausslets to form an atom-centered basis in which the electron-electron interaction takes a two-index integral-diagonal form. The angular basis starts from localized spherical Gaussians and uses injection to make a low-$\ell$ spherical-harmonic subspace exact. Tests of the kinetic spectrum, low-$\ell$ Coulomb matrix elements, spherium, first-row Hartree--Fock calculations, and He exact diagonalization show systematic convergence with increasing angular resolution. We also develop DMRG methods for this basis, including compact MPOs, correlated small-space starting states, Givens-rotation transfers between nearby angular sizes, and embedded sampled variance extrapolation (ESVE). We show that this combination of ingredients can be used to solve the Be atom, with extrapolations in the number of angular functions but with fixed radial resolution, to within about 0.1 mH of the complete basis set limit exact energy. This shows that DMRG calculations of first row atoms which include both static and accurate dynamic correlation on the same footing are feasible.

</details>

### [123] [SemiConLens: Visual Analytics for 2D Semiconductor Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04067)
*Kavinda Athapaththu,Shiwei Chen,Yuan Fang,Sanchali Mitra,Yee Sin Ang,Yong Wang*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为 SemiConLens 的可视分析（visual analytics）方法，通过结合人类专家知识与机器学习（ML），解决现有二维半导体材料发现中数据稀疏、可靠性不足等问题，并实现了有效且可信的候选材料筛选与比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统二维半导体发现方法（如密度泛函理论 DFT 或基于机器学习的方法）面临小数据集、可靠性与可信度不足等挑战，亟需一种结合人类专家知识与机器学习优势的手段来提升发现效率与可信度。

Method: 首先提出一种新的相关性感知多变量插补（Correlation Aware Multivariate Imputation, CAMI）方法，并结合自动编码器（autoencoder）等 ML 模型，从有限数据中学习并揭示不确定性，以解决半导体性预测中的稀疏数据问题；在此基础上构建包含三个可视化视图及其联动交互的可视化模块，支持材料研究人员交互式地过滤、发现和比较二维半导体候选材料；引入新型圆形字形（circular glyph）设计与聚类感知布局优化（cluster-aware layout optimization）方法，以展示每个候选材料的关键属性及预测不确定性。

Result: 通过定量评估、专家访谈和用例分析，证明了 SemiConLens 能够帮助材料研究人员有效发现所需的二维半导体材料。

Conclusion: SemiConLens 作为一种结合人类专业知识与机器学习能力的可视分析方法，能够有效应对二维半导体发现中的数据稀疏与可靠性挑战，为材料研究人员提供可信赖的候选材料筛选与比较工具。

Abstract: The past few years have witnessed vibrant efforts in discovering new two-dimensional (2D) semiconductor materials from both academia and the industry, due to their promising potential in resolving the severe performance deterioration of traditional semiconductors resulting from condensed silicon thickness. However, existing methods (e.g., Density Functional Theory (DFT) or machine-learning-based approaches) suffer from various challenges such as small datasets, and reliability and trustworthiness issues. To bridge this gap, we propose SemiConLens, a visual analytics approach to combine human expertise with the power of ML to enable effective and reliable 2D semiconductor discovery. Specifically, we first develop a new Correlation Aware Multivariate Imputation (CAMI) method and use ML models like autoencoder, which can better learn from limited data and reveal uncertainty, to address the challenge of sparse data in semiconductivity prediction. Built upon this, our visualization module, consisting of three visualization views with linked interactions, allows material researchers to interactively filter, discover and compare 2D semiconductor candidates. A novel circular glyph design and a new cluster-aware layout optimization approach are proposed to effectively display all the user-configurable key attributes and possible prediction uncertainties of each semiconductor candidate, ensuring a reliable and trustable 2D semiconductor discovery. We assess SemiConLens through quantitative evaluations, expert interviews, and use cases. The results demonstrate SemiConLens's capability to help material researchers conduct effective discovery of desirable 2D semiconductors.

</details>

### [124] [Stability and dynamics of dark-bright solitons in spin-orbit- and Rabi-coupled binary Bose-Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04441)
*K. Rajaswathi,R. Ravisankar,R. Radha,P. K. Mishra,P. Muruganandam*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了带有自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和拉比耦合（Rabi coupling）的一维二元玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中暗亮孤子（dark-bright solitons）的稳定性与非线性动力学，揭示了两种耦合对系统可积性、基态相图及非平衡动力学的不同影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在含合成自旋-轨道和拉比耦合的多分量量子气体中，非线性激发（如孤子）的稳定性与动力学行为尚不清晰，缺乏系统性的理论表征。

Method: 将无自旋-轨道耦合情形映射到可积的Manakov模型获得精确孤子解；采用虚时传播（imaginary-time propagation）和Bogoliubov-de Gennes分析表征基态相与激发谱；通过实时模拟研究有限规范场和相互作用淬火（interaction quench）驱动的非平衡动力学。

Result: 有限自旋-轨道耦合通过诱导自旋相关相位梯度破坏可积性，导致自旋分量空间分离并产生内禀密度振荡；拉比耦合则强制分量间锁相，支持稳定的呼吸子（breather-like）激发。非平衡动力学展现出多孤子碎裂、呼吸条纹斑图（breathing stripe patterns）和孤子动力学等丰富非线性现象。

Conclusion: 合成规范场（synthetic gauge field）、外部约束（external confinement）和相互作用工程（interaction engineering）三者协同，可作为控制多分量量子气体中非线性激发稳定性与动力学行为的有效工具。

Abstract: We investigate the stability and nonlinear dynamics of dark-bright solitons in a one-dimensional binary Bose-Einstein condensate subjected to synthetic spin-orbit and Rabi couplings. In the absence of spin-orbit coupling, we map the coupled Gross-Pitaevskii equations onto the integrable Manakov model and obtain exact dark-bright soliton solutions, providing a rigorous theoretical benchmark. We demonstrate that finite spin-orbit coupling breaks integrability by inducing spin-dependent phase gradients, which result in spatial separation of the spin components and the emergence of intrinsic density oscillations. By contrast, Rabi coupling enforces phase locking between components and supports robust breather-like excitations. Using imaginary-time propagation together with Bogoliubov-de Gennes analysis, we systematically characterise ground-state phases and excitation spectra for both symmetric and asymmetric interaction regimes in homogeneous and harmonically trapped systems. Real-time simulations further demonstrate that finite gauge fields and interaction quenches drive the system far from equilibrium, giving rise to diverse nonlinear phenomena, including multi-soliton fragmentation, breathing stripe patterns, and soliton dynamics. Our results highlight the interplay of synthetic gauge fields, external confinement, and interaction engineering as powerful tools for controlling the stability and dynamical behaviour of nonlinear excitations in multicomponent quantum gases.

### [125] [Geometrical control of topology with orbital angular momentum modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05002)
*Yunjia Zhai,Anselmo M. Marques,Ricardo G. Dias,Verònica Ahufinger,David Viedma*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了通过调节一维交错晶格（staggered lattice）中位点间的相对角度来控制其拓扑性质，揭示了该Creutz梯子模型（Creutz ladder model）中拓扑相变与缠绕数（winding number）的关系，并提出了光子波导（photonic waveguide）系统中的实验实现方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何通过简单调节轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）$l=1$的一维交错晶格中的位点相对角度，来实现对系统拓扑性质的有效控制。

Method: 将原始系统在合成维度（synthetic dimension）中解构为Creutz梯子模型，通过解析和数值方法分析不同跳跃强度（hopping strength）下的拓扑相区，并利用缠绕数（winding number）与能带反转（band inversion）作为拓扑标记进行表征。

Result: 发现通过改变梯子角度可以进入不同的拓扑相区，确定了各相区中拓扑保护边缘态（topologically protected edge state）的数目，并验证了能带反转与缠绕数计算结果的一致性。

Conclusion: 在光子波导系统中实现了拓扑相变（topological transition）的可观测表现——光传播行为的突变，从而为拓扑光学的实验研究提供了可行的平台。

Abstract: We study how the topological properties of a one-dimensional staggered lattice, loaded into states with orbital angular momentum $l=1$, can be controlled simply by tuning the relative angle between sites. The original system under consideration can be depicted as a Creutz ladder model when unwrapping the different state circulations in a synthetic dimension. Depending on the hopping strengths of the chain, different topological regimes may be accessed by changing the ladder angle, as determined by the value of the winding number of the chain. We analytically and numerically explore the different available regimes, and determine the number of topologically protected edge states that exist in each case. We also study the emergence of band inversion across topological transitions and show that it agrees with the winding number calculations, thus serving as an additional topological marker. Then, we propose a realistic experimental implementation in a photonic waveguide system, where the topological transition manifests as a sudden change of the behavior of the propagation of light in the system.

### [126] [A dynamical approach to Schur's Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04121)
*Sonia L'Innocente,Francesco G. Russo,Ilaria Svampa*

Main category: math.GR

TL;DR: 本文通过拓扑熵（topological entropy）概念，将 Schur 经典定理（离散群若中心商有限则导子群有限）推广到拓扑 Hausdorff 群，证明 Z-群（Z-group）若具有有限拓扑熵的连续自同态，则其闭导子群也具备相同性质，从而建立 Schur 定理的动力学版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典 Schur 定理（Schur's Theorem，1904）表明：若无限离散群 E 的中心商 E/Z(E) 有限，则其导子群 [E,E] 有限。该定理在群论中影响深远，但原版本局限于离散群。本文旨在将其推广到拓扑 Hausdorff 群（topological Hausdorff groups），借助拓扑熵（topological entropy）这一动力学概念建立 Schur 定理的动力学对应版本。

Method: 采用 Adler、Konheim 和 McAndrew 提出的拓扑熵（topological entropy）定义（源于 Kolmogorov 与 Sinai 在动力系统领域的直觉）。首先分析具有紧致闭导子群的最大几乎周期群（maximal almost periodic groups）的连续自同态的拓扑熵，这类群的性质由 Takahashi（1952）揭示，其中包含 Grosser 与 Moskowitz 定义的 Z-群（Z-group）。然后基于此给出 Schur 定理的新动力学解释。

Result: 证明了一个动力学版本的 Schur 定理：若 Z-群 G 具有有限拓扑熵（finite topological entropy）的连续自同态，则其闭导子群 $\overline{[G,G]}$ 也具备连续自同态且拓扑熵有限。此外，通过一系列构造与例子阐明了该结果与原始 Schur 定理的关联。

Conclusion: 本文通过拓扑熵建立了 Schur 定理在拓扑群框架下的动力学推广，所给出的构造与示例表明该动力学版本可以视为原始 Schur 定理的自然泛化（generalization）。

Abstract: A classical result of Schur of 1904 shows that an infinite (discrete) group $E$ with finite central quotient $E/Z(E)$ should have finite derived subgroup $[E,E]$. Schur's Theorem has many important consequences, which have been extensively investigated in the literature. Here we focus on topological Hausdorff groups, which are not necessarily discrete groups, and show a dynamical version of Schur's Theorem via the notion of topological entropy of Adler, Konheim and McAndrew. Their perspective follows some original intuitions of Kolmogov and Sinai from the area of the dynamical systems. Firstly, we investigate the topological entropy of continuous endomorphisms of maximal almost periodic groups whose closed derived subgroup is compact. The properties of these groups were known to Takahashi in 1952 and among them we find the $\mathsf{Z}$-groups of Grosser and Moskowitz. Secondly, we give a new dynamical interpretation of the Schur's Theorem, showing that a $\mathsf{Z}$-group $G$ with continuous endomorphisms of finite topological entropy should have closed derived subgroup $\overline{[G,G]}$ with continuous endomorphisms of finite topological entropy. Finally, we illustrate a series of constructions and examples, which allow us to justify our interpretation of Schur's Theorem as generalization of the original version.

</details>

Method: 基于高保真相场模拟构建数据集；采用自编码器神经网络（auto-encoder neural networks）结合主成分分析（principal component analysis, PCA）进行降维；使用长短期记忆网络（Long Short Term Memory, LSTM）进行下一帧预测，并提及门控循环单元（Gated Recurrent Unit, GRU）作为时间序列分析的备选方法。

Analyses demonstrated that the association of auto-encoder neural networks and principal component analyses leads to ensure efficient and significant dimensionality reduction: 1/196 of reduction ratio with more than 80% of accuracy. These findings give insight to apply analyses on data from the latent dimension. Application of Long Short Term Memory (LSTM) neural networks showed the possibility of making next frame predictions; that makes possible the acceleration of Phase-Field simulation without the need of high computing resources. We discussed the application of such a framework on various areas of research. Different methods are proposed from the conducted analyses, in order to ensure dimensionality reduction, including auto-encoders, principal component analysis and Artificial Neural Networks, and time-series analysis, including LSTM and Gated Recurrent Unit (GRU).

### [128] [Improving FMQA via Initial Training Data Design Considering Marginal Bit Coverage in One-Hot Encoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04825)
*Taiga Hayashi,Yuya Seki,Kotaro Terada,Yosuke Mukasa,Shuta Kikuchi,Shu Tanaka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对因子分解机二次退火（FMQA）方法在离散优化中因初始采样不均导致的参数学习不充分问题，提出了通过拉丁超立方采样（LHS）和Sobol'序列实现完整边缘比特覆盖的改进方案，并在无人机翼型优化基准上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准FMQA在通过独热编码（one-hot encoding）处理整数或离散化连续变量时，均匀随机初始采样会导致许多二元变量（binary variables）在初始训练数据中从未被激活（active），对应的因子分解机（FM）参数无法从观测响应中获得直接的梯度更新，从而影响代理模型的拟合质量。

Method: 设计初始训练数据以实现完整边缘比特覆盖（complete marginal bit coverage），即确保每个经独热编码得到的二元变量至少有一次取值为1。采用两种空间填充采样（space-filling sampling）方法：拉丁超立方采样（LHS）和Sobol'序列，分别得到LHS-FMQA和Sobol'-FMQA。

Result: 在17变量和32变量的人力飞行器翼型形状优化基准（human-powered aircraft wing-shape optimization benchmark）上，两种提出的方法均取得了数值上高于基线FMQA的平均最终巡航速度（mean final cruising speed），且在32变量问题上的优势更为显著。

Conclusion: 通过空间填充采样实现初始数据的完整边缘比特覆盖，可以有效改善FMQA在离散优化中的性能，尤其在高维（32变量）问题上提升效果更为明显。

Abstract: Factorization machine with quadratic-optimization annealing (FMQA) is a black-box optimization method that combines a factorization machine (FM) surrogate with QUBO-based search by an Ising machine. When FMQA is applied to integer or discretized continuous variables via one-hot encoding, uniform random initial sampling can leave many binary variables never active in the initial training data, and the corresponding FM parameters receive no direct gradient updates from the observed responses. We address this by designing the initial training data to achieve complete marginal bit coverage, namely, ensuring that every binary variable obtained by one-hot encoding takes the value one at least once. We use two space-filling sampling methods, Latin hypercube sampling (LHS) and the Sobol' sequence, yielding LHS-FMQA and Sobol'-FMQA. On the human-powered aircraft wing-shape optimization benchmark with 17 and 32 design variables, both proposed methods achieved numerically higher mean final cruising speeds than the baseline FMQA, with the advantage more pronounced on the 32-variable problem.

### [129] [Estimating the expected output of wide random MLPs more efficiently than sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05179)
*Wilson Wu,Victor Lecomte,Michael Winer,George Robinson,Jacob Hilton,Paul Christiano*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需实际采样即可估计多层感知机（MLP）在初始化状态下对高斯输入的期望输出的方法，利用累积量（cumulants）和埃尔米特展开（Hermite expansions）近似各层激活分布，在宽网络下相比蒙特卡洛采样（Monte Carlo sampling）能以更少FLOPs达到同等均方误差，尤其擅长估计稀有事件概率，并可用于模型训练以降低灾难性尾部风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器学习中估计期望损失最常用的方法是采样并取经验平均，但采样并非最优方式。本文旨在探索一种在不实际运行样本通过网络的情况下，直接估计期望输出的方法，从而提高计算效率。

Method: 针对初始化状态下的MLP和高斯输入，利用累积量和埃尔米特展开等工具，近似表示每一层激活值的分布（approximate representations of the distributions of activations），从而在不执行前向传播采样的条件下估计网络的期望输出。

Result: 理论和实验表明，对于足够宽的网络，该方法在达到目标均方误差（mean squared error）时所需的FLOPs远少于蒙特卡洛采样；尤其在估计稀有事件概率（probabilities of rare events）时表现优异，且可应用于模型训练过程。

Conclusion: 该研究工作为构建具有更低灾难性尾部风险（catastrophic tail risks）概率的模型提供了一条可行路径，展示了基于分布近似而非采样的估计方法在机器学习的潜力。

Abstract: By far the most common way to estimate an expected loss in machine learning is to draw samples, compute the loss on each one, and take the empirical average. However, sampling is not necessarily optimal. Given an MLP at initialization, we show how to estimate its expected output over Gaussian inputs without running samples through the network at all. Instead, we produce approximate representations of the distributions of activations at each layer, leveraging tools such as cumulants and Hermite expansions. We show both theoretically and empirically that for sufficiently wide networks, our estimator achieves a target mean squared error using substantially fewer FLOPs than Monte Carlo sampling. We find moreover that our methods perform particularly well at estimating the probabilities of rare events, and additionally demonstrate how they can be used for model training. Together, these findings suggest a path to producing models with a greatly reduced probability of catastrophic tail risks.

</details>

### [130] [Super Krawtchouk Polynomials via Lie Superalgebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04301)
*Plamen Iliev,Songhao Zhu*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文基于一般线性李超代数（general linear Lie superalgebra）的表示理论（representation theory），发展了多元超Krawtchouk多项式（multivariate super Krawtchouk polynomials）的理论，将其从经典Krawtchouk多项式推广到超对称情形，并证明了正交性、构造了递推关系，讨论了其在量子力学费米子福克空间（fermionic Fock-space）框架中与球带函数（zonal spherical functions）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，Krawtchouk多项式（Krawtchouk polynomials）的多元扩展因与概率论（probability）、表示论（representation theory）和量子可积性（quantum integrability）的新联系而受到广泛研究。本工作旨在利用一般线性李超代数的表示理论，将经典Krawtchouk多项式的已有结果推广到超对称（super）情形，建立多元超Krawtchouk多项式的理论体系。

Method: 采用一般线性李超代数（general linear Lie superalgebra）的表示理论作为核心方法，将经典Krawtchouk多项式的代数构造推广至超对称情形。具体手段包括：利用超代数表示来定义多元超Krawtchouk多项式，证明其正交性（orthogonality），构造递推关系（recurrence relations），并借助量子力学中的费米子福克空间框架分析其与球带函数（zonal spherical functions）的关联。

Result: 成功推广了经典Krawtchouk多项式，得到了多元超Krawtchouk多项式的正交性证明，构造了相应的递推关系，并揭示了这些多项式与费米子福克空间框架下球带函数之间的内在联系。

Conclusion: 本文通过李超代数表示理论建立了多元超Krawtchouk多项式的完整理论框架，这一推广不仅拓展了经典特殊函数（special functions）理论，还为其在量子力学和量子可积系统中的应用提供了新的代数工具。

Abstract: Multivariate extensions of the Krawtchouk polynomials have been studied by numerous authors in recent decades by exploring new connections to probability, representation theory and quantum integrability. We develop a theory of multivariate super Krawtchouk polynomials using the representation theory of the general linear Lie superalgebra, extending results of the first author in the classical setting. Specifically, in the present work we generalize the classical Krawtchouk polynomials, prove their orthogonality, construct certain recurrence relations, and discuss their connections with zonal spherical functions arising from a fermionic Fock-space framework in quantum mechanics.

</details>

### [131] [High-Power AM-CW Lunar Laser Ranging as a $μ$Hz SGWB Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04110)
*Slava G. Turyshev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证地月系统可作为随机引力波背景（SGWB）的共振探测器，并量化了调幅连续波月球激光测距（AM-CW LLR）在微赫兹频段探测SGWB的能力，展示了在不同测距精度和协方差退化因子下的灵敏度与信号发现潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前微赫兹（μHz）频段的随机引力波背景（SGWB）探测手段有限，而地月系统因其轨道共振特性为该频段提供了独特的探测窗口。本文旨在量化调幅连续波月球激光测距（AM-CW LLR）作为SGWB探针的性能。

Method: 利用地月系统作为共振探测器，分析SGWB在月球轨道频率谐波处的响应；采用调幅连续波月球激光测距（AM-CW LLR）测量GHz调制的1064 nm光载波经月面角反射器返回的射频相位，获取距离（range）和距离变率（range rate）观测量，以此校准SGWB响应灵敏度。

Result: 主导的低偏心率响应位于频率 f₂=0.847245 μHz。绝对距离不确定度为80 μm时，5年观测的有效相位归一化点率 ν_eff=500 yr⁻¹ 下的校准灵敏度为 Ω_gw⁹⁵=5.29×10⁻⁹ D_cov；成熟方案（σ_R=50 μm）则为2.07×10⁻⁹ D_cov。预期的一阶相变（first-order phase-transition）和致密双星（compact-binary）信号在80 μm情形下分别位于5-σ协方差振幅阈值以上（D_cov≲3.6和5.4），在50 μm情形下为D_cov≲9.1和13.7。

Conclusion: 该实验是一种灵敏的协方差检验：绝对距离观测量承载SGWB信号，而距离变率和多反射器差分数据可用于判断干扰参数相关性是否使协方差退化因子（D_cov）保持在发现裕度以下。因此，AM-CW LLR有能力在微赫兹频段实现SGWB的统计显著探测。

Abstract: The Earth--Moon binary is a resonant detector for stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB) at harmonics of the lunar orbital frequency. We quantify high-power amplitude-modulated continuous-wave lunar laser ranging (AM-CW LLR) as a $μ$Hz SGWB probe. The dominant low-eccentricity response is at $f_2=2/P_{\rm M}=0.847245\,μ{\rm Hz}$. AM-CW LLR measures radio-frequency phase on a GHz-modulated 1064 nm optical carrier reflected by lunar corner cubes, giving range and range rate observables. With an $80\,μ{\rm m}$ absolute range uncertainty, a 5-year campaign with statistically independent AM-CW phase-normal-point rate of $ν_{\rm eff}=500\,{\rm yr}^{-1}$ has response-calibrated sensitivity $Ω_{\rm gw}^{95}=5.29\times10^{-9}D_{\rm cov}$; a mature implementation with $σ_R=50\,μ{\rm m}$ gives $2.07\times10^{-9}D_{\rm cov}$, where $D_{\rm cov}\ge1$ is a covariance-degradation factor for time-correlated residuals and nuisance-parameter correlations in the global solution. Anticipated first-order phase-transition and compact-binary signals lie above the nominal 5-$σ$ covariance-amplitude threshold for $D_{\rm cov}\lesssim3.6$ and $5.4$, respectively, in the $80\,μ{\rm m}$ case, and for $D_{\rm cov}\lesssim9.1$ and $13.7$ in the $50\,μ{\rm m}$ case. Thus the experiment is a sharp covariance test: absolute range carries the SGWB signal, while range rate and multi-reflector differential data determine whether nuisance correlations keep $D_{\rm cov}$ below the discovery margins.

</details>


### [132] [Comparative Study of $f(T)$ Gravity Models with Observational Constraints from \textit{OHD} and \textit{Pantheon+ datasets}](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04113)
*Anirudh Pradhan,S. A. Salve,V. B. Raut,S. H. Shekh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对三种不同形式的$f(T)$引力模型（幂律型、指数型和对数型）进行了比较分析，利用哈勃参数和重子声学振荡（BAO）数据通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法约束模型参数，并系统研究了有效能量密度、状态方程参数、平方声速、$Om(z)$诊断以及能量条件等物理行为。结果表明，所有模型在晚期渐近趋近于$Λ$CDM行为，但稳定性和能量条件表现存在差异，其中强能量条件（SEC）的违反是共同特征，与当前宇宙加速膨胀一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙晚期加速膨胀是现代宇宙学中最重大的未解问题之一。修正引力框架（如$f(T)$引力）通过引入扭转效应（torsional effects）为暗能量（dark energy）提供了一种几何替代方案，因此有必要对不同形式的$f(T)$模型进行系统比较，以评估其解释观测数据的能力。

Method: 本研究选取了三种$f(T)$模型形式：幂律型$f(T) = η(-T)^{n}$、指数型$f(T) = βT_{0}\left(1-e^{-p \sqrt{T/T_{0}}}\right)$和对数型$f(T) = γT \ln\!\left(\frac{T}{T_{0}}\right)$。通过参数化减速参数$q(z)$及其对应的$H(z)$表达式，结合最新的哈勃参数和BAO数据，采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法对模型参数进行约束。

Result: 所有三种模型在晚期均渐近趋近于$Λ$CDM行为。三种模型在稳定性属性和能量条件（energy conditions）表现上存在差异；强能量条件（strong energy condition, SEC）的违反是所有模型的共同特征，这与当前宇宙加速膨胀一致。有效能量密度、状态方程参数（equation of state parameter）、平方声速（squared sound speed）以及宇宙学$Om(z)$诊断的物理行为均得到了系统分析。

Conclusion: 不同的$f(T)$函数形式在保持与观测数据一致的前提下，可以产生不同的宇宙学动力学。SEC的违反是三种模型的共同特征，符合当前宇宙加速膨胀的观测事实。该比较分析揭示了$f(T)$模型在解释晚期宇宙加速方面的有效性和多样性。

Abstract: The late-time acceleration of the universe remains one of the most significant open problems in modern cosmology. Modified gravity frameworks such as $f(T)$ gravity provide a geometric alternative to dark energy by attributing cosmic acceleration to torsional effects. In this study, we present a comparative analysis of three different forms of $f(T)$ models: (i) a simple power-law form $f(T) = η(-T)^{n}$, (ii) the exponential form $f(T) = βT_{0}\left(1-e^{-p \sqrt{T/T_{0}}}\right)$ and (iii) a logarithmic form $f(T) = γT \ln\!\left(\frac{T}{T_{0}}\right)$. Using parameterization of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ and the corresponding $H(z)$ expression, we constrain the model parameters with the recent Hubble parameter and BAO data through a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) approach. The physical behavior of the effective energy density, equation of state parameter, squared sound speed, cosmological $Om(z)$ diagnostics, and energy conditions (NEC, DEC, SEC) were investigated for all three models. Our comparative analysis shows that all models asymptotically approach the $Λ$CDM behavior at late times, while they differ in stability properties and energy condition behaviors. In particular, the violation of the strong energy condition (SEC) has emerged as a common feature consistent with current accelerated expansion. This study highlights how different $f(T)$ functional forms can yield distinct cosmological dynamics while maintaining consistency with observational data.

</details>


### [133] [Testing an anisotropic spinor field--based Modified Chaplygin Gas model in Kantowski--Sachs spacetime with observational constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04123)
*Mahendra Goray,Bijan Saha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Kantowski–Sachs时空下构建了一个无质量非线性旋量场（spinor field）耦合修正Chaplygin气体（MCG）的宇宙学模型，利用Pantheon+、宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometers）、DESI DR2和CMB距离先验等观测数据通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）分析约束模型参数。结果显示哈勃常数H₀约67–68 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，剪切参数（shear parameter）与零一致表明晚期宇宙各向同性，模型比ΛCDM更优的χ²和Akaike信息准则（AIC）支持，为暗物质与暗能量统一描述及各向异性提供了可行框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索各向异性（anisotropy）和统一暗扇区动力学（unified dark sector dynamics），在Kantowski–Sachs时空中构建无质量非线性旋量场耦合修正Chaplygin气体的宇宙学模型以统一描述暗物质与暗能量。

Method: 采用修正Chaplygin气体（MCG）作为统一暗扇区组分，耦合无质量非线性旋量场，在Kantowski–Sachs度规下建立模型；利用Pantheon+超新星数据、宇宙计时器、DESI DR2重子声学振荡数据和CMB距离先验，通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）分析约束模型参数。

Result: 哈勃常数H₀约67–68 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹；剪切参数与零一致，表明晚期宇宙有效各向同性（isotropic）；当前减速参数q₀约-0.49，重现晚期宇宙加速膨胀；模型χ²值低于ΛCDM，Akaike信息准则（AIC）显示模型更受数据支持。

Conclusion: 自旋场MCG模型在Kantowski–Sachs时空中提供了一个可行框架，自然融入各向异性并实现暗物质与暗能量的统一描述，与当前观测数据一致。

Abstract: We investigate a cosmological model based on a massless nonlinear spinor field coupled to a Modified Chaplygin Gas (MCG) in the Kantowski--Sachs spacetime, aiming to probe anisotropies and unified dark sector dynamics. The model parameters are constrained using recent observational data, including Pantheon+, cosmic chronometers, DESI DR2, and CMB distance priors, via a Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis. We find $H_0 \sim 67$--$68~\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$, while the shear parameter is consistent with zero, indicating an effectively isotropic Universe at late times. The model reproduces late-time cosmic acceleration with a present-day deceleration parameter $q_0 \sim -0.49$, and provides a good fit to the data, yielding a lower minimum $χ^2$ than $Λ$CDM, and is favored by the Akaike Information Criterion. Overall, the spinor field MCG model in Kantowski--Sachs spacetime offers a viable framework that naturally incorporates anisotropy and a unified description of dark matter and dark energy, consistent with current observations.

### [134] [Unifying the Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli and Bardeen-Press-Teukolsky formalisms on spherical backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04147)
*David Pereñiguez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于自对偶曲率方程（self-dual curvature equations）与球谐展开（spherical harmonic expansions），提出了一套球对称背景上的微扰论（perturbation theory）新框架，统一了Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli (RWZ)与Bardeen-Press-Teukolsky (BPT)两种形式体系，并揭示了拟正规模（quasinormal mode）等谱性（isospectrality）的几何起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 球对称背景上的引力微扰（gravitational perturbation）存在RWZ与BPT两种经典形式体系，各自具有优势但尚未被统一。本文旨在建立一套融合两者优点的统一框架，并揭示自对偶变量在其中的核心作用。

Method: 将自对偶曲率方程与球谐展开相结合，在球对称背景上构建微扰论形式体系；先对一般能动张量（energy-momentum tensor）进行推导，再特化到含物质源的真空广义相对论（General Relativity）以展示其实际优势。

Result: 核心结果表明，RWZ方程与BPT方程直接源自同一张量曲率方程（tensorial curvature equation）的不同分量。在频域（frequency domain）中，度量可由任意主函数（master function）及其导数代数重建；在时域（time domain）中可能存在重建障碍。自对偶变量使拟正规模等谱性（当存在时）得以显式体现。

Conclusion: 本文提出的形式体系成功统一了RWZ与BPT两种框架，揭示了自对偶变量在引力微扰理论中的关键作用。随文发布基于xAct的Mathematica笔记本，可供其他研究者使用该形式体系。

Abstract: We develop a formulation of perturbation theory on spherically symmetric backgrounds based on self-dual curvature equations combined with spherical harmonic expansions. The resulting framework unifies the Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli (RWZ) and Bardeen-Press-Teukolsky (BPT) formalisms and is designed to combine key advantages of both. The use of self-dual variables is crucial, and makes quasinormal mode isospectrality manifest, when present. We present the formalism first for a general energy-momentum tensor, and then specialize to vacuum General Relativity with matter sources to illustrate its practical advantages. A central result is that the RWZ and BPT equations arise directly as different components of a single tensorial curvature equation. We also show that, in the frequency domain, the metric can be reconstructed algebraically from any of the proposed master functions and their derivatives, and we comment on possible obstructions to such a reconstruction in the time domain. A Mathematica notebook, based on xAct, that implements the formalism and was used in our computations is released alongside this work.

</details>


### [135] [A Master Equation for Screening in Luminal Horndeski Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04154)
*Sergi Sirera,Tessa Baker,James Hallam,Krishna Naidoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在亮度（luminal）Horndeski理论框架下，通过α-基（α-basis）系统推导了二阶非线性宇宙学扰动方程，并应用准静态与弱场极限，识别出Vainshtein、Chameleon及一种新型筛选机制（Phaedrus screening），同时发布了两个开源软件包xAlpha和escut，用于从拉格朗日量直接识别活跃筛选机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从一般标量-张量（scalar-tensor）拉格朗日量中确定活跃的筛选机制（screening mechanism）仍是一个具有挑战性的问题，需要发展系统性的诊断工具。

Method: 在平坦FLRW背景下的α-基中，推导并整理未经近似的二阶扰动方程全集，系统施加准静态与弱场极限；针对静态球对称位形导出主筛选方程；开发了xAlpha（Mathematica包）和escut（Python模块）两个开源软件。

Result: 二阶效应仅修正标量场方程；主筛选方程可恢复Vainshtein和Chameleon机制；识别出一种新机制Phaedrus screening，其筛选半径与源质量呈线性标度关系；给出了每种机制的分析解与数值解及其激活条件。

Conclusion: 所开发的软件工具（xAlpha和escut）在多数情况下能够直接从亮度Horndeski拉格朗日量中识别出活跃的筛选类型，为诊断筛选机制提供了系统化手段。

Abstract: Determining the active screening mechanism from a general scalar-tensor Lagrangian remains a challenging problem. As a diagnostic tool, we present a systematic study of nonlinear cosmological perturbations in luminal Horndeski theories. Working in the $α$-basis on a flat FLRW background, we derive and organise the full set of unapproximated second-order perturbation equations, and systematically apply the quasi-static and weak-field limits. We find that second-order effects modify only the scalar field equation. We derive, for static and spherically symmetric configurations, a master screening equation recovering the Vainshtein and Chameleon mechanisms. We also identify a novel regime, which we term Phaedrus screening, characterised by a screening radius that scales linearly with the source mass. For each mechanism, we derive analytical and numerical solutions and clarify the conditions under which they activate. Finally, we introduce two new publicly available software packages: (i) xAlpha, a Mathematica package to compute and organise perturbation equations in scalar-tensor theories, and (ii) escut, a Python module to solve the nonlinear scalar equation. In many cases, these tools enable the identification of the active screening type directly from a luminal Horndeski Lagrangian.

</details>


### [136] [Emergent gravity from nonlinear perturbation of spherical accretion with variable adiabatic index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04158)
*Rohith Ghosh,Souvik Ghose,Biplab Raychaudhuri,Apashanka Das,Tapas K. Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，类比引力现象（analogue gravity phenomena）并非线性微扰的特例，而是可以通过跨音速流体的非线性高阶微扰（non-linear higher order perturbation）涌现。通过将声学度规（acoustic metric）形式扩展到线性 regime 之外，并考虑球对称吸积流（spherically accreting flow）中相对论性、多组分、位置依赖绝热指数的状态方程，研究表明上述微扰满足一个带有非线性修正的协变波动方程，使类比几何（analogue geometry）变得动态化。声学视界（acoustic horizon）的位置会因密度、温度和吸积率涨落的相对振幅而发生向内或向外的移动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有类比引力研究多局限于线性微扰框架，无法确认引力效应是否仅是线性近似的人工产物。本文旨在证明，即使在非线性高阶微扰下，引力类效应（gravity-like effects）依然可以从跨音速流体（transonic fluid）中涌现，从而排除线性近似的偶然性。

Method: 考虑球对称吸积天体物理系统，采用具有相对论性、多组分状态方程（equation of state）且绝热指数（adiabatic index）随位置变化的流体动力学吸积模型。将声学度规形式扩展到线性 regime 之外，推导非线性高阶微扰满足的协变波动方程。

Result: 非线性高阶微扰满足一个在有效声学时空中带有非线性修正的协变波动方程，使类比几何从静态变为动态。声学视界的位置取决于密度、温度和吸积率涨落的相对振幅，可以向内或向外移动。

Conclusion: 类比引力效应不是线性微扰的人为产物，非线性效应使类比时空变得动态，为研究天体物理吸积流中非线性类比时空（non-linear analogue spacetime）的动力学提供了更真实的框架。

Abstract: The main aim of the present work is to demonstrate that the analogue gravity phenomena is not an artifact of linear perturbation, rather gravity-like effects emerge through the non linear higher order perturbation of transonic fluid as well. To establish that fact, a spherically accreting astrophysical system has been considered where the hydrodynamic accretion with a relativistic, multi-component equation of state with position dependent adiabatic index onto compact astrophysical objects has been considered. rate. By extending the acoustic metric formalism beyond the linear regime, it has been shown that the aforementioned perturbations satisfy a covariant wave equation in an effective acoustic spacetime with non-linear corrections, making the analogue geometry dynamical. As a consequence, the acoustic horizon can shift (inward or outward), depending on the relative amplitudes of density, temperature, and mass accretion-rate fluctuations. This provides a more realistic framework to investigate the dynamics of the non-linear analogue spacetime in astrophysically relevant accretion flows.

Method: 采用爱因斯坦-标量-高斯-博内引力（Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity）这一动机良好的引力有效场论（effective field theory），首次进行全非线性黑洞散射模拟，并将所得散射角与有效单体（effective-one-body）解析描述进行对比。

Abstract: The study of hyperbolic binary black hole encounters yields an effective probe of the strong field regime of black holes, thus providing an additional channel to test General Relativity. We study the scattering of two black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity, a well-motivated effective field theory of gravity, by comparing the scattering angle obtained from the first fully nonlinear black hole scattering simulations with its effective-one-body analytic description. We obtain excellent agreement between analytics and numerics, exhibiting accurate capturing of strong-field scalar-gravitational dynamics. Our work paves the way towards semi-analytical waveform templates of compact object binaries in modified theories of gravity.

### [138] [The Impact of Spin Priors on Parameterized Tests of General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04579)
*Tianhao Wu,Shujun Rong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了引力波参数估计中自旋先验（spin priors）对广义相对论参数化检验中1.5PN偏离参数δ\hatφ_3的影响，发现自旋参数χ_p比χ_eff对先验更敏感，而δ\hatφ_3在多数事件中鲁棒但部分短旋进事件呈现显著偏差；进一步揭示了当δ\hatφ_3纳入分析时χ_eff与δ\hatφ_3之间存在强相关性，该相关性由高灵敏度事件子集驱动，表明自旋先验选择可能以非平凡且依赖模型的方式影响GR检验结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋先验（spin prior）在引力波参数估计中具有基础性作用，但其对广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）参数化检验的影响尚未得到充分理解。本文旨在系统探究自旋先验选择如何影响1.5PN偏离参数δ\hatφ_3的推断。

Method: 使用真实引力波事件（gravitational-wave events）数据，通过Jensen–Shannon散度（Jensen-Shannon divergence, JSD）和后验分布的中位数偏移（median shift）定量刻画先验诱导效应；进一步采用留一法检验（leave-one-out test）分析相关性的稳定性。

Result: 有效进动自旋参数χ_p比有效旋进自旋χ_eff对先验敏感度显著更强；δ\hatφ_3在多数事件中表现鲁棒，但事件GW231123_135430的JSD达O(0.4)量级；短旋进时长事件（如GW231028_153006等）的中位数偏移更显著；在标准GR框架下自旋参数与δ\hatφ_3无显著相关性，但纳入δ\hatφ_3后χ_eff与δ\hatφ_3之间出现强相关性。

Conclusion: 自旋先验选择能够以非平凡且依赖模型的方式传播到GR参数化检验中，可能掩盖或重塑表观的GR偏离信号；相关性由部分高灵敏度事件驱动，提示需谨慎处理先验效应对GR检验结果的影响。

Abstract: Spin priors play a fundamental role in gravitational-wave parameter estimation, yet their impact on parameterized tests of General Relativity (GR) remains insufficiently understood. In this work, we systematically investigate how spin prior choices affect the 1.5PN deviation parameter $δ\hatφ_3$ using real gravitational-wave events. We quantify prior-induced effects through the Jensen--Shannon divergence (JSD) and median shifts of posterior distributions. We find that the effective precession spin parameter $χ_p$ exhibits significantly stronger prior sensitivity than the effective inspiral spin $χ_{\rm eff}$. While $δ\hatφ_3$ is generally robust across most events, GW231123\_135430 exhibits a noticeable discrepancy, with a JSD at the $\mathcal{O}(0.4)$ level. Examining the median shift, we note that events with very short inspiral durations, such as GW231028\_153006, GW231123\_135430, and GW191109\_010717, show more pronounced shifts, indicating increased sensitivity in low-information regimes. We further explore the relationship between the prior sensitivity of spin parameters and that of $δ\hatφ_3$. No significant correlation is observed when spin parameters are inferred within the standard GR framework. However, when $δ\hatφ_3$ is included in the analysis, a strong correlation emerges between $χ_{\rm eff}$ and $δ\hatφ_3$, which we attribute to partial parameter degeneracy at the 1.5PN order. A leave-one-out test shows that the observed correlation is sensitive to the inclusion of specific events, indicating that it is partially driven by a subset of high-sensitivity events. Our results demonstrate that spin-prior choices can propagate into parameterized tests of GR in a non-trivial and model-dependent manner, and may mimic or reshape apparent deviations from GR.

Abstract: In this work, we review gravitational-wave generation in a two-scalar-field cosmological model. ### [140] [Nearly universal CMB TT spectrum from pre-inflationary dynamics in a closed universe: KICI scenario, bouncing universe, and emergent universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04755)

Method: 采用相空间分析（phase space analysis）方法对空间闭合宇宙的早期演化进行动力学分类；在此基础上计算各演化路径对应的原始功率谱（primordial power spectrum）和CMB TT谱（CMB TT spectrum）。

Result: 存在一个代表德西特膨胀（de Sitter expansion）阶段的吸引子；宇宙有三种不同的演化路径：KICI（kinetic initial conditions for inflation）场景、反弹宇宙（bouncing universe）和涌现宇宙（emergent universe）。这些模型的原始功率谱和CMB TT谱在大尺度上均受到抑制，且各模型的CMB TT谱完全重叠，无法区分。

Conclusion: 基于CMB TT谱无法区分KICI、反弹宇宙和涌现宇宙这三种演化路径；CMB TT谱在大尺度上的抑制效应及详细形状不依赖于具体的暴胀前动力学（pre-inflationary dynamics）或过渡阶段（transition stage）的存在。

Abstract: We utilize the phase space analysis method to study the early evolution of the spatially closed universe and find that there exists an attractor denoting the de Sitter expansion phase, and that the universe has three distinct evolutionary paths, which correspond to the kinetic initial conditions for inflation (KICI) scenario, bouncing universe, and emergent universe. Based on the results of the phase space analysis, we calculate the primordial power spectrum and CMB TT spectrum for these models. We find that, for these models, the primordial power spectrum and CMB TT spectrum are suppressed at large scales. Moreover, the CMB TT spectra for these models overlap completely, indicating that these models are indistinguishable via their CMB TT spectra, and that the suppression and the detailed shape of the CMB TT spectrum are independent of the specific pre-inflationary dynamics or the presence of a transition stage.

### [141] [Hawking Temperature, Sparsity and Energy Emission Rate of Regular Black Holes Supported by Primordial Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04923)

Result: PDM尺度抑制了霍金温度和光谱能量发射率；固定α的热容在物理支上保持负值，表明正则系综（canonical ensemble）中局部热力学不稳定性持续存在；几何稀疏参数在微扰区域α≪2M中受到负的领头阶修正，导致霍金通量的间歇性（intermittency）略有降低。

Conclusion: 规则黑洞的PDM尺度参数显著影响其热力学和辐射行为，但未能消除系统在正则系综下的局部热力学不稳定性；稀疏参数的负修正表明霍金通量的间歇性有所减弱；同时需区分近地平线几何估计与基于阴影的高能吸收截面（shadow-based high-energy absorption cross-section）在发射率计算中的应用差异。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the thermodynamic and radiative properties of a regular black hole sourced by primordial dark matter (PDM), modeled effectively through a Dirac--Born--Infeld (DBI) scalar field. We compute the Hawking temperature, the entropy obtained from the first law at fixed PDM scale, the specific heat capacity, the sparsity parameter of the Hawking flux, and the spectral energy emission rate. Particular attention is devoted to the role played by the regularity scale parameter \(α\) and to the recovery of the Schwarzschild limit. Using the normalization in which the integration constant \(M\) is the ADM mass and \(f(r)=1-2M/r+\mathcal{O}(r^{-3})\), we find that the PDM scale suppresses the Hawking temperature and the spectral energy emission rate relative to the Schwarzschild case. The fixed-\(α\) heat capacity remains negative along the physical branch, indicating the persistence of local thermodynamic instability in the canonical ensemble. Moreover, within the effective-area prescription adopted here, the geometrical sparsity parameter receives a negative leading correction in the perturbative regime \(α\ll 2M\), implying a slight reduction of the intermittency of the Hawking flux. We also distinguish between the near-horizon geometrical estimate and the shadow-based high-energy absorption cross-section used in the emission rate.

### [142] [Perturbations and greybody bounds of Euler-Heisenberg black holes surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04994)
*Fernando M. Belchior,Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Euler-Heisenberg黑洞（周围分布完美流体暗物质）背景下自旋为0、1和1/2的无质量场传播，通过严谨的Boonserm-Visser下界方法估计灰体因子（greybody factor）和吸收截面，发现非线性电动力学和暗物质参数显著改变有效势垒，导致可区分的透射概率和吸收谱修正。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先推导出标量、电磁和Dirac扰动的类Schrödinger径向方程及有效势；随后采用严格的Boonserm-Visser下界方法估计灰体因子，并由此获取部分吸收截面和能量发射率。

Result: 非线性电动力学和暗物质参数显著改变有效势垒，使透射概率和吸收谱产生可区分的修正；灰体因子下界随频率单调递增并趋近高频极限，低频行为受背景几何和扰动场自旋的强烈影响；与Schwarzschild、Reissner-Nordström和纯EH极限的比较表明，EH+PFDM联合背景产生可区分的散射修正。

Conclusion: 灰体因子下界可作为探测非线性电动力学效应和致密天体周围暗物质晕（dark matter halo）的灵敏诊断探针。

Abstract: We investigate the propagation of massless fields with spins $s=0$, $s=1$, and $s=1/2$ in the spacetime of an Euler-Heisenberg (EH) black hole surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM). This background incorporates both the nonlinear electrodynamic correction associated with the EH effective theory and the logarithmic contribution induced by the surrounding dark matter distribution. After deriving the corresponding Schrödinger-like radial equations, we construct the effective potentials for scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations and analyze how they are modified by the black hole charge, the EH parameter, and the PFDM parameter. The greybody factors are estimated through the rigorous Boonserm-Visser lower-bound method, and the associated partial absorption cross sections are obtained for different spin sectors using these bounds. Our results show that the nonlinear electrodynamic and dark matter parameters significantly deform the effective potential barrier, leading to potentially distinguishable changes in the transmission probabilities and absorption spectra within the model. In particular, the greybody lower bounds increase monotonically with the frequency and approach the high-frequency limit, while their low-frequency behavior is strongly affected by the geometry and by the spin of the perturbing field. Moreover, we utilize the greybody lower bound to calculate the energy emission rate. Finally, we make comparisons with the Schwarzschild, Reissner-Nordström, and pure EH limits, showing that the combined EH+PFDM background produces distinguishable corrections to black-hole scattering within the model. These results highlight greybody bounds as sensitive diagnostic probes of nonlinear electrodynamic effects and dark matter halos around compact objects.

### [143] [Phase Transitions and Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05019)
*Diego Rios,William H. Kinney*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用Fisher矩阵预报方法，分析了未来空间引力波探测器DECIGO和LISA对早期宇宙一阶相变（first-order phase transition）产生的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）的探测能力。基于声波与湍流贡献的引力波频谱模型，对相变强度α和逆持续时间β/H_*两参数进行Fisher分析，发现DECIGO的1σ不确定性约为0.12和0.145，参数高度相关（相关系数~0.98）；LISA的对应不确定性为非对称形式，相关系数~0.78。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙一阶相变产生的随机引力波背景是理解宇宙早期物理过程（如电弱相变）的重要探针。量化未来空间引力波探测器（DECIGO和LISA）对这一信号的参数估计精度，对于评估其科学潜力具有重要意义。

Method: 采用Fisher矩阵（Fisher matrix）预报方法。引力波频谱模型Ω_GW(f)=Ω_sw+Ω_turb由声波与湍流贡献构成，参数化为相变强度α、逆持续时间β/H_*、相变温度T_*和泡壁速度v_w。对每个探测器，固定T_*和v_w，选取信号峰值位于探测器敏感带内的基准模型（fiducial model），对lnα和ln(β/H_*)进行两参数Fisher分析。

Result: 对于DECIGO，两参数Fisher分析给出边际化1σ不确定性σ(lnα)≈0.12和σ[ln(β/H_*)]≈0.145，参数高度相关（corr≈0.98）。对于LISA，边际化1σ不确定性为Δα/α≈⁺⁰·⁰⁴⁴₋₀·₀₄₂和Δ(β/H_*)/(β/H_*)≈⁺⁰·¹¹⁹₋₀·₁₀₇，相关系数corr≈0.78。

Conclusion: DECIGO和LISA均能对早期宇宙一阶相变参数提供有意义的约束，但两参数之间存在显著相关性（DECIGO尤为强烈），这提示联合多探测器或多频段观测可能有助于打破简并，提高参数估计精度。

Abstract: We present a Fisher-matrix forecast for the detectability of a stochastic gravitational wave background generated by a first-order phase transition in the early universe. We use the DECIGO and LISA missions as reference cases. The source gravitational wave spectrum $Ω_{\rm GW}(f)$ is modeled as the sum of sound wave and turbulence contributions and is parameterized by the transition strength $α$, its inverse duration $β/H_*$, its transition temperature $T_{*}$, and the bubble wall velocity $v_{w}$. For each detector, we construct fiducial models with signal peaking in the sensitivity band of the detector, fixing $T_{*}$ and $v_{w}$, and perform a Fisher analysis on the remaining parameters $\lnα$ and $\ln(β/H_{*})$. A two-parameter Fisher analysis in $\{\lnα,\ln(β/H_{*})\}$, with fixed values of $T_{*}$ and $v_{w}$, yields marginalized $1σ$ uncertainties $σ(\lnα)\simeq 0.12$ and $σ[\ln(β/H_{*})]\simeq 0.145$. The parameters are strongly correlated, with correlation coefficient $\mathrm{corr}\simeq 0.98$. We perform a corresponding analysis for LISA and report marginalized $1σ$ uncertainties $Δα/α\simeq {}^{+0.044}_{-0.042}$ and $Δ(β/H_{*})/(β/H_{*}) \simeq {}^{+0.119}_{-0.107}$, with correlation coefficient $\mathrm{corr}\simeq 0.78$.

*Jonathan Ramírez*

TL;DR: 本论文建立了线性依赖X的Φ(R,φ,X)理论与广义混合度规-帕拉蒂尼引力（generalized hybrid metric–Palatini gravity）之间的局部重构框架，在爱因斯坦框架（Einstein frame）的真空中将两者统一为具有相同场空间几何的双标量理论，并给出了两种表述之间的系统转换方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展Φ(R,φ,X)理论与广义混合度规-帕拉蒂尼引力之间的形式化联系，为两种看似不同的修正引力模型提供统一的描述框架，并解决两者在爱因斯坦框架下的等价性问题。

Method: 在爱因斯坦框架真空中将两种理论均表示为具有相同场空间几何的双标量理论，通过推导Clairaut型方程来建立Φ(R,φ,X)与f(R,ℛ)函数之间的对应关系，并引入动力学耦合参数来参数化逆重构中的非唯一性。

Result: 推导出从给定Φ(R,φ,X)模型确定兼容的混合函数f(R,ℛ)的方程，并证明该方程具有Clairaut型结构；发现逆重构不唯一：一个规则混合爱因斯坦框架势能对应一族由动力学耦合参数化的兼容Φ(R,φ,X)理论。

Conclusion: 该重构框架为两种修正引力理论之间的转换提供了实用方法，并通过具体算例验证了重构过程的有效性和参数翻译规则。

Abstract: We develop a local reconstruction framework between $Φ(R,φ,X)$ theories with linear dependence on $X$ and generalized hybrid metric--Palatini gravity. The construction is formulated in vacuum in the Einstein frame, where both formulations can be written as two-scalar theories with the same field-space geometry. The framework provides a practical method for finding $Φ(R,φ,X)$ and $f(R,\mathcal R)$ functions that describe the same regular Einstein-frame two-scalar sector. Starting from a given $Φ(R,φ,X)$ model, we derive the equation that determines the compatible hybrid functions $f(R,\mathcal R)$ and show that it has a Clairaut-type structure. We also show that the inverse reconstruction is not unique: a regular hybrid Einstein-frame potential determines a family of compatible $Φ(R,φ,X)$ theories, parametrized by the kinetic coupling. Explicit examples illustrate the reconstruction procedure, its domain of validity, and the translation of model parameters between the $Φ(R,φ,X)$ and $f(R,\mathcal R)$ formulations.

</details>


### [145] [Quantum gravitational contrast in creating Schrödinger cat state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05153)
*Anupam Mazumdar,Tian Zhou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文展示了一个通过物质波干涉仪（matter-wave interferometer）产生的薛定谔猫态（Schrödinger cat state），可以被视为最简单的同时在微扰水平上平等处理物质与引力的量子引力（quantum-gravity）设定。研究利用有效场论（effective field theory）方法处理广义相对论（general relativity），在非相对论极限下量子化无质量自旋-2引力子（graviton），并分析物质-引力子耦合导致引力子真空位移类似于相干态（coherent state），以及由此产生的干涉对比度、物质与引力子之间的纠缠，并与量子几何的重叠相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种能够同时在微扰层次上平等处理物质与引力的量子引力最小设定，即利用物质波干涉仪中的薛定谔猫态作为研究平台。

Method: 采用有效场论（effective field theory）方法处理广义相对论，在非相对论极限下量子化无质量自旋-2引力子（graviton），并引入量子空间叠加的物质态以构建物质波干涉仪（matter-wave interferometer）。

Result: 物质-引力子耦合导致引力子真空发生位移，位移行为类似于相干态（coherent state）。进一步分析了左右叠加态对应的相干态之间的对比度/重叠（contrast/overlap），并研究了物质与引力子之间的纠缠，将其与引力对比度（gravitational contrast）或相干态所对应的量子几何（quantum geometry）重叠相联系。

Conclusion: 该设定为在微扰层次上同时处理物质与引力的量子效应提供了一个最小模型；物质波干涉仪中的对比度与物质-引力子纠缠及量子几何重叠之间存在内在关联。附录中通过一个含时谐振子（time-dependent harmonic oscillator）示例进一步说明了引力子相干态的对比度/重叠。

Abstract: In this paper, we illustrate how a Schrödinger cat state created via a matter-wave interferometer can be viewed as the simplest quantum-gravity setup where we can treat both matter and gravity on an equal footing at a perturbative level. Here we treat Einstein's theory of general relativity using an effective field theory approach, quantising the massless spin-2 graviton in the presence of a quantum spatial superposition of matter that creates a matter-wave interferometer in the non-relativistic limit. We show that due to the matter-graviton coupling the graviton vacuum is displaced analogous to the coherent state. We study the contrast/overlap between the coherent states of the left and right superpositions in the matter-wave interferometer. We also study the entanglement between matter and the graviton in this setup and relate it to a gravitational contrast, or the overlap of the quantum geometries led by the coherent states. In the appendix, we provide an example of a time-dependent harmonic oscillator and study the contrast/overlap of such coherent states of the graviton.

</details>

### [146] [Search for magnetoacoustic quantum oscillations in the insulating phase of YbB$_{12}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04350)
*Ryosuke Kurihara,Atsuhiko Miyata,Koji Araki,Shusaku Imajo,Ruo Hibino,Atsushi Miyake,Sergei Zherlitsyn,Joachim Wosnitza,Hiroshi Yaguchi,Fumitoshi Iga,Masashi Tokunaga,Yasuhiro H. Matsuda*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过体敏感性超声实验，在高达65 T的磁场和低至485 mK的温度下，对近藤绝缘体（Kondo insulator）YbB$_{12}$中的磁量子振荡（magnetic quantum oscillations）进行了搜索。虽然确认了磁阻（magnetoresistance）与磁热效应（magnetocaloric effect）中存在振荡现象，但未在绝缘态中观察到磁声量子振荡（magnetoacoustic quantum oscillations），仅在场诱导金属态中出现。绝缘态中观察到一些来源不明的超声异常，为理解YbB$_{12}$绝缘态的异常行为提供了新的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体物理学中一个高度反常的现象是在绝缘体中观测到磁量子振荡，这似乎源自费米面（Fermi surfaces），但与绝缘体不存在带电准粒子（charged quasiparticles）的基本概念相矛盾。此前多个研究组在近藤绝缘体YbB$_{12}$中报道了此类振荡。本研究的动机是通过体敏感性超声实验，进一步系统搜索YbB$_{12}$中的量子振荡，以澄清绝缘态中是否存在这类振荡及其来源。

Method: 采用体敏感性超声实验（bulk-sensitive ultrasonic experiments），在高达65 T的强磁场和低至485 mK的极低温条件下进行测量。使用此前已在磁阻中观测到振荡现象的YbB$_{12}$单晶样品，同时测量磁阻（magnetoresistance）和磁热效应（magnetocaloric effect），并重点搜索磁声量子振荡。

Result: 确认了绝缘态中磁阻的振荡行为以及磁热效应中场依赖的振荡。但在绝缘态中未观测到磁声量子振荡，仅在磁场诱导的金属态（field-induced metallic state）中观测到。此外，在绝缘态的超声数据中发现了一些来源不明的异常现象（anomalies）。

Conclusion: 该研究的发现为YbB$_{12}$绝缘态中令人困惑的行为提供了进一步信息。绝缘态中磁阻和磁热效应的振荡与磁声量子振荡的缺失形成对比，暗示这些振荡的可能机制可能并非源自传统的费米面，其物理起源仍需进一步探索。

Abstract: A highly exotic phenomenon in solid-state physics is the observation of magnetic quantum oscillations in insulators. For instance, in the Kondo insulator YbB$_{12}$ various groups reported the observation of such oscillations seemingly originating from Fermi surfaces, though this contradicts the concept of an insulator having no charged quasiparticles. In this study, we searched for quantum oscillations in YbB$_{12}$ by using bulk-sensitive ultrasonic experiments in high magnetic fields up to 65 T and down to 485 mK. For that, we utilized an YbB$_{12}$ single crystal that, in previous experiments, revealed oscillations in the magnetoresistance in the insulating state. We confirmed oscillation-like behavior of the magnetoresistance as well as field-dependent oscillations in the magnetocaloric effect. However, we could not observe magnetoacoustic quantum oscillations in the insulating state, only in the field-induced metallic state. In the insulating state, we found some anomalies in our ultrasound data, the origin of which remains elusive. Our findings provide further information on the puzzling behavior of the insulating state of YbB$_{12}$.

### [147] [Imaging GHz surface acoustic wave modes in electrostricted LaAlO$_3$/SrTiO$_3$ heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04402)
*Ranjani Ramachandran,Sayanwita Biswas,Prithwijit Mandal,Kyoungjun Lee,Madeleine Msall,Chang-Beom Eom,Patrick Irvin,Jeremy Levy,Mingyun Yuan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃（LAO/STO）界面上的表面声波（SAW），在室温下观测到高达2.2 GHz的SAW模式，传播损耗极低（约10⁻³ dB/波长），并通过原子声学力显微镜（AAFM）实现了亚微米分辨率的波形成像，揭示了电致伸缩诱导的SAW产生机制，为在STO平台上实现声电耦合量子器件奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LAO/STO界面可调控的二维电子气（two-dimensional electron gas, 2DEG）为实现弹道电子波导和量子点等量子器件提供了平台，但要将单个电子、电子对及其他奇异态在空间分离的器件之间精确传输，需要有效的调控手段。表面声波（surface acoustic wave, SAW）在GaAs基2DEG中已有成熟应用，然而由于STO在室温下缺乏本征压电性，SAW在STO上的产生与传播尚缺乏系统研究。因此，本文旨在探索LAO/STO体系中SAW的产生机制与传播特性，以拓展其在声电耦合与量子器件中的应用。

Method: 实验上，本研究在LAO/STO界面样品上激发SAW，并测量其高达2.2 GHz的声波模式及传播损耗；利用原子声学力显微镜（Atomic Acoustic Force Microscopy, AAFM）对SAW波形进行亚微米分辨率成像，以直接观察声波形态并分析其产生机制。

Result: 观察到LAO/STO界面在室温下可激发高达2.2 GHz的SAW模式，传播损耗极低，约为10⁻³ dB/波长。AAFM成像实现了对SAW波形的亚微米分辨率可视化。测量结果表明该SAW为剪切水平型（shear horizontal-type）模式，能够耦合到面内自由度。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了STO上SAW激发与传播的基本机制，尤其是通过电致伸缩效应实现声波产生的路径。由于STO是一种广泛使用且商业可得的衬底，这一工作使得SAW能够便捷地耦合到多种可生长或转移至STO上的材料，为后续声电耦合及量子器件应用提供了基础。

Abstract: The LaAlO$_3$/SrTiO$_3$ (LAO/STO) interface hosts a gate-tunable superconducting two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG) which can be programmed to create quantum devices such as ballistic electron waveguides and quantum dots. To fully exploit this platform for quantum transport, a key requirement is the ability to shuttle single electrons, electron pairs, and other exotic states between spatially separated devices with precision. Surface acoustic waves (SAWs), which travel along the surface of a solid, offer a powerful route to achieve this through their moving electrical potential that captures and transfers electrons. %acoustoelectric coupling. In particular, SAWs in the GHz regime enable fast, controlled transport of individual quantum particles. Although this approach is well-explored in GaAs-based 2DEG, SAW generation in STO remains largely unexplored due to the lack of intrinsic piezoelectricity at room temperature. Here, we investigate room-temperature SAWs in LAO/STO and observe SAW modes up to 2.2 GHz with very low propagation loss of the order $10^{-3}$ dB per wavelength. To directly visualize these modes, we employ Atomic Acoustic Force Microscopy (AAFM), achieving sub-micron resolution imaging of the SAW wave forms, providing insight into the electrostriction-induced SAW generation mechanism. Our measurements indicate a shear horizontal-type mode, which provides the ability to couple to in-plane degrees of freedom for future acoustoelectric and quantum device applications. This work studies the fundamentals of SAW excitation and propagation on STO, a widely used and commercially available substrate, enabling straightforward coupling of SAWs to a broad range of materials that can be grown or transferred onto STO.
