### [148] [Second quantization of anyons and spin-anyon duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04538)
*Priyanshi Bhasin,Diptiman Sen,Tanmoy Das*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文为阿贝尔任意子（Abelian anyons）开发了一套一维代数和第二量子化（second-quantization）框架，建立了 $π$/3 任意子与自旋-1 算符之间的精确 Jordan-Wigner 对偶（Jordan-Wigner duality），揭示出任意子密度依赖的通量、不可压缩/无带隙相以及基态电流与关联函数中的临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 任意子（anyons）兼具局域排斥规则与非局域编织/交换相位，导致其交换代数自洽构造和第二量子化（second-quantization）形式面临根本困难。本文致力于为遵守特定统计相位 $θ = π/N$ 的阿贝尔任意子（Abelian anyons）建立严格的代数和量子化框架。

Method: 通过构造一维阿贝尔任意子的代数框架，强制规定最大在位占据数为 N-1，并引入统计相位 $θ = π/N$。进一步推导 $π/3$ 任意子与自旋-1 算符之间的精确 Jordan-Wigner 对偶（Jordan-Wigner duality），将紧束缚任意子模型映射为 XY 型自旋-1 模型。

Result: 该模型展现出任意子密度依赖的有效通量（anyone-density-dependent flux）、不可压缩相（incompressible phases）与无带隙区域（gapless regions），以及能级交叉导致的临界点。这些临界点表现为基态电流、动量、保真度（fidelity）和关联函数中的不连续性。

Conclusion: 所发展的第二量子化形式建立了一种新颖的自旋-任意子对偶（spin anyon duality），为从自旋哈密顿量（spin Hamiltonians）实现任意子及设计相应的器件架构提供了概念上全新的途径。

Abstract: Anyons exhibit a non-trivial interplay between local exclusion rules and non-local braiding and exchange phases, making a consistent commutation algebra and second-quantized formulation challenging. We develop an algebraic framework for Abelian anyons in one dimension with statistical phase $θ$ = $π$/N that enforces a finite on-site occupancy of N-1 anyons with the exchange phase $θ$ between different sites. Moreover, we introduce an exact Jordan-Wigner duality between $π$/3 anyons and spin-1 operators, allowing us to map a tight-binding anyon model to an XY-like spin-1 model. The model exhibits anyon-density-dependent flux, incompressible or gapless regions, and critical points with level crossings that appear as discontinuities in ground-state currents, momenta, fidelities, and correlation functions. Our second-quantization formalism establishes a novel spin anyon duality, offering a conceptually new route to realize anyons from spin Hamiltonians and to engineer corresponding device architectures.

</details>


### [149] [Melting upon cooling in a quantum magnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04611)
*K. Jaksetič,T. Arh,M. Pregelj,M. Gomilšek,M. Dragomir,P. Prelovšek,M. Ulaga,L. Šibav,M. Malovrh,K. Železnikar,Z. Jagličić,P. Manuel,F. Orlandi,D. Khalyavin,M. D. Le,N. Bujault,E. Lhotel,J. van Tol,U. Jena,B. Sana,P. Khuntia,A. Zorko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究报告了一种在阻挫（frustrated）量子磁性材料七钽酸铒（erbium heptatantalate）中观察到的逆熔化（inverse melting）现象：随着温度降低，体系先形成类似固体的长程磁有序，随后在更低温度下“熔化”为类似液体的短程关联自旋条纹态（spin-stripe state），即“自旋波梅兰丘克效应”（spin Pomeranchuk effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索加热导致固体熔化这一常规认知的反例——逆熔化现象，是否在量子磁性体系中存在，从而揭示阻挫磁体中自旋-自旋相互作用（spin-spin interactions）竞争所导致的新奇物相转变机制。

Method: 以伊辛型三角晶格反铁磁体（Ising-like triangular-lattice antiferromagnet）七钽酸铒为研究对象，通过降温实验观测其磁有序结构的变化过程。

Result: 冷却过程中，材料首先形成三子晶格长程磁有序（three-sublattice long-range magnetic order），类似于固体的有序结构；随后在更低温下意外地转变为一个短程关联的自旋条纹态，类似于液体的无序状态，即发生了逆熔化。

Conclusion: 这种“自旋波梅兰丘克效应”可能普遍源于阻挫磁体中自旋-自旋相互作用的强竞争，并为理解奇异磁性相之间的转变提供了新的研究途径。

Abstract: Heating enhances thermal fluctuations and typically leads to melting of solids, but in exceptional cases, heating can also cause liquids to solidify. The paradigm of this counterintuitive phenomenon is solidification of liquid $^3$He upon increasing temperature, known as the Pomeranchuk effect. Here we show that such inverse melting also appears in quantum magnetism. We find that, on cooling, the Ising-like triangular-lattice antiferromagnet erbium heptatantalate first develops a three-sublattice long-range magnetic order -- analogous to a solid -- which then, unexpectedly, melts at even lower temperatures into a short-range correlated spin-stripe state -- analogous to a liquid. We propose that such an unprecedented ``spin Pomeranchuk effect" can generically arise from strong competition between spin-spin interactions in frustrated magnets, and provides a novel avenue to transformations between exotic magnetic phases.

</details>


### [150] [Symmetric estimator for discrete self-energy of discrete many-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04974)
*Aleksandrs Zacinskis,Frank T. Ebel,Mathias Pelz,Fabian B. Kugler,Karsten Held,Jan von Delft,Maurits W. Haverkort,Andreas Gleis*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于Kugler对称改进估计量的离散化，构造了单粒子自能的离散谱表示，该表示在实频率和复频率（Matsubara频率）轴上均能保证因果性，并应用于量子杂质模型和动力学平均场理论（DMFT），显著提高了杂质性质的数值精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准的单粒子自能谱表示方法可能在数值上产生非物理的负谱权重，或需要额外的展宽（broadening）处理，且难以同时保证因果性（causality）与数值精度。

Method: 利用Kugler对称改进估计量（symmetric improved estimator）的离散求值，在实频率轴和复Matsubara频率轴上构造离散谱表示（discrete spectral representation）。该方法适用于任意哈密顿量（Hamiltonian），并进一步在动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）的自洽循环中采用离散杂化函数（discrete hybridization function）进行表述。

Result: 将该表示应用于量子杂质模型（quantum impurity models）和DMFT，在多种数值方法下，杂质性质（impurity properties）的计算精度均获得显著提升。

Conclusion: 所提出的离散谱表示能够在数值层面上天然保证因果性，避免非物理负谱权重或额外展宽问题，是一种高精度且普适的自能数值表示方案。

Abstract: We derive a discrete spectral representation of the single-particle self-energy using a discrete evaluation of Kugler's symmetric improved estimator. Our construction can be used on both the real and the complex (Matsubara) frequency axis. It is guaranteed to remain causal at the numerical level, in contrast to standard approaches that may generate unphysical negative spectral weight or require additional broadening. Our representation can be used for any Hamiltonian; here we apply it to quantum impurity models and in dynamical mean-field theory. The latter is formulated with a discrete hybridization function throughout its self-consistency loop. In both cases and across various numerical methods, we obtain significantly improved accuracy for a range of impurity properties.

</details>


### [151] [Interaction-controlled localization in one-dimensional chain: From edges to domain walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05064)
*Rahul Samanta,Sudin Ganguly,Santanu K. Maiti*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过Hartree-Fock平均场方法研究半填充Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）链中在位（U）和扩展（V）Hubbard相互作用对边缘模式存在与演化的影响，发现局域态由2V/U比值控制，独立于能带拓扑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究半填充SSH链中在位与扩展Hubbard相互作用如何影响边缘模式的存在与演化，明确关联效应对局域态形成的作用。

Method: 采用Hartree-Fock平均场方法（Hartree-Fock mean-field approach），分析能量谱、局域概率振幅以及位点分辨的电荷和自旋密度分布。

Result: 局域态（localized states）的束缚由比值2V/U控制：当U>2V时出现边缘自旋密度波（spin-density-wave）模式，当U<2V时出现链中电荷密度波（charge-density-wave）畴壁，且该行为独立于能带拓扑（band topology）。

Conclusion: 有限一维链中局域态起源于关联效应（correlation-driven origin），而非仅由拓扑决定。

Abstract: Using Hartree-Fock mean-field approach, we study the role of on-site ($U$) and extended ($V$) Hubbard interactions on the existence and evolution of edge modes in a half-filled Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) chain. We analyze the energy spectrum, local probability amplitudes, and site-resolved charge and spin density profiles across topological, critical, and trivial hopping regimes. We find that the localization of bound states is controlled by the ratio $2V/U$, with edge spin-density-wave modes for $U>2V$ and mid-chain charge-density-wave domain walls for $U<2V$, independent of band topology. These results establish the correlation-driven origin of localized states in finite one-dimensional chains.

</details>


### [152] [Microscopic evidence for imaginary charge density wave in a kagome metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05101)
*S. Suetsugu,F. Hori,M. Shibata,S. Kitagawa,K. Ishida,T. Asaba,S. Nakazawa,Q. Li,H. -H. Wen,T. Shibauchi,H. Kontani,Y. Matsuda*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文通过核四极共振（nuclear quadrupole resonance, NQR）谱学实验，在kagome非磁金属CsV₃Sb₅中发现了纯虚电荷密度波（imaginary charge density wave, iCDW）的光谱证据，揭示了手性环电流（chiral loop current）导致的约1 mT局域磁场和自发时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking），从而建立了一种新型量子有序态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无耗散电荷输运是凝聚态物理中最引人入胜的现象之一，除超导体（superconductor）和量子霍尔系统（quantum Hall system）外，手性环电流有序（chiral loop current order）被视为可能的第三类无耗散体系，但其微观起源——虚电荷密度波（iCDW）的存在长期存在争议，亟需直接的微观实验证据。

Method: 研究团队使用位点选择性的核四极共振（NQR）谱学技术，探测kagome非磁金属CsV₃Sb₅中对外平面电流敏感的面外¹²¹Sb位点，分析谱线在磁场下的展宽与非对称线形，以区分磁效应与四极效应（electric quadrupolar effect）对谱线的贡献。

Result: 在温度T*≈120 K（高于实电荷密度波CDW转变温度）以下，NQR谱出现反常展宽；施加磁场后谱线呈现不对称线形，表明展宽纯来自磁效应而非CDW涨落相关的电四极效应。观测到的线形与约1 mT的手性环电流局域场定量一致，证明存在自发时间反演对称性破缺。

Conclusion: 该工作从微观层面识别了长期寻找的纯iCDW，建立了一种新型量子有序态，有望革命性地改变对量子材料中奇异电子态（exotic electronic state）的理解。

Abstract: Dissipationless charge transport without any energy loss is one of the most fascinating phenomena in condensed matter physics. This extraordinary state manifests in two well-established systems: superconductors and quantum Hall systems. A proposed third category is associated with chiral loop current order, characterized by the spontaneous formation of microscopic electric current loops. The microscopic origin of these currents stems from imaginary hopping terms, conceptualized as an imaginary charge density wave (iCDW). Despite extensive investigations, its existence remains highly controversial. Here we report site-selective spectroscopic evidence for a pure iCDW in the kagome nonmagnetic metal CsV$_3$Sb$_5$. Nuclear quadrupole resonance spectra at out-of-plane $^{121}$Sb site sensitive to in-plane currents reveal anomalous broadening below $T^*\approx$120 K, coinciding with the nematic transition well above the real charge density wave (CDW). Under magnetic fields, the spectra exhibit asymmetric lineshapes, demonstrating that this broadening purely originates from magnetic effects rather than from electric quadrupolar effects associated with CDW fluctuations. The observed lineshapes are quantitatively consistent with ~1 mT local fields induced by chiral loop currents, indicating spontaneous time-reversal symmetry breaking. This microscopic identification of the long-sought pure iCDW establishes a novel form of quantum order, potentially revolutionizing our understanding of exotic electronic states in quantum materials.

</details>


### [153] [Dynamical correlations in a dissipative XXZ spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05162)
*Cătălin Paşcu Moca,Doru Sticlet,Ovidiu I. Pâţu,Balazs Dóra*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文研究了耗散XXZ自旋链中，在均匀自旋损失与泵浦作用下的动力学自旋关联函数。在有限磁化的混合稳态基础上，纵向关联函数重现了从弹道、KPZ超扩散到扩散的输运普适类层次，但在有限磁化下额外叠加了磁子传播导致的弹道光锥。横向关联函数在易平面情形下呈现指数衰减，各向同性点遵循KPZ标度，易轴区表现为弹道传播。全林德布拉德动力学下，早期普适类保持，长时极限中关联函数受到整体指数衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解耗散开放量子系统中自旋动力学关联函数的普适类行为，特别是在有限磁化稳态背景下的非平衡输运性质与普适类分类。

Method: 采用矢量化的TEBD（vectorized TEBD）进行数值模拟，同时利用Pfaffian表示（Pfaffian representation）和第三量子化框架（third-quantization framework）对非相互作用XX情形获得精确解析结果。

Result: 在纯幺正演化下，纵向关联函数重现了自旋输运的普适类层次（弹道、KPZ超扩散、扩散），有限磁化下额外叠加磁子传播的弹道光锥。横向关联函数在易平面情形呈指数衰减，各向同性点遵循KPZ标度，易轴区为弹道传播。全林德布拉德动力学下，早期普适类保持，长时关联呈指数衰减。

Conclusion: 耗散XXZ自旋链在有限磁化稳态上展现出丰富的动力学关联行为，既有封闭系统下的普适类输运层次，又受到耗散效应带来的指数衰减修正，为理解开放量子多体系统的非平衡普适类提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study dynamical spin correlations in a dissipative XXZ spin chain subject to uniform local spin-loss and pumping. Starting from a mixed steady state that is featureless albeit possessing finite magnetization, rich dynamics emerges in time-dependent two-point correlators evaluated on top of it. For unitary evolution in which the reservoir is absent, the longitudinal correlators reproduce the established hierarchy of spin-transport universality classes - ballistic, Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) superdiffusive, and diffusive - across the phase diagram. However, for finite magnetization, additional ballistic light cone propagation gets superimposed on the previous universality classes, arising from magnon propagation.The transverse correlator displays very fast, exponential decay of correlations without wavefront propagation in the easy-plane case. At the isotropic point, it follows KPZ scaling due to $SU(2)$ symmetry, while in the easy-axis regime, it is characterized by ballistic spreading of correlations. Under full Lindbladian dynamics, the universality classes are preserved at early times, while the correlations acquire an overall exponential damping in the long-time limit. In terms of methods, we have used vectorized TEBD for numerical simulations and exact analytical results obtained via a Pfaffian representation and the third-quantization framework for the noninteracting XX case.

</details>


### [154] [Frustrated magnetic order in hybrid Kitaev spin-orbital models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05196)
*Ivan Dutta,Aayush Vijayvargia,Anamitra Mukherjee,Onur Erten,Kush Saha*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了两类独立可精确求解的自旋液体哈密顿量（Kitaev六角格点模型与正方格点模型，以及Yao-Lee模型与正方格点模型）在共同格点环境下的混合行为。通过自洽平均场和微扰计算发现，强Kitaev耦合会在自旋（spin）部分产生磁序，而轨道（orbital）部分保持拓扑序；当Yao-Lee与正方格点耦合等大反向时，模型恢复精确可解性并出现单一巡游马约拉纳（Majorana）味。这表明混合自旋液体平台可承载超越传统可解极限的新奇涌现相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实材料中常存在竞争相互作用，破坏Kitaev模型的精确可解性并可能催生新相。受近期关于共存的Yao-Lee与Kitaev耦合的微观理论提案启发，探索将两个原本定义在不同晶格上的精确可解自旋液体哈密顿量置于同一格点环境中的基态行为。

Method: 采用自洽平均场分析（self-consistent mean-field analysis）和微扰计算（perturbative calculation）对混合模型进行理论分析；具体研究了Kitaev六角格点-正方格点混合模型以及Yao-Lee-正方格点混合模型。

Result: 强Kitaev耦合区域中，自旋扇区出现磁序（magnetic order），轨道扇区保持拓扑序（topological order）。Yao-Lee与正方格点模型中展现出马约拉纳狄拉克能带（Majorana Dirac bands）的丰富演化和利夫希茨相变（Lifshitz transitions）。当Yao-Lee与正方格点耦合等大反向时，模型恢复精确可解性，仅保留单一巡游马约拉纳味（itinerant Majorana flavor）。

Conclusion: 混合自旋液体平台（hybrid spin liquid platforms）可以承载超越传统精确可解极限的多种涌现相（emergent phases），为设计新型自旋液体材料提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Spin-orbital generalization of Kitaev model provides a robust extension to the original Kitaev model. However, real materials often exhibit competing interactions that break exact solvability which can give rise to new phases. Motivated by recent microscopic proposals of coexisting Yao-Lee and Kitaev couplings, we investigate the fate of the ground state when two independent exactly solvable spin liquid Hamiltonians each originally formulated on different lattice geometries are combined on a common lattice environment. We first focus on the hybrid Kitaev's honeycomb and square-lattice model. Using self-consistent mean-field analysis and perturbative calculation, we show that the strong-Kitaev regime yields magnetic order in the spin sector, while the orbital sector retains its topological order. We further analyze the hybridization of the Yao-Lee and square-lattice models and find that the model exhibits a rich evolution of Majorana Dirac bands and Lifshitz transitions. Remarkably, when the Yao-Lee and square-lattice couplings are equal and opposite, the model restores its exact solvability with a single itinerant Majorana flavor. These results demonstrate that hybrid spin liquid platforms may host various emergent phases beyond conventional exactly solvable limits.

</details>

### [155] [Tropical resolutions of configuration hypersurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04252)
*Daniel Bath,Graham Denham,Mathias Schulze,Uli Walther*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种两步法，用于对任意不可约配置超曲面（configuration hypersurface）进行奇点消解（resolution of singularities），方法结合了Nash blow-up的正规化、Bloch引入的incidence variety、以及基于双置换多面体拟阵（bipermutohedral matroid）组合学构造的tropical紧化（tropical compactification），并证明了该正规化Nash blow-up在正特征下具有强F-正则奇点（strongly $F$-regular singularities），在复数域上具有有理奇点（rational singularities）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 配置多项式（configuration polynomial）推广了图的Kirchhoff多项式和Feynman积分的Symanzik多项式，但对应的配置超曲面（configuration hypersurface）通常具有高度奇异性（highly singular），这给Feynman积分的计算带来了挑战。本文旨在提供一种系统的方法来消解这种奇异性。

Method: 首先考虑Nash blow-up的正规化（normalization of the Nash blow-up），将其与Bloch引入的incidence variety等同。该簇通常仍非光滑，但它是环面（torus）中一个光滑子簇的闭包。随后，利用Tevelev的工作，对该光滑子簇构造一个光滑的tropical紧化（tropical compactification），并建立从该紧化到正规化Nash blow-up的态射（morphism），整个构造由Ardila、Denham和Huh提出的双置换多面体拟阵（bipermutohedral matroid）组合学描述。

Result: 证明了配置超曲面的正规化Nash blow-up在正特征（positive characteristic）下具有强F-正则奇点（strongly $F$-regular singularities），通过认证其双射影锥（biprojective cone）的F-有理性（$F$-rationality）推导得出；进而推断在复数域上该正规化Nash blow-up具有有理奇点（rational singularities）。

Conclusion: 该工作为任意不可约配置超曲面提供了一种显式的奇点消解方案，并将组合结构与代数几何中的奇点性质建立了联系，为Feynman积分在简化设定下的进一步评估奠定了基础。

Abstract: Configuration polynomials generalize the Kirchhoff polynomial of a graph, as well as the Symanzik polynomials that appear in the denominators of Feynman integrands. The configuration hypersurfaces cut out by such polynomials are typically highly singular, which poses a challenge for the evaluation of Feynman integrals even in simplified settings.
  In this paper, we provide a two-step recipe for a resolution of singularities of any irreducible configuration hypersurface. We first consider the normalization of the Nash blow-up, which we identify with an incidence variety introduced by Bloch. This variety is typically still not smooth, but it is the closure of a smooth subvariety of a torus. The latter then a smooth, tropical compactification, using work of Tevelev. We construct explicitly such a compactification and a morphism to the normalized Nash blow-up for every configuration, described in terms of bipermutohedral matroid combinatorics introduced by Ardila, Denham and Huh.
  Along the way, we find that the normalized Nash blow-up of the configuration hypersurface has strongly $F$-regular singularities in positive characteristic. We deduce this by certifying $F$-rationality of its biprojective cone, and infer from it that the normalized Nash blow-up has rational singularities over the complex numbers.

</details>
